pratyakpuṣpī pītatailodakīryā śvetāyugmaṃ tāpasānāṃ ca vṛkṣaḥ
ayam arkādiko vargaḥ kaphamedoviṣāpahaḥ
kṛmikuṣṭhapraśamano viśeṣād vraṇaśodhanaḥ
surasayugaphaṇijjaṃ kālamālā viḍaṅgaṃ kharabusavṛṣakarṇīkaṭphalaṃ kāsamardaḥ
kṣavakasarasībhārgīkārmukāḥ kākamācī kulahalaviṣamuṣṭī bhūstṛṇo bhūtakeśī
surasādir gaṇaḥ śleṣmamedaḥkṛminiṣūdanaḥ
pratiśyāyāruciśvāsakāsaghno vraṇaśodhanaḥ
gulmamehāśmarīpāṇḍumedo'rśaḥkaphaśukrajit
vatsakamūrvābhārgīkaṭukā marīcaṃ ghuṇapriyā ca gaṇḍīram
elā pāṭhājājī kaṭvaṅgaphalājamodasiddhārthavacāḥ
jīrakahiṅguviḍaṅgaṃ paśugandhā pañcakolakaṃ hanti
calakaphamedaḥpīnasagulmajvaraśūladurnāmnaḥ
haridrādvayayaṣṭyāhvakalaśīkuṭajodbhavāḥ
vacāharidrādigaṇāv āmātīsāranāśanau
medaḥkaphāḍhyapavanastanyadoṣanibarhaṇau
priyaṅgupuṣpāñjanayugmapadmāḥ padmād rajo yojanavally anantā
mānadrumo mocarasaḥ samaṅgā puṃnāgaśītaṃ madanīyahetuḥ
ambaṣṭhā madhukaṃ namaskarī nandīvṛkṣapalāśakacchurāḥ
lodhraṃ dhātakībilvapeśike kaṭvaṅgaḥ kamalodbhavaṃ rajaḥ
gaṇau priyaṅgvambaṣṭhādī pakvātīsāranāśanau
saṃdhānīyau hitau pitte vraṇānām api ropaṇau
mustāvacāgnidviniśādvitiktābhallātapāṭhātriphalāviṣākhyāḥ
kuṣṭhaṃ truṭī haimavatī ca yonistanyāmayaghnā malapācanāś ca
nyagrodhapippalasadāphalalodhrayugmaṃ jambūdvayārjunakapītanasomavalkāḥ
plakṣāmravañjulapiyālapalāśanandīkolīkadambaviralāmadhukaṃ madhūkam
nyagrodhādir gaṇo vraṇyaḥ saṃgrāhī bhagnasādhanaḥ
medaḥpittāsratṛḍdāhayoniroganibarhaṇaḥ
elāyugmaturuṣkakuṣṭhaphalinīmāṃsījaladhyāmakaṃ spṛkkācorakacocapattratagarasthauṇeyajātīrasāḥ
śuktir vyāghranakho 'marāhvam aguruḥ śrīvāsakaḥ kuṅkumaṃ caṇḍāgugguludevadhūpakhapurāḥ puṃnāganāgāhvayam
elādiko vātakaphau viṣaṃ ca viniyacchati
varṇaprasādanaḥ kaṇḍūpiṭikākoṭhanāśanaḥ
śyāmādantīdravantīkramukakuṭaraṇāśaṅkhinīcarmasāhvā
bastāntrī vyādhighāto bahalabahurasas tīkṣṇavṛkṣāt phalāni
śyāmādyo hanti gulmaṃ viṣamarucikaphau hṛdrujaṃ mūtrakṛcchram
trayastriṃśad iti proktā vargās teṣu tv alābhataḥ
yuñjyāt tadvidham anyac ca dravyaṃ jahyād ayaugikam
ete vargā doṣadūṣyādy apekṣya kalkakvāthasnehalehādiyuktāḥ
pāne nasye 'nvāsane 'ntar bahir vā lepābhyaṅgair ghnanti rogān sukṛcchrān
athātaḥ snehavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
guruśītasarasnigdhamandasūkṣmamṛdudravam
auṣadhaṃ snehanaṃ prāyo viparītaṃ virūkṣaṇam
sarpir majjā vasā tailaṃ sneheṣu pravaraṃ matam
tatrāpi cottamaṃ sarpiḥ saṃskārasyānuvartanāt
mādhuryād avidāhitvājjanmādyeva ca śīlanāt
pittaghnās te yathāpūrvam itaraghnā yathottaram
ghṛtāt tailaṃ guru vasā tailān majjā tato 'pi ca
dvābhyāṃ tribhiś caturbhis tair yamakas trivṛto mahān
svedyasaṃśodhyamadyastrīvyāyāmāsaktacintakāḥ
bālābalakṛśā rūkṣāḥ kṣīṇāsraretasaḥ
vātārtasyandatimiradāruṇapratibodhinaḥ
snehyāḥ na tv atimandāgnitīkṣṇāgnisthūladurbalāḥ
ūrustambhātisārāmagalarogagarodaraiḥ
mūrcchāchardyaruciśleṣmatṛṣṇāmadyaiś ca pīḍitāḥ
apaprasūtā yukte ca nasye bastau virecane
tatra dhīsmṛtimedhādikāṅkṣiṇāṃ śasyate ghṛtam
granthināḍīkṛmiśleṣmamedomārutarogiṣu
tailaṃ lāghavadārḍhyārthikrūrakoṣṭheṣu dehiṣu
vātātapādhvabhārastrīvyāyāmakṣīṇadhātuṣu
rūkṣakleśakṣamātyagnivātāvṛtapatheṣu ca
śeṣau vasā tu sandhyasthimarmakoṣṭharujāsu ca
tathā dagdhāhatabhraṣṭayonikarṇaśiroruji
tailaṃ prāvṛṣi varṣānte sarpir anyau tu mādhave
ṛtau sādhāraṇe snehaḥ śasto 'hni vimale ravau
tailaṃ tvarāyāṃ śīte 'pi gharme 'pi ca ghṛtaṃ niśi
niśy eva pitte pavane saṃsarge pittavaty api
niśyanyathā vātakaphād rogāḥ syuḥ pittato divā
yuktyāvacārayet snehaṃ bhakṣyādyannena bastibhiḥ
nasyābhyañjanagaṇḍūṣamūrdhakarṇākṣitarpaṇaiḥ
rasabhedaikakatvābhyāṃ catuḥṣaṣṭirvicāraṇāḥ
snehasyānyābhibhūtatvādalpatvācca kramātsmṛtāḥ
yathoktahetvabhāvācca nācchapeyo vicāraṇā
snehasya kalpaḥ sa śreṣṭhaḥ snehakarmāśusādhanāt
dvābhyāṃ caturbhiraṣṭābhiryāmairjīryanti yāḥ kramāt
hrasvamadhyottamā mātrāstāstābhyaśca hrasīyasīm
kalpayedvīkṣya doṣādīnprāgeva tu hrasīyasīm
hyastane jīrṇa evānne sneho'cchaḥ śuddhaye bahuḥ
śamanaḥ kṣudvato'nanno madhyamātraśca śasyate
bṛṃhaṇo rasamadyādyaiḥ sabhakto'lpaḥ hitaḥ sa ca
bālavṛddhapipāsārtasnehadviṇmadyaśīliṣu
strīsnehanityamandāgnisukhitakleśabhīruṣu
mṛdukoṣṭhālpadoṣeṣu kāle coṣṇe kṛśeṣu ca
prāṅmadhyottarabhakto'sāvadhomadhyordhvadehajān
vyādhīñjayed balaṃ kuryādaṅgānāṃ ca yathākramam
svedas tāpopanāhoṣmadravabhedāc caturvidhaḥ
tāpo 'gnitaptavasanaphālahastatalādibhiḥ
upanāho vacākiṇvaśatāhvādevadārubhiḥ
dhānyaiḥ samastair gandhaiś ca rāsnairaṇḍajaṭāmiṣaiḥ
udriktalavaṇaiḥ snehacukratakrapayaḥplutaiḥ
kevale pavane śleṣmasaṃsṛṣṭe surasādibhiḥ
pittena padmakādyais tu śālvaṇākhyaiḥ punaḥ punaḥ
snigdhoṣṇavīryair mṛdubhiś carmapaṭṭair apūtibhiḥ
alābhe vātajitpattrakauśeyāvikaśāṭakaiḥ
baddhaṃ rātrau divā muñcen muñced rātrau divākṛtam
ūṣmā tūtkārikāloṣṭakapālopalapāṃsubhiḥ
pattrabhaṅgena dhānyena karīṣasikatātuṣaiḥ
anekopāyasaṃtaptaiḥ prayojyo deśakālataḥ
śigruvāraṇakairaṇḍakarañjasurasārjakāt
śirīṣavāsāvaṃśārkamālatīdīrghavṛntataḥ
pattrabhaṅgair vacādyaiś ca māṃsaiś cānūpavārijaiḥ
daśamūlena ca pṛthak sahitair vā yathāmalam
snehavadbhiḥ surāśuktavārikṣīrādisādhitaiḥ
kumbhīr galantīr nāḍīr vā pūrayitvā rujārditam
vāsasācchāditaṃ gātraṃ snigdhaṃ siñced yathāsukham
tair eva vā dravaiḥ pūrṇaṃ kuṇḍaṃ sarvāṅgage 'nile
avagāhyāturas tiṣṭhed arśaḥkṛcchrādirukṣu ca
nivāte 'ntarbahiḥsnigdho jīrṇānnaḥ svedam ācaret
vyādhivyādhitadeśartuvaśān madhyavarāvaram
kaphārto rūkṣaṇaṃ rūkṣo rūkṣaḥ snigdhaṃ kaphānile
āmāśayagate vāyau kaphe pakvāśayāśrite
rūkṣapūrvaṃ tathā snehapūrvaṃ sthānānurodhataḥ
alpaṃ vaṅkṣaṇayoḥ svalpaṃ dṛṅmuṣkahṛdaye na vā
śītaśūlakṣaye svinno jāte 'ṅgānāṃ ca mārdave
syāc chanair mṛditaḥ snātas tataḥ snehavidhiṃ bhajet
pittāsrakopatṛṇmūrchāsvarāṅgasadanabhramāḥ
saṃdhipīḍā jvaraḥ śyāvaraktamaṇḍaladarśanam
svedātiyogāc chardiś ca tatra stambhanam auṣadham
viṣakṣārāgnyatīsāracchardimohātureṣu ca
svedanaṃ guru tīkṣṇoṣṇaṃ prāyaḥ stambhanam anyathā
dravasthirasarasnigdharūkṣasūkṣmaṃ ca bheṣajam
svedanaṃ stambhanaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ rūkṣasūkṣmasaradravam
prāyas tiktaṃ kaṣāyaṃ ca madhuraṃ ca samāsataḥ
stambhitaḥ syād bale labdhe yathoktāmayasaṃkṣayāt
stambhatvaksnāyusaṃkocakampahṛdvāgghanugrahaiḥ
pādauṣṭhatvakkaraiḥ śyāvair atistambhitam ādiśet
na svedayed atisthūlarūkṣadurbalamūrchitān
stambhanīyakṣatakṣīṇakṣāmamadyavikāriṇaḥ
timirodaravīsarpakuṣṭhaśoṣāḍhyarogiṇaḥ
pītadugdhadadhisnehamadhūn kṛtavirecanān
bhraṣṭadagdhagudaglānikrodhaśokabhayārditān
kṣuttṛṣṇākāmalāpāṇḍumehinaḥ pittapīḍitān
garbhiṇīṃ puṣpitāṃ sūtāṃ mṛdu cātyayike gade
svarabhedānilavyādhiśleṣmāmastambhagaurave
aṅgamardakaṭīpārśvapṛṣṭhakukṣihanugrahe
mahattve muṣkayoḥ khalyām āyāme vātakaṇṭake
mūtrakṛcchrārbudagranthiśukrāghātāḍhyamārute
svedaṃ yathāyathaṃ kuryāt tadauṣadhavibhāgataḥ
svedo hitas tv anāgneyo vāte medaḥkaphāvṛte
nivātaṃ gṛham āyāso guruprāvaraṇaṃ bhayam
snehaklinnāḥ koṣṭhagā dhātugā vā srotolīnā ye ca śākhāsthisaṃsthāḥ
doṣāḥ svedais te dravīkṛtya koṣṭhaṃ nītāḥ samyak śuddhibhir nirhriyante
kaphe vidadhyād vamanaṃ saṃyoge vā kapholbaṇe
tadvad virecanaṃ pitte viśeṣeṇa tu vāmayet
navajvarātisārādhaḥpittāsṛgrājayakṣmiṇaḥ
kuṣṭhamehāpacīgranthiślīpadonmādakāsinaḥ
śvāsahṛllāsavīsarpastanyadoṣordhvarogiṇaḥ
avāmyā garbhiṇī rūkṣaḥ kṣudhito nityaduḥkhitaḥ
bālavṛddhakṛśasthūlahṛdrogikṣatadurbalāḥ
prasaktavamathuplīhatimirakṛmikoṣṭhinaḥ
ūrdhvapravṛttavāyvasradattavastihatasvarāḥ
mūtrāghāty udarī gulmī durvamo 'tyagnir arśasaḥ
udāvartabhramāṣṭhīlāpārśvarugvātarogiṇaḥ
ṛte viṣagarājīrṇaviruddhābhyavahārataḥ
prasaktavamathoḥ pūrve prāyeṇāmajvaro 'pi ca
dhūmāntaiḥ karmabhir varjyāḥ sarvair eva tv ajīrṇinaḥ
virekasādhyā gulmārśovisphoṭavyaṅgakāmalāḥ
jīrṇajvarodaragaracchardiplīhahalīmakāḥ
vidradhis timiraṃ kācaḥ syandaḥ pakvāśayavyathā
yoniśukrāśrayā rogāḥ koṣṭhagāḥ kṛmayo vraṇāḥ
vātāsram ūrdhvagaṃ raktaṃ mūtrāghātaḥ śakṛdgrahaḥ
vāmyaś ca kuṣṭhamehādyā na tu recyā navajvarī
alpāgnyadhogapittāsrakṣatapāyvatisāriṇaḥ
saśalyāsthāpitakrūrakoṣṭhātisnigdhaśoṣiṇaḥ
atha sādhāraṇe kāle snigdhasvinnaṃ yathāvidhi
śvovamyam utkliṣṭakaphaṃ matsyamāṣatilādibhiḥ
niśāṃ suptaṃ sujīrṇānnaṃ pūrvāhṇe kṛtamaṅgalam
nirannam īṣatsnigdhaṃ vā peyayā pītasarpiṣam
vṛddhabālābalaklībabhīrūn rogānurodhataḥ
ākaṇṭhaṃ pāyitān madyaṃ kṣīram ikṣurasaṃ rasam
yathāvikāravihitāṃ madhusaindhavasaṃyutām
koṣṭhaṃ vibhajya bhaiṣajyamātrāṃ mantrābhimantritām
ṛṣayaḥ sauṣadhigrāmā bhūtasaṃghāś ca pāntu vaḥ
rasāyanam ivarṣīṇām amarāṇām ivāmṛtam
sudhevottamanāgānāṃ bhaiṣajyam idam astu te
prāṅmukhaṃ pāyayet pīto muhūrtam anupālayet
tanmanā jātahṛllāsaprasekaś chardayet tataḥ
aṅgulībhyām anāyasto nālena mṛdunāthavā
galatālv arujan vegān apravṛttān pravartayan
pravartayan pravṛttāṃś ca jānutulyāsane sthitaḥ
ubhe pārśve lalāṭaṃ ca vamataś cāsya dhārayet
prapīḍayet tathā nābhiṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ ca pratilomataḥ
kaphe tīkṣṇoṣṇakaṭukaiḥ pitte svāduhimair iti
vamet snigdhāmlalavaṇaiḥ saṃsṛṣṭe marutā kaphe
pittasya darśanaṃ yāvac chedo vā śleṣmaṇo bhavet
hīnavegaḥ kaṇādhātrīsiddhārthalavaṇodakaiḥ
vamet punaḥ punas tatra vegānām apravartanam
pravṛttiḥ savibandhā vā kevalasyauṣadhasya vā
ayogas tena niṣṭhīvakaṇḍūkoṭhajvarādayaḥ
nirvibandhaṃ pravartante kaphapittānilāḥ kramāt
samyagyoge 'tiyoge tu phenacandrakaraktavat
vamitaṃ kṣāmatā dāhaḥ kaṇṭhaśoṣas tamo bhramaḥ
ghorā vāyvāmayā mṛtyur jīvaśoṇitanirgamāt
samyagyogena vamitaṃ kṣaṇam āśvāsya pāyayet
dhūmatrayasyānyatamaṃ snehācāram athādiśet
tataḥ sāyaṃ prabhāte vā kṣudvān snātaḥ sukhāmbunā
bhuñjāno raktaśālyannaṃ bhajet peyādikaṃ kramam
peyāṃ vilepīm akṛtaṃ kṛtaṃ ca yūṣaṃ rasaṃ trīn ubhayaṃ tathaikam
krameṇa seveta naro 'nnakālān pradhānamadhyāvaraśuddhiśuddhaḥ
yathāṇur agnis tṛṇagomayādyaiḥ saṃdhukṣyamāṇo bhavati krameṇa
mahān sthiraḥ sarvapacas tathaiva śuddhasya peyādibhir antarāgniḥ
jaghanyamadhyapravare tu vegāś catvāra iṣṭā vamane ṣaḍ aṣṭau
daśaiva te dvitriguṇā vireke prasthas tathā syād dvicaturguṇaś ca
pittāvasānaṃ vamanaṃ virekād ardhaṃ kaphāntaṃ ca virekam āhuḥ
dvitrān saviṭkān apanīya vegān meyaṃ vireke vamane tu pītam
athainaṃ vāmitaṃ bhūyaḥ snehasvedopapāditam
śleṣmakāle gate jñātvā koṣṭhaṃ samyag virecayet
bahupitto mṛduḥ koṣṭhaḥ kṣīreṇāpi viricyate
prabhūtamārutaḥ krūraḥ kṛcchrāc chyāmādikair api
kaṣāyamadhuraiḥ pitte virekaḥ kaṭukaiḥ kaphe
snigdhoṣṇalavaṇair vāyāv apravṛttau tu pāyayet
uṣṇāmbu svedayed asya pāṇitāpena codaram
utthāne 'lpe dine tasmin bhuktvānyedyuḥ punaḥ pibet
adṛḍhasnehakoṣṭhas tu pibed ūrdhvaṃ daśāhataḥ
bhūyo 'py upaskṛtatanuḥ snehasvedair virecanam
yaugikaṃ samyag ālocya smaran pūrvam atikramam
hṛtkukṣyaśuddhir arucir utkleśaḥ śleṣmapittayoḥ
kaṇḍūvidāhaḥ piṭikāḥ pīnaso vātaviḍgrahaḥ
ayogalakṣaṇaṃ yogo vaiparītye yathoditāt
viṭpittakaphavāteṣu niḥsṛteṣu kramāt sravet
niḥśleṣmapittam udakaṃ śvetaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ salohitam
māṃsadhāvanatulyaṃ vā medaḥkhaṇḍābham eva vā
gudaniḥsaraṇaṃ tṛṣṇā bhramo netrapraveśanam
bhavanty ativiriktasya tathātivamanāmayāḥ
samyagviriktam enaṃ ca vamanoktena yojayet
dhūmavarjyena vidhinā tato vamitavān iva
krameṇānnāni bhuñjāno bhajet prakṛtibhojanam
mandavahnim asaṃśuddham akṣāmaṃ doṣadurbalam
adṛṣṭajīrṇaliṅgaṃ ca laṅghayet pītabheṣajam
snehasvedauṣadhotkleśasaṅgair iti na bādhyate
saṃśodhanāsravisrāvasnehayojanalaṅghanaiḥ
yāty agnir mandatāṃ tasmāt kramaṃ peyādim ācaret
srutālpapittaśleṣmāṇaṃ madyapaṃ vātapaittikam
peyāṃ na pāyayet teṣāṃ tarpaṇādikramo hitaḥ
apakvaṃ vamanaṃ doṣān pacyamānaṃ virecanam
nirhared vamanasyātaḥ pākaṃ na pratipālayet
durbalo bahudoṣaś ca doṣapākena yaḥ svayam
viricyate bhedanīyair bhojyais tam upapādayet
durbalaḥ śodhitaḥ pūrvam alpadoṣaḥ kṛśo naraḥ
aparijñātakoṣṭhaś ca piben mṛdv alpam auṣadham
varaṃ tad asakṛtpītam anyathā saṃśayāvaham
hared bahūṃś calān doṣān alpān alpān punaḥ punaḥ
durbalasya mṛdudravyair alpān saṃśamayet tu tān
kleśayanti ciraṃ te hi hanyur vainam anirhṛtāḥ
mandāgniṃ krūrakoṣṭhaṃ ca sakṣāralavaṇair ghṛtaiḥ
saṃdhukṣitāgniṃ vijitakaphavātaṃ ca śodhayet
rūkṣabahvanilakrūrakoṣṭhavyāyāmaśīlinām
dīptāgnīnāṃ ca bhaiṣajyam avirecyaiva jīryati
tebhyo vastiṃ purā dadyāt tataḥ snigdhaṃ virecanam
śakṛn nirhṛtya vā kiṃcit tīkṣṇābhiḥ phalavartibhiḥ
pravṛttaṃ hi malaṃ snigdho vireko nirharet sukham
viṣābhighātapiṭikākuṣṭhaśophavisarpiṇaḥ
kāmalāpāṇḍumehārtān nātisnigdhān viśodhayet
sarvān snehavirekaiś ca rūkṣais tu snehabhāvitān
karmaṇāṃ vamanādīnāṃ punar apy antare 'ntare
snehasvedau prayuñjīta sneham ante balāya ca
malo hi dehād utkleśya hriyate vāsaso yathā
snehasvedais tathotkliṣṭaḥ śodhyate śodhanair malaḥ
snehasvedāv anabhyasya kuryāt saṃśodhanaṃ tu yaḥ
buddhiprasādaṃ balam indriyāṇāṃ dhātusthiratvaṃ jvalanasya dīptim
cirāc ca pākaṃ vayasaḥ karoti saṃśodhanaṃ samyagupāsyamānam
ūrdhvajatruvikāreṣu viśeṣān nasyam iṣyate
nāsā hi śiraso dvāraṃ tena tad vyāpya hanti tān
virecanaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ ca śamanaṃ ca tridhāpi tat
virecanaṃ śiraḥśūlajāḍyasyandagalāmaye
śophagaṇḍakṛmigranthikuṣṭhāpasmārapīnase
bṛṃhaṇaṃ vātaje śūle sūryāvarte svarakṣaye
nāsāsyaśoṣe vāksaṅge kṛcchrabodhe 'vabāhuke
śamanaṃ nīlikāvyaṅgakeśadoṣākṣirājiṣu
yathāsvaṃ yaugikaiḥ snehair yathāsvaṃ ca prasādhitaiḥ
kalkakvāthādibhiś cādyaṃ madhupaṭvāsavair api
bṛṃhaṇaṃ dhanvamāṃsottharasāsṛkkhapurair api
śamanaṃ yojayet pūrvaiḥ kṣīreṇa salilena vā
marśaś ca pratimarśaś ca dvidhā sneho 'tra mātrayā
kalkādyair avapīḍas tu sa tīkṣṇair mūrdharecanaḥ
dhmānaṃ virecanaścūrṇo yuñjyāt taṃ mukhavāyunā
ṣaḍaṅguladvimukhayā nāḍyā bheṣajagarbhayā
sa hi bhūritaraṃ doṣaṃ cūrṇatvād apakarṣati
pradeśinyaṅgulīparvadvayān magnasamuddhṛtāt
yāvat patatyasau bindur daśāṣṭau ṣaṭ krameṇa te
marśasyotkṛṣṭamadhyonā mātrās tā eva ca kramāt
bindudvayonāḥ kalkāder yojayen na tu nāvanam
toyamadyagarasnehapītānāṃ pātum icchatām
navapīnasavegārtasūtikāśvāsakāsinām
śuddhānāṃ dattavastīnāṃ tathānārtavadurdine
anyatrātyayikād vyādher atha nasyaṃ prayojayet
prātaḥ śleṣmaṇi madhyāhne pitte sāyaṃ niśoścale
svasthavṛtte tu pūrvāhṇe śaratkālavasantayoḥ
śīte madhyaṃdine grīṣme sāyaṃ varṣāsu sātape
vātābhibhūte śirasi hidhmāyām apatānake
manyāstambhe svarabhraṃśe sāyaṃ prātar dine dine
ekāhāntaram anyatra saptāhaṃ ca tad ācaret
snigdhasvinnottamāṅgasya prākkṛtāvaśyakasya ca
nivātaśayanasthasya jatrūrdhvaṃ svedayet punaḥ
athottānarjudehasya pāṇipāde prasārite
kiṃcidunnatapādasya kiṃcinmūrdhani nāmite
nāsāpuṭaṃ pidhāyaikaṃ paryāyeṇa niṣecayet
uṣṇāmbutaptaṃ bhaiṣajyaṃ praṇāḍyā picunāthavā
datte pādatalaskandhahastakarṇādi mardayet
śanair ucchidya niṣṭhīvet pārśvayor ubhayos tataḥ
ā bheṣajakṣayād evaṃ dvis trir vā nasyam ācaret
mūrchāyāṃ śītatoyena siñcet pariharan śiraḥ
snehaṃ virecanasyānte dadyād doṣādyapekṣayā
nasyānte vākśataṃ tiṣṭhed uttāno dhārayet tataḥ
dhūmaṃ pītvā kavoṣṇāmbukavaḍān kaṇṭhaśuddhaye
samyaksnigdhe sukhocchvāsasvapnabodhākṣapāṭavam
rūkṣe 'kṣistabdhatā śoṣo nāsāsye mūrdhaśūnyatā
snigdhe 'ti kaṇḍūgurutāprasekārucipīnasāḥ
suvirikte 'kṣilaghutāvaktrasvaraviśuddhayaḥ
durvirikte gadodrekaḥ kṣāmatātivirecite
pratimarśaḥ kṣatakṣāmabālavṛddhasukhātmasu
prayojyo 'kālavarṣe 'pi na tviṣṭo duṣṭapīnase
madyapīte 'balaśrotre kṛmidūṣitamūrdhani
utkṛṣṭotkliṣṭadoṣe ca hīnamātratayā hi saḥ
śiro'bhyañjanagaṇḍūṣaprasrāvāñjanavarcasām
dantakāṣṭhasya hāsasya yojyo 'nte 'sau dvibindukaḥ
pañcasu srotasāṃ śuddhiḥ klamanāśas triṣu kramāt
dṛgbalaṃ pañcasu tato dantadārḍhyaṃ marucchamaḥ
na nasyam ūnasaptābde nātītāśītivatsare
na conāṣṭādaśe dhūmaḥ kavaḍo nonapañcame
na śuddhir ūnadaśame na cātikrāntasaptatau
ājanmamaraṇaṃ śastaḥ pratimarśas tu vastivat
marśavacca guṇān kuryāt sa hi nityopasevanāt
na cātra yantraṇā nāpi vyāpadbhyo marśavad bhayam
tailam eva ca nasyārthe nityābhyāsena śasyate
śirasaḥ śleṣmadhāmatvāt snehāḥ svasthasya netare
āśukṛccirakāritvaṃ guṇotkarṣāpakṛṣṭatā
marśe ca pratimarśe ca viśeṣo na bhaved yadi
ko marśaṃ saparīhāraṃ sāpadaṃ ca bhajet tataḥ
acchapānavicārākhyau kuṭīvātātapasthitī
anvāsamātrāvastī ca tadvad eva vinirdiśet
paṭolamudgavārtākahrasvamūlakajāṅgalaiḥ
rasaiḥ śāliyavān adyān nasyakarmaṇi ṣaḍvidhe
jīvantījaladevadārujaladatvaksevyagopīhimam
dārvītvaṅmadhukaplavāguruvarīpuṇḍrāhvabilvotpalam
dhāvanyau surabhiṃ sthire kṛmiharaṃ pattraṃ truṭīṃ reṇukām
kiñjalkaṃ kamalād balāṃ śataguṇe divye 'mbhasi kvāthayet
tailād rasaṃ daśaguṇaṃ pariśeṣya tena tailaṃ paceta salilena daśaiva vārān
pāke kṣipecca daśame samam ājadugdhaṃ nasyaṃ mahāguṇam uśantyaṇutailam etat
ghanonnataprasannatvakskandhagrīvāsyavakṣasaḥ
dṛḍhendriyāstapalitā bhaveyur nasyaśīlinaḥ
jatrūrdhvakaphavātotthavikārāṇām ajanmane
ucchedāya ca jātānāṃ pibed dhūmaṃ sadātmavān
snigdho madhyaḥ sa tīkṣṇaśca vāte vātakaphe kaphe
yojyo na raktapittārtiviriktodaramehiṣu
timirordhvānilādhmānarohiṇīdattavastiṣu
matsyamadyadadhikṣīrakṣaudrasnehaviṣāśiṣu
śirasyabhihate pāṇḍuroge jāgarite niśi
raktapittāndhyabādhiryatṛṇmūrchāmadamohakṛt
dhūmo 'kāle 'tipīto vā tatra śīto vidhir hitaḥ
kṣutajṛmbhitaviṇmūtrastrīsevāśastrakarmaṇām
hāsasya dantakāṣṭhasya dhūmam ante piben mṛdum
kāleṣveṣu niśāhāranāvanānte ca madhyamam
nidrānasyāñjanasnānaccharditānte virecanam
vastinetrasamadravyaṃ trikośaṃ kārayed ṛju
mūlāgre 'ṅguṣṭhakolāsthipraveśaṃ dhūmanetrakam
tīkṣṇasnehanamadhyeṣu trīṇi catvāri pañca ca
aṅgulānāṃ kramāt pātuḥ pramāṇenāṣṭakāni tat
ṛjūpaviṣṭas taccetā vivṛtāsyas triparyayam
pidhāya chidram ekaikaṃ dhūmaṃ nāsikayā pibet
prāk piben nāsayotkliṣṭe doṣe ghrāṇaśirogate
utkleśanārthaṃ vaktreṇa viparītaṃ tu kaṇṭhage
mukhenaivodvamed dhūmaṃ nāsayā dṛgvighātakṛt
ākṣepamokṣaiḥ pātavyo dhūmas tu tris tribhis tribhiḥ
ahnaḥ pibet sakṛt snigdhaṃ dvir madhyaṃ śodhanaṃ param
triścatur vā mṛdau tatra dravyāṇyaguru guggulu
mustasthauṇeyaśaileyanaladośīravālakam
varāṅgakauntīmadhukabilvamajjailavālukam
śrīveṣṭakaṃ sarjaraso dhyāmakaṃ madanaṃ plavam
śallakī kuṅkumaṃ māṣā yavāḥ kundurukas tilāḥ
snehaḥ phalānāṃ sārāṇāṃ medo majjā vasā ghṛtam
śamane śallakī lākṣā pṛthvīkā kamalotpalam
nyagrodhodumbarāśvatthaplakṣalodhratvacaḥ sitā
yaṣṭīmadhu suvarṇatvak padmakaṃ raktayaṣṭikā
gandhāś cākuṣṭhatagarās tīkṣṇe jyotiṣmatī niśā
daśamūlamanohvālaṃ lākṣā śvetā phalatrayam
gandhadravyāṇi tīkṣṇāni gaṇo mūrdhavirecanaḥ
jale sthitām ahorātram iṣīkāṃ dvādaśāṅgulām
piṣṭair dhūmauṣadhair evaṃ pañcakṛtvaḥ pralepayet
vartir aṅguṣṭhakasthūlā yavamadhyā yathā bhavet
chāyāśuṣkāṃ vigarbhāṃ tāṃ snehābhyaktāṃ yathāyatham
dhūmanetrārpitāṃ pātum agnipluṣṭāṃ prayojayet
śarāvasampuṭacchidre nāḍīṃ nyasya daśāṅgulām
kāsaḥ śvāsaḥ pīnaso visvaratvaṃ pūtir gandhaḥ pāṇḍutā keśadoṣaḥ
karṇāsyākṣisrāvakaṇḍvartijāḍyaṃ tandrā hidhmā dhūmapaṃ na spṛśanti
catuḥprakāro gaṇḍūṣaḥ snigdhaḥ śamanaśodhanau
ropaṇaśca trayas tatra triṣu yojyāścalādiṣu
antyo vraṇaghnaḥ snigdho 'tra svādvamlapaṭusādhitaiḥ
snehaiḥ saṃśamanas tiktakaṣāyamadhurauṣadhaiḥ
śodhanas tiktakaṭvamlapaṭūṣṇai ropaṇaḥ punaḥ
kaṣāyatiktakais tatra snehaḥ kṣīraṃ madhūdakam
śuktaṃ madyaṃ raso mūtraṃ dhānyāmlaṃ ca yathāyatham
kalkair yuktaṃ vipakvaṃ vā yathāsparśaṃ prayojayet
dantaharṣe dantacāle mukharoge ca vātike
sukhoṣṇam athavā śītaṃ tilakalkodakaṃ hitam
gaṇḍūṣadhāraṇe nityaṃ tailaṃ māṃsaraso 'thavā
ūṣādāhānvite pāke kṣate cāgantusambhave
viṣe kṣārāgnidagdhe ca sarpir dhāryaṃ payo 'thavā
vaiśadyaṃ janayatyāśu saṃdadhāti mukhe vraṇān
dāhatṛṣṇāpraśamanaṃ madhugaṇḍūṣadhāraṇam
dhānyāmlam āsyavairasyamaladaurgandhyanāśanam
tad evālavaṇaṃ śītaṃ mukhaśoṣaharaṃ param
āśu kṣārāmbugaṇḍūṣo bhinatti śleṣmaṇaś cayam
sukhoṣṇodakagaṇḍūṣair jāyate vaktralāghavam
nivāte sātape svinnamṛditaskandhakandharaḥ
gaṇḍūṣam apiban kiṃcidunnatāsyo vidhārayet
kaphapūrṇāsyatā yāvat sravadghrāṇākṣatāthavā
manyāśiraḥkarṇamukhākṣirogāḥ prasekakaṇṭhāmayavaktraśoṣāḥ
hṛllāsatandrārucipīnasāśca sādhyā viśeṣāt kavaḍagraheṇa
kalko rasakriyā cūrṇas trividhaṃ pratisāraṇam
yuñjyāt tat kapharogeṣu gaṇḍūṣavihitauṣadhaiḥ
mukhālepas tridhā doṣaviṣahā varṇakṛcca saḥ
uṣṇo vātakaphe śastaḥ śeṣeṣvatyarthaśītalaḥ
tripramāṇaś caturbhāgatribhāgārdhāṅgulonnatiḥ
aśuṣkasya sthitis tasya śuṣko dūṣayati chavim
tam ārdrayitvāpanayet tadante 'bhyaṅgam ācaret
vivarjayed divāsvapnabhāṣyāgnyātapaśukkrudhaḥ
na yojyaḥ pīnase 'jīrṇe dattanasye hanugrahe
arocake jāgarite sa tu hanti suyojitaḥ
akālapalitavyaṅgavalītimiranīlikāḥ
kolamajjā vṛṣān mūlaṃ śābaraṃ gaurasarṣapāḥ
siṃhīmūlaṃ tilāḥ kṛṣṇā dārvītvaṅ nistuṣā yavāḥ
darbhamūlahimośīraśirīṣamiśitaṇḍulāḥ
kumudotpalakalhāradūrvāmadhukacandanam
kālīyakatilośīramāṃsītagarapadmakam
ityardhārdhoditā lepā hemantādiṣu ṣaṭ smṛtāḥ
mukhālepanaśīlānāṃ dṛḍhaṃ bhavati darśanam
vadanaṃ cāparimlānaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ tāmarasopamam
abhyaṅgasekapicavo vastiś ceti caturvidham
mūrdhatailaṃ bahuguṇaṃ tad vidyād uttarottaram
tatrābhyaṅgaḥ prayoktavyo raukṣyakaṇḍūmalādiṣu
arūṃṣikāśirastodadāhapākavraṇeṣu tu
pariṣekaḥ picuḥ keśaśātasphuṭanadhūpane
netrastambhe ca vastis tu prasuptyarditajāgare
nāsāsyaśoṣe timire śiroroge ca dāruṇe
vidhis tasya niṣaṇṇasya pīṭhe jānusame mṛdau
śuddhāktasvinnadehasya dinānte gavyamāhiṣam
dvādaśāṅgulavistīrṇaṃ carmapaṭṭaṃ śiraḥsamam
ā karṇabandhanasthānaṃ lalāṭe vastraveṣṭite
cailaveṇikayā baddhvā māṣakalkena lepayet
tato yathāvyādhi śṛtaṃ snehaṃ koṣṇaṃ niṣecayet
ūrdhvaṃ keśabhuvo yāvad aṅgulaṃ dhārayecca tam
ā vaktranāsikotkledād daśāṣṭau ṣaṭ calādiṣu
mātrāsahasrāṇyaruje tvekaṃ skandhādi mardayet
muktasnehasya paramaṃ saptāhaṃ tasya sevanam
dhārayet pūraṇaṃ karṇe karṇamūlaṃ vimardayan
rujaḥ syān mārdavaṃ yāvan mātrāśatam avedane
yāvat paryeti hastāgraṃ dakṣiṇaṃ jānumaṇḍalam
nimeṣonmeṣakālena samaṃ mātrā tu sā smṛtā
kacasadanasitatvapiñjaratvaṃ pariphuṭanaṃ śirasaḥ samīrarogān
jayati janayatīndriyaprasādaṃ svarahanumūrdhabalaṃ ca mūrdhatailam
sarveṣām akṣirogāṇām ādāvāścyotanaṃ hitam
ruktodakaṇḍugharṣāśrudāharāganibarhaṇam
uṣṇaṃ vāte kaphe koṣṇaṃ tacchītaṃ raktapittayoḥ
nivātasthasya vāmena pāṇinonmīlya locanam
śuktau pralambayānyena picuvartyā kanīnike
daśa dvādaśa vā bindūn dvyaṅgulād avasecayet
tataḥ pramṛjya mṛdunā cailena kaphavātayoḥ
anyena koṣṇapānīyaplutena svedayen mṛdu
atyuṣṇatīkṣṇaṃ rugrāgadṛṅnāśāyākṣisecanam
atiśītaṃ tu kurute nistodastambhavedanāḥ
kaṣāyavartmatāṃ gharṣaṃ kṛcchrād unmeṣaṇaṃ bahu
vikāravṛddhim atyalpaṃ saṃrambham aparisrutam
gatvā saṃdhiśiroghrāṇamukhasrotāṃsi bheṣajam
ūrdhvagān nayane nyastam apavartayate malān
athāñjanaṃ śuddhatanor netramātrāśraye male
pakvaliṅge 'lpaśophātikaṇḍūpaicchilyalakṣite
mandagharṣāśrurāge 'kṣṇi prayojyaṃ ghanadūṣike
ārte pittakaphāsṛgbhir mārutena viśeṣataḥ
lekhanaṃ ropaṇaṃ dṛṣṭiprasādanam iti tridhā
añjanaṃ lekhanaṃ tatra kaṣāyāmlapaṭūṣaṇaiḥ
ropaṇaṃ tiktakair dravyaiḥ svāduśītaiḥ prasādanam
tīkṣṇāñjanābhisaṃtapte nayane tat prasādanam
prayujyamānaṃ labhate pratyañjanasamāhvayam
daśāṅgulā tanur madhye śalākā mukulānanā
praśastā lekhane tāmrī ropaṇe kālalohajā
aṅgulī ca suvarṇotthā rūpyajā ca prasādane
piṇḍo rasakriyā cūrṇas tridhaivāñjanakalpanā
gurau madhye laghau doṣe tāṃ krameṇa prayojayet
hareṇumātrā piṇḍasya vellamātrā rasakriyā
tīkṣṇasya dviguṇaṃ tasya mṛdunaś cūrṇitasya ca
dve śalāke tu tīkṣṇasya tisras taditarasya ca
niśi svapne na madhyāhne mlāne noṣṇagabhastibhiḥ
akṣirogāya doṣāḥ syur vardhitotpīḍitadrutāḥ
prātaḥ sāyaṃ ca tacchāntyai vyabhre 'rke 'to 'ñjayet sadā
vadantyanye tu na divā prayojyaṃ tīkṣṇam añjanam
virekadurbalaṃ cakṣur ādityaṃ prāpya sīdati
svapnena rātrau kālasya saumyatvena ca tarpitā
śītasātmyā dṛg āgneyī sthiratāṃ labhate punaḥ
atyudrikte balāse tu lekhanīye 'thavā gade
kāmam ahnyapi nātyuṣṇe tīkṣṇam akṣṇi prayojayet
aśmano janma lohasya tata eva ca tīkṣṇatā
upaghāto 'pi tenaiva tathā netrasya tejasaḥ
na rātrāvapi śīte 'ti netre tīkṣṇāñjanaṃ hitam
doṣam asrāvayet stabdhaṃ kaṇḍūjāḍyādikāri tat
nāñjayed bhītavamitaviriktāśitavegite
kruddhajvaritatāntākṣiśirorukśokajāgare
adṛṣṭe 'rke śiraḥsnāte pītayor dhūmamadyayoḥ
ajīrṇe 'gnyarkasaṃtapte divāsupte pipāsite
atitīkṣṇamṛdustokabahvacchaghanakarkaśam
atyarthaśītalaṃ taptam añjanaṃ nāvacārayet
athānumīlayan dṛṣṭim antaḥ saṃcārayecchanaiḥ
añjite vartmanī kiṃcic cālayeccaivam añjanam
tīkṣṇaṃ vyāpnoti sahasā na conmeṣanimeṣaṇam
niṣpīḍanaṃ ca vartmabhyāṃ kṣālanaṃ vā samācaret
apetauṣadhasaṃrambhaṃ nirvṛtaṃ nayanaṃ yadā
vyādhidoṣartuyogyābhir adbhiḥ prakṣālayet tadā
dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhakenākṣi tato vāmaṃ savāsasā
ūrdhvavartmani saṃgṛhya śodhyaṃ vāmena cetarat
vartmaprāpto 'ñjanād doṣo rogān kuryād ato 'nyathā
kaṇḍūjāḍye 'ñjanaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ dhūmaṃ vā yojayet punaḥ
nayane tāmyati stabdhe śuṣke rūkṣe 'bhighātite
vātapittāture jihme śīrṇapakṣmāvilekṣaṇe
kṛcchronmīlasirāharṣasirotpātatamo'rjunaiḥ
syandamanthānyatovātavātaparyāyaśukrakaiḥ
āture śāntarāgāśruśūlasaṃrambhadūṣike
nivāte tarpaṇaṃ yojyaṃ śuddhayor mūrdhakāyayoḥ
kāle sādhāraṇe prātaḥ sāyaṃ vottānaśāyinaḥ
yavamāṣamayīṃ pālīṃ netrakośād bahiḥ samām
dvyaṅguloccāṃ dṛḍhāṃ kṛtvā yathāsvaṃ siddham āvapet
sarpir nimīlite netre taptāmbupravilāyitam
naktāndhyavātatimirakṛcchrabodhādike vasām
ā pakṣmāgrād athonmeṣaṃ śanakais tasya kurvataḥ
mātrā vigaṇayet tatra vartmasaṃdhisitāsite
dṛṣṭau ca kramaśo vyādhau śataṃ trīṇi ca pañca ca
śatāni sapta cāṣṭau ca daśa manthe daśānile
pitte ṣaṭ svasthavṛtte ca balāse pañca dhārayet
kṛtvāpāṅge tato dvāraṃ snehaṃ pātre nigālayet
pibecca dhūmaṃ nekṣeta vyoma rūpaṃ ca bhāsvaram
itthaṃ pratidinaṃ vāyau pitte tvekāntaraṃ kaphe
svasthe tu dvyantaraṃ dadyād ā tṛpter iti yojayet
prakāśakṣamatā svāsthyaṃ viśadaṃ laghu locanam
tṛpte viparyayo 'tṛpte 'titṛpte śleṣmajā rujaḥ
snehapītā tanur iva klāntā dṛṣṭir hi sīdati
tarpaṇānantaraṃ tasmād dṛgbalādhānakāriṇam
puṭapākaṃ prayuñjīta pūrvokteṣveva yakṣmasu
sa vāte snehanaḥ śleṣmasahite lekhano hitaḥ
dṛgdaurbalye 'nile pitte rakte svasthe prasādanaḥ
bhūśayaprasahānūpamedomajjavasāmiṣaiḥ
snehanaṃ payasā piṣṭair jīvanīyaiśca kalpayet
mṛgapakṣiyakṛnmāṃsamuktāyastāmrasaindhavaiḥ
srotojaśaṅkhaphenālair lekhanaṃ mastukalkitaiḥ
mṛgapakṣiyakṛnmajjavasāntrahṛdayāmiṣaiḥ
madhuraiḥ saghṛtaiḥ stanyakṣīrapiṣṭaiḥ prasādanam
bilvamātraṃ pṛthak piṇḍaṃ māṃsabheṣajakalkayoḥ
uruvūkavaṭāmbhojapattraiḥ snehādiṣu kramāt
veṣṭayitvā mṛdā liptaṃ dhavadhanvanagomayaiḥ
pacet pradīptair agnyābhaṃ pakvaṃ niṣpīḍya tadrasam
netre tarpaṇavad yuñjyācchataṃ dve trīṇi dhārayet
lekhanasnehanāntyeṣu koṣṇau pūrvau himo 'paraḥ
dhūmapo 'nte tayor eva yogās tatra ca tṛptivat
tarpaṇaṃ puṭapākaṃ ca nasyānarhe na yojayet
yāvantyahāni yuñjīta dvistato hitabhāgbhavet
mālatīmallikāpuṣpair baddhākṣo nivasen niśām
sarvātmanā netrabalāya yatnaṃ kurvīta nasyāñjanatarpaṇādyaiḥ
dṛṣṭiś ca naṣṭā vividhaṃ jagacca tamomayaṃ jāyata ekarūpam
nānāvidhānāṃ śalyānāṃ nānādeśaprabodhinām
āhartum abhyupāyo yastad yantraṃ yacca darśane
arśobhagandarādīnāṃ śastrakṣārāgniyojane
śeṣāṅgaparirakṣāyāṃ tathā vastyādikarmaṇi
ghaṭikālābuśṛṅgaṃ ca jāmbavauṣṭhādikāni ca
anekarūpakāryāṇi yantrāṇi vividhānyataḥ
vikalpya kalpayet buddhyā yathāsthūlaṃ tu vakṣyate
tulyāni kaṅkasiṃharkṣakākādimṛgapakṣiṇām
mukhair mukhāni yantrāṇāṃ kuryāt tatsaṃjñakāni ca
aṣṭādaśāṅgulāyāmānyāyasāni ca bhūriśaḥ
masūrākāraparyantaiḥ kaṇṭhe baddhāni kīlakaiḥ
vidyāt svastikayantrāṇi mūle 'ṅkuśanatāni ca
tair dṛḍhair asthisaṃlagnaśalyāharaṇam iṣyate
kīlabaddhavimuktāgrau saṃdaṃśau ṣoḍaśāṅgulau
tvaksirāsnāyupiśitalagnaśalyāpakarṣaṇau
ṣaḍaṅgulo 'nyo haraṇe sūkṣmaśalyopapakṣmaṇām
mucuṇḍī sūkṣmadantarjur mūle rucakabhūṣaṇā
gambhīravraṇamāṃsānām armaṇaḥ śeṣitasya ca
dve dvādaśāṅgule matsyatālavat dvyekatālake
tālayantre smṛte karṇanāḍīśalyāpahāriṇī
nāḍīyantrāṇi suṣirāṇy ekānekamukhāni ca
srotogatānāṃ śalyānām āmayānāṃ ca darśane
kriyāṇāṃ sukaratvāya kuryād ācūṣaṇāya ca
tadvistāraparīṇāhadairghyaṃ sroto'nurodhataḥ
daśāṅgulārdhanāhāntaḥkaṇṭhaśalyāvalokinī
nāḍī pañcamukhacchidrā catuṣkarṇasya saṃgrahe
vāraṅgasya dvikarṇasya tricchidrā tatpramāṇataḥ
nāḍīr evaṃvidhāś cānyā draṣṭuṃ śalyāni kārayet
padmakarṇikayā mūrdhni sadṛśī dvādaśāṅgulā
caturthasuṣirā nāḍī śalyanirghātinī matā
arśasāṃ gostanākāraṃ yantrakaṃ caturaṅgulam
nāhe pañcāṅgulaṃ puṃsāṃ pramadānāṃ ṣaḍaṅgulam
dvicchidraṃ darśane vyādher ekacchidraṃ tu karmaṇi
madhye 'sya tryaṅgulaṃ chidram aṅguṣṭhodaravistṛtam
ardhāṅgulocchritodvṛttakarṇikaṃ ca tadūrdhvataḥ
śamyākhyaṃ tādṛg acchidraṃ yantram arśaḥprapīḍanam
sarvathāpanayed oṣṭhaṃ chidrād ūrdhvaṃ bhagandare
ghrāṇārbudārśasām ekacchidrā nāḍyaṅguladvayā
pradeśinīparīṇāhā syād bhagandarayantravat
aṅgulītrāṇakaṃ dāntaṃ vārkṣaṃ vā caturaṅgulam
dvicchidraṃ gostanākāraṃ tadvaktravivṛtau sukham
yonivraṇekṣaṇaṃ madhye suṣiraṃ ṣoḍaśāṅgulam
mudrābaddhaṃ caturbhittam ambhojamukulānanam
catuḥśalākam ākrāntaṃ mūle tad vikasen mukhe
yantre nāḍīvraṇābhyaṅgakṣālanāya ṣaḍaṅgule
vastiyantrākṛtī mūle mukhe 'ṅguṣṭhakalāyakhe
agrato 'karṇike mūle nibaddhamṛducarmaṇī
dvidvārā nalikā picchanalikā vodakodare
dhūmavastyādiyantrāṇi nirdiṣṭāni yathāyatham
tryaṅgulāsyaṃ bhavecchṛṅgaṃ cūṣaṇe 'ṣṭādaśāṅgulam
agre siddhārthakacchidraṃ sunaddhaṃ cūcukākṛti
syād dvādaśāṅgulo 'lābur nāhe tvaṣṭādaśāṅgulaḥ
catustryaṅgulavṛttāsyo dīpto 'ntaḥ śleṣmaraktahṛt
tadvad ghaṭī hitā gulmavilayonnamane ca sā
śalākākhyāni yantrāṇi nānākarmākṛtīni ca
yathāyogapramāṇāni teṣām eṣaṇakarmaṇī
ubhe gaṇḍūpadamukhe srotobhyaḥ śalyahāriṇī
masūradalavaktre dve syātām aṣṭanavāṅgule
śaṅkavaḥ ṣaḍ ubhau teṣāṃ ṣoḍaśadvādaśāṅgulau
vyūhane 'hiphaṇāvaktrau dvau daśadvādaśāṅgulau
cālane śarapuṅkhāsyāvāhārye baḍiśākṛtī
nato 'gre śaṅkunā tulyo garbhaśaṅkur iti smṛtaḥ
aṣṭāṅgulāyatas tena mūḍhagarbhaṃ haret striyāḥ
aśmaryāharaṇaṃ sarpaphaṇāvad vakram agrataḥ
śarapuṅkhamukhaṃ dantapātanaṃ caturaṅgulam
kārpāsavihitoṣṇīṣāḥ śalākāḥ ṣaṭ pramārjane
pāyāvāsannadūrārthe dve daśadvādaśāṅgule
dve ṣaṭsaptāṅgule ghrāṇe dve karṇe 'ṣṭanavāṅgule
karṇaśodhanam aśvatthapattraprāntaṃ sruvānanam
śalākājāmbavauṣṭhānāṃ kṣāre 'gnau ca pṛthak trayam
yuñjyāt sthūlāṇudīrghāṇāṃ śalākām antravardhmani
madhyordhvavṛttadaṇḍāṃ ca mūle cārdhendusaṃnibhām
kolāsthidalatulyāsyā nāsārśo'rbudadāhakṛt
aṣṭāṅgulā nimnamukhās tisraḥ kṣārauṣadhakrame
kanīnīmadhyamānāmīnakhamānasamair mukhaiḥ
svaṃ svam uktāni yantrāṇi meḍhraśuddhyañjanādiṣu
anuyantrāṇyayaskāntarajjūvastrāśmamudgarāḥ
vadhrāntrajihvāvālāśca śākhānakhamukhadvijāḥ
kālaḥ pākaḥ karaḥ pādo bhayaṃ harṣaś ca tatkriyāḥ
upāyavit pravibhajed ālocya nipuṇaṃ dhiyā
nirghātanonmathanapūraṇamārgaśuddhisaṃvyūhanāharaṇabandhanapīḍanāni
ācūṣaṇonnamananāmanacālabhaṅgavyāvartanarjukaraṇāni ca yantrakarma
vivartate sādhvavagāhate ca grāhyaṃ gṛhītvoddharate ca yasmāt
yantreṣvataḥ kaṅkamukhaṃ pradhānaṃ sthāneṣu sarveṣvadhikāri yacca
ṣaḍviṃśatiḥ sukarmārair ghaṭitāni yathāvidhi
śastrāṇi romavāhīni bāhulyenāṅgulāni ṣaṭ
surūpāṇi sudhārāṇi sugrahāṇi ca kārayet
akarālāni sudhmātasutīkṣṇāvartite 'yasi
samāhitamukhāgrāṇi nīlāmbhojacchavīni ca
nāmānugatarūpāṇi sadā saṃnihitāni ca
svonmānārdhacaturthāṃśaphalānyekaikaśo 'pi ca
prāyo dvitrāṇi yuñjīta tāni sthānaviśeṣataḥ
maṇḍalāgraṃ phale teṣāṃ tarjanyantarnakhākṛti
lekhane chedane yojyaṃ pothakīśuṇḍikādiṣu
vṛddhipattraṃ kṣurākāraṃ chedabhedanapāṭane
ṛjvagram unnate śophe gambhīre ca tad anyathā
natāgraṃ pṛṣṭhato dīrghahrasvavaktraṃ yathāśrayam
utpalādhyardhadhārākhye bhedane chedane tathā
sarpāsyaṃ ghrāṇakarṇārśaśchedane 'rdhāṅgulaṃ phale
gateranveṣaṇe ślakṣṇā gaṇḍūpadamukhaiṣaṇī
bhedanārthe 'parā sūcīmukhā mūlaniviṣṭakhā
vetasaṃ vyadhane srāvye śarāryāsyatrikūrcake
kuśāṭā vadane srāvye dvyaṅgulaṃ syāt tayoḥ phalam
tadvad antarmukhaṃ tasya phalam adhyardham aṅgulam
ardhacandrānanaṃ caitat tathādhyardhāṅgulaṃ phale
vrīhivaktraṃ prayojya ca tat sirodarayor vyadhe
pṛthuḥ kuṭhārī godantasadṛśārdhāṅgulānanā
tayordhvadaṇḍayā vidhyed uparyasthnāṃ sthitāṃ sirām
tāmrī śalākā dvimukhī mukhe kuruvakākṛtiḥ
liṅganāśaṃ tayā vidhyet kuryād aṅguliśastrakam
mudrikānirgatamukhaṃ phale tvardhāṅgulāyatam
yogato vṛddhipattreṇa maṇḍalāgreṇa vā samam
tat pradeśinyagraparvapramāṇārpaṇamudrikam
sūtrabaddhaṃ galasrotorogacchedanabhedane
grahaṇe śuṇḍikārmāder baḍiśaṃ sunatānanam
chede 'sthnāṃ karapattraṃ tu kharadhāraṃ daśāṅgulam
vistāre dvyaṅgulaṃ sūkṣmadantaṃ sutsarubandhanam
snāyusūtrakacachede kartarī kartarīnibhā
vakrarjudhāraṃ dvimukhaṃ nakhaśastraṃ navāṅgulam
sūkṣmaśalyoddhṛticchedabhedapracchānalekhane
ekadhāraṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ prabaddhākṛti caikataḥ
dantalekhanakaṃ tena śodhayed dantaśarkarām
vṛttā gūḍhadṛḍhāḥ pāśe tisraḥ sūcyo 'tra sīvane
māṃsalānāṃ pradeśānāṃ tryaśrā tryaṅgulam āyatā
alpamāṃsāsthisaṃdhisthavraṇānāṃ dvyaṅgulāyatā
vrīhivaktrā dhanurvakrā pakvāmāśayamarmasu
sā sārdhadvyaṅgulā sarvavṛttās tāścaturaṅgulāḥ
kūrco vṛttaikapīṭhasthāḥ saptāṣṭau vā subandhanāḥ
sa yojyo nīlikāvyaṅgakeśaśāteṣu kuṭṭane
ardhāṅgulamukhair vṛttairaṣṭābhiḥ kaṇṭakaiḥ khajaḥ
pāṇibhyāṃ mathyamānena ghrāṇāt tena hared asṛk
vyadhanaṃ karṇapālīnāṃ yūthikāmukulānanam
ārārdhāṅgulavṛttāsyā tatpraveśā tathordhvataḥ
caturaśrā tayā vidhyecchophaṃ pakvāmasaṃśaye
karṇapālīṃ ca bahalāṃ bahalāyāśca śasyate
sūcī tribhāgasuṣirā tryaṅgulā karṇavedhanī
jalaukaḥkṣāradahanakācopalanakhādayaḥ
alauhānyanuśastrāṇi tānyevaṃ ca vikalpayet
aparāṇyapi yantrādīnyupayogaṃ ca yaugikam
utpāṭyapāṭyasīvyaiṣyalekhyapracchānakuṭṭanam
chedyaṃ bhedyaṃ vyadho mantho graho dāhaśca tatkriyāḥ
kuṇṭhakhaṇḍatanusthūlahrasvadīrghatvavakratāḥ
śastrāṇāṃ kharadhāratvam aṣṭau doṣāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
chedabhedanalekhyārthaṃ śastraṃ vṛntaphalāntare
tarjanīmadhyamāṅguṣṭhair gṛhṇīyāt susamāhitaḥ
visrāvaṇāni vṛntāgre tarjanyaṅguṣṭhakena ca
talapracchannavṛntāgraṃ grāhyaṃ vrīhimukhaṃ mukhe
mūleṣvāharaṇārthāni kriyāsaukaryato 'param
syān navāṅgulavistāraḥ sughano dvādaśāṅgulaḥ
kṣaumapattrorṇakauśeyadukūlamṛducarmajaḥ
vinyastapāśaḥ susyūtaḥ sāntarorṇāsthaśastrakaḥ
śalākāpihitāsyaśca śastrakośaḥ susaṃcayaḥ
jalaukasas tu sukhināṃ raktasrāvāya yojayet
duṣṭāmbumatsyabhekāhiśavakothamalodbhavāḥ
raktāḥ śvetā bhṛśaṃ kṛṣṇāścapalāḥ sthūlapicchilāḥ
indrāyudhavicitrordhvarājayo romaśāśca tāḥ
saviṣā varjayet tābhiḥ kaṇḍūpākajvarabhramāḥ
viṣapittāsranut kāryaṃ tatra śuddhāmbujāḥ punaḥ
nirviṣāḥ śaivalaśyāvā vṛttā nīlordhvarājayaḥ
kaṣāyapṛṣṭhās tanvaṅgyaḥ kiṃcitpītodarāśca yāḥ
tā apyasamyagvamanāt pratataṃ ca nipātanāt
sīdantīḥ salilaṃ prāpya raktamattā iti tyajet
athetarā niśākalkayukte 'mbhasi pariplutāḥ
avantisome takre vā punaścāśvāsitā jale
lāgayed ghṛtamṛtstanyaraktaśastranipātanaiḥ
pibantīrunnataskandhāśchādayen mṛduvāsasā
saṃpṛktād duṣṭaśuddhāsrāj jalaukā duṣṭaśoṇitam
ādatte prathamaṃ haṃsaḥ kṣīraṃ kṣīrodakād iva
gulmārśovidradhīn kuṣṭhavātaraktagalāmayān
netrarugviṣavīsarpān śamayanti jalaukasaḥ
daṃśasya tode kaṇḍvāṃ vā mokṣayed vāmayecca tām
paṭutailāktavadanāṃ ślakṣṇakaṇḍanarūṣitām
rakṣan raktamadād bhūyaḥ saptāhaṃ tā na pātayet
pūrvavat paṭutā dārḍhyaṃ samyagvānte jalaukasām
klamo 'tiyogān mṛtyur vā durvānte stabdhatā madaḥ
anyatrānyatra tāḥ sthāpyā ghaṭe mṛtsnāmbugarbhiṇi
lālādikothanāśārthaṃ saviṣāḥ syus tadanvayāt
aśuddhau srāvayed daṃśān haridrāguḍamākṣikaiḥ
śatadhautājyapicavas tato lepāśca śītalāḥ
duṣṭaraktāpagamanāt sadyo rāgarujāṃ śamaḥ
aśuddhaṃ calitaṃ sthānāt sthitaṃ raktaṃ vraṇāśaye
vyamlībhavet paryuṣitaṃ tasmāt tat srāvayet punaḥ
yuñjyān nālābughaṭikā rakte pittena dūṣite
tāsām analasaṃyogād yuñjyāt tu kaphavāyunā
kaphena duṣṭaṃ rudhiraṃ na śṛṅgeṇa vinirharet
skannatvād vātapittābhyāṃ duṣṭaṃ śṛṅgeṇa nirharet
gātraṃ baddhvopari dṛḍhaṃ rajjvā paṭṭena vā samam
snāyusaṃdhyasthimarmāṇi tyajan pracchānam ācaret
adhodeśa pravisṛtaiḥ padairuparigāmibhiḥ
na gāḍhaghanatiryagbhir na pade padam ācaran
pracchānenaikadeśasthaṃ grathitaṃ jalajanmabhiḥ
harecchṛṅgādibhiḥ suptam asṛg vyāpi sirāvyadhaiḥ
pracchānaṃ piṇḍite vā syād avagāḍhe jalaukasaḥ
tvaksthe 'lābughaṭīśṛṅgaṃ siraiva vyāpake 'sṛji
vātādidhāma vā śṛṅgajalauko'lābubhiḥ kramāt
srutāsṛjaḥ pradehādyaiḥ śītaiḥ syād vāyukopataḥ
satodakaṇḍuḥ śophas taṃ sarpiṣoṣṇena secayet
athātaḥ sirāvyadhavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
madhuraṃ lavaṇaṃ kiṃcid aśītoṣṇam asaṃhatam
padmendragopahemāviśaśalohitalohitam
lohitaṃ prabhavaḥ śuddhaṃ tanos tenaiva ca sthitaḥ
tat pittaśleṣmalaiḥ prāyo dūṣyate kurute tataḥ
visarpavidradhiplīhagulmāgnisadanajvarān
mukhanetraśirorogamadatṛḍlavaṇāsyatāḥ
kuṣṭhavātāsrapittāsrakaṭvamlodgiraṇabhramān
śītoṣṇasnigdharūkṣādyairupakrāntāśca ye gadāḥ
samyak sādhyā na sidhyanti te ca raktaprakopajāḥ
teṣu srāvayituṃ raktam udriktaṃ vyadhayet sirām
na tūnaṣoḍaśātītasaptatyabdasrutāsṛjām
asnigdhāsveditātyarthasveditānilarogiṇām
garbhiṇīsūtikājīrṇapittāsraśvāsakāsinām
atīsārodaracchardipāṇḍusarvāṅgaśophinām
snehapīte prayukteṣu tathā pañcasu karmasu
nāyantritāṃ sirāṃ vidhyen na tiryaṅ nāpyanutthitām
nātiśītoṣṇavātābhreṣvanyatrātyayikād gadāt
śironetravikāreṣu lalāṭyāṃ mokṣayet sirām
apāṅgyām upanāsyāṃ vā karṇarogeṣu karṇajām
nāsārogeṣu nāsāgre sthitāṃ nāsālalāṭayoḥ
pīnase mukharogeṣu jihvauṣṭhahanutālugāḥ
jatrūrdhvagranthiṣu grīvākarṇaśaṅkhaśiraḥśritāḥ
uro'pāṅgalalāṭasthā unmāde 'pasmṛtau punaḥ
hanusaṃdhau samaste vā sirāṃ bhrūmadhyagāminīm
vidradhau pārśvaśūle ca pārśvakakṣāstanāntare
tṛtīyake 'ṃsayor madhye skandhasyādhaścaturthake
pravāhikāyāṃ śūlinyāṃ śroṇito dvyaṅgule sthitām
śukrameḍhrāmaye meḍhra ūrugāṃ galagaṇḍayoḥ
gṛdhrasyāṃ jānuno 'dhastād ūrdhvaṃ vā caturaṅgule
indravasteradho 'pacyāṃ dvyaṅgule caturaṅgule
ūrdhvaṃ gulphasya sakthyartau tathā kroṣṭukaśīrṣake
pādadāhe khuḍe harṣe vipādyāṃ vātakaṇṭake
cipye ca dvyaṅgule vidhyed upari kṣipramarmaṇaḥ
gṛdhrasyām iva viśvācyāṃ yathoktānām adarśane
marmahīne yathāsanne deśe 'nyāṃ vyadhayet sirām
atha snigdhatanuḥ sajjasarvopakaraṇo balī
kṛtasvastyayanaḥ snigdharasānnapratibhojitaḥ
agnitāpātapasvinno jānūccāsanasaṃsthitaḥ
mṛdupaṭṭāttakeśānto jānusthāpitakūrparaḥ
muṣṭibhyāṃ vastragarbhābhyāṃ manye gāḍhaṃ nipīḍayet
dantaprapīḍanotkāsagaṇḍādhmānāni cācaret
pṛṣṭhato yantrayeccainaṃ vastram āveṣṭayan naraḥ
kandharāyāṃ parikṣipya nyasyāntar vāmatarjanīm
eṣo 'ntarmukhavarjyānāṃ sirāṇāṃ yantraṇe vidhiḥ
tato madhyamayāṅgulyā vaidyo 'ṅguṣṭhavimuktayā
tāḍayed utthitāṃ jñātvā sparśād vāṅguṣṭhapīḍanaiḥ
kuṭhāryā lakṣayen madhye vāmahastagṛhītayā
phaloddeśe suniṣkampaṃ sirāṃ tadvacca mokṣayet
tāḍayan pīḍayaṃścaināṃ vidhyed vrīhimukhena tu
aṅguṣṭhenonnamayyāgre nāsikām upanāsikām
abhyunnatavidaṣṭāgrajihvasyādhas tadāśrayām
yantrayet stanayorūrdhvaṃ grīvāśritasirāvyadhe
pāṣāṇagarbhahastasya jānusthe prasṛte bhuje
kukṣerārabhya mṛdite vidhyed baddhordhvapaṭṭake
vidhyeddhastasirāṃ bāhāv anākuñcitakūrpare
baddhvā sukhopaviṣṭasya muṣṭim aṅguṣṭhagarbhiṇam
ūrdhvaṃ vedhyapradeśācca paṭṭikāṃ caturaṅgule
vidhyed ālambamānasya bāhubhyāṃ pārśvayoḥ sirām
prahṛṣṭe mehane jaṅghāsirāṃ jānunyakuñcite
pāde tu susthite 'dhastājjānusaṃdher nipīḍite
gāḍhaṃ karābhyām ā gulphaṃ caraṇe tasya copari
dvitīye kuñcite kiṃcidārūḍhe hastavat tataḥ
baddhvā vidhyet sirām ittham anukteṣvapi kalpayet
teṣu teṣu pradeśeṣu tat tad yantram upāyavit
māṃsale nikṣiped deśe vrīhyāsyaṃ vrīhimātrakam
yavārdham asthnām upari sirāṃ vidhyan kuṭhārikām
samyagviddhā sraveddhārāṃ yantre mukte tu na sravet
alpakālaṃ vahatyalpaṃ durviddhā tailacūrṇanaiḥ
saśabdam atividdhā tu sraved duḥkhena dhāryate
bhīmūrchāyantraśaithilyakuṇṭhaśastrātitṛptayaḥ
kṣāmatvavegitāsvedā raktasyāsrutihetavaḥ
asamyag asre sravati vellavyoṣaniśānataiḥ
sāgāradhūmalavaṇatailair dihyāt sirāmukham
samyakpravṛtte koṣṇena tailena lavaṇena ca
agre sravati duṣṭāsraṃ kusumbhād iva pītikā
samyak srutvā svayaṃ tiṣṭhecchuddhaṃ tad iti nāharet
yantraṃ vimucya mūrchāyāṃ vījite vyajanaiḥ punaḥ
srāvayen mūrchati punas tvaparedyus tryahe 'pi vā
vātācchyāvāruṇaṃ rūkṣaṃ vegasrāvyacchaphenilam
pittāt pītāsitaṃ visram askandyauṣṇyāt sacandrikam
kaphāt snigdham asṛk pāṇḍu tantumat picchilaṃ ghanam
saṃsṛṣṭaliṅgaṃ saṃsargāt tridoṣaṃ malināvilam
aśuddhau balino 'pyasraṃ na prasthāt srāvayet param
atisrutau hi mṛtyuḥ syād dāruṇā vā calāmayāḥ
tatrābhyaṅgarasakṣīraraktapānāni bheṣajam
srute rakte śanair yantram apanīya himāmbunā
prakṣālya tailaplotāktaṃ bandhanīyaṃ sirāmukham
aśuddhaṃ srāvayed bhūyaḥ sāyam ahnyapare 'pi vā
snehopaskṛtadehasya pakṣād vā bhṛśadūṣitam
kiṃciddhi śeṣe duṣṭāsre naiva rogo 'tivartate
saśeṣam apyato dhāryaṃ na cātisrutim ācaret
harecchṛṅgādibhiḥ śeṣaṃ prasādam athavā nayet
śītopacārapittāsrakriyāśuddhiviśoṣaṇaiḥ
duṣṭaṃ raktam anudriktam evam eva prasādayet
rakte tvatiṣṭhati kṣipraṃ stambhanīm ācaret kriyām
lodhrapriyaṅgupattaṅgamāṣayaṣṭyāhvagairikaiḥ
mṛtkapālāñjanakṣaumamaṣīkṣīritvagaṅkuraiḥ
vicūrṇayed vraṇamukhaṃ padmakādihimaṃ pibet
tām eva vā sirāṃ vidhyed vyadhāt tasmād anantaram
sirāmukhaṃ vā tvaritaṃ dahet taptaśalākayā
unmārgagā yantranipīḍanena svasthānam āyānti punar na yāvat
doṣāḥ praduṣṭā rudhiraṃ prapannās tāvaddhitāhāravihārabhāk syāt
nātyuṣṇaśītaṃ laghu dīpanīyaṃ rakte 'panīte hitam annapānam
tadā śarīraṃ hyanavasthitāsṛg agnir viśeṣād iti rakṣitavyaḥ
prasannavarṇendriyam indriyārthān icchantam avyāhatapaktṛvegam
sukhānvitaṃ puṣṭibalopapannaṃ viśuddharaktaṃ puruṣaṃ vadanti
athātaḥ śalyāharaṇavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
vakrarjutiryagūrdhvādhaḥ śalyānāṃ pañcadhā gatiḥ
dhyāmaṃ śopharujāvantaṃ sravantaṃ śoṇitaṃ muhuḥ
abhyudgataṃ budbudavat piṭikopacitaṃ vraṇam
mṛdumāṃsaṃ ca jānīyād antaḥśalyaṃ samāsataḥ
viśeṣāt tvaggate śalye vivarṇaḥ kaṭhināyataḥ
śopho bhavati māṃsasthe coṣaḥ śopho vivardhate
pīḍanākṣamatā pākaḥ śalyamārgo na rohati
peśyantaragate māṃsaprāptavacchvayathuṃ vinā
ākṣepaḥ snāyujālasya saṃrambhastambhavedanāḥ
snāyuge durharaṃ caitat sirādhmānaṃ sirāśrite
svakarmaguṇahāniḥ syāt srotasāṃ srotasi sthite
dhamanīsthe 'nilo raktaṃ phenayuktam udīrayet
niryāti śabdavān syācca hṛllāsaḥ sāṅgavedanaḥ
saṃgharṣo balavān asthisaṃdhiprāpte 'sthipūrṇatā
naikarūpā rujo 'sthisthe śophas tadvacca saṃdhige
ceṣṭānivṛttiśca bhaved āṭopaḥ koṣṭhasaṃśrite
ānāho 'nnaśakṛnmūtradarśanaṃ ca vraṇānane
vidyān marmagataṃ śalyaṃ marmaviddhopalakṣaṇaiḥ
yathāsvaṃ ca parisrāvais tvagādiṣu vibhāvayet
ruhyate śuddhadehānām anulomasthitaṃ tu tat
doṣakopābhighātādikṣobhād bhūyo 'pi bādhate
tvaṅnaṣṭe yatra tatra syurabhyaṅgasvedamardanaiḥ
rāgarugdāhasaṃrambhā yatra cājyaṃ vilīyate
āśu śuṣyati lepo vā tatsthānaṃ śalyavad vadet
māṃsapraṇaṣṭaṃ saṃśuddhyā karśanācchlathatāṃ gatam
kṣobhād rāgādibhiḥ śalyaṃ lakṣayet tadvad eva ca
peśyasthisaṃdhikoṣṭheṣu naṣṭam asthiṣu lakṣayet
asthnām abhyañjanasvedabandhapīḍanamardanaiḥ
prasāraṇākuñcanataḥ saṃdhinaṣṭaṃ tathāsthivat
naṣṭe snāyusirāsrotodhamanīṣvasame pathi
aśvayuktaṃ rathaṃ khaṇḍacakram āropya rogiṇam
śīghraṃ nayet tatas tasya saṃrambhācchalyam ādiśet
marmanaṣṭaṃ pṛthaṅ noktaṃ teṣāṃ māṃsādisaṃśrayāt
sāmānyena saśalyaṃ tu kṣobhiṇyā kriyayā saruk
vṛttaṃ pṛthu catuṣkoṇaṃ tripuṭaṃ ca samāsataḥ
adṛśyaśalyasaṃsthānaṃ vraṇākṛtyā vibhāvayet
teṣām āharaṇopāyau pratilomānulomakau
arvācīnaparācīne nirharet tadviparyayāt
sukhāhāryaṃ yataśchittvā tatas tiryaggataṃ haret
śalyaṃ na nirghātyam uraḥkakṣāvaṅkṣaṇapārśvagam
pratilomam anuttuṇḍaṃ chedyaṃ pṛthumukhaṃ ca yat
naivāhared viśalyaghnaṃ naṣṭaṃ vā nirupadravam
athāharet karaprāpyaṃ kareṇaivetarat punaḥ
dṛśyaṃ siṃhāhimakaravarmikarkaṭakānanaiḥ
adṛśyaṃ vraṇasaṃsthānād grahītuṃ śakyate yataḥ
kaṅkabhṛṅgāhvakuraraśarārivāyasānanaiḥ
saṃdaṃśābhyāṃ tvagādisthaṃ tālābhyāṃ suṣiraṃ haret
suṣirasthaṃ tu nalakaiḥ śeṣaṃ śeṣair yathāyatham
śastreṇa vā viśasyādau tato nirlohitaṃ vraṇam
kṛtvā ghṛtena saṃsvedya baddhācārikam ādiśet
sirāsnāyuvilagnaṃ tu cālayitvā śalākayā
hṛdaye saṃsthitaṃ śalyaṃ trāsitasya himāmbunā
tataḥ sthānāntaraṃ prāptam āharet tad yathāyatham
yathāmārgaṃ durākarṣam anyato 'pyevam āharet
asthidaṣṭe naraṃ padbhyāṃ pīḍayitvā vinirharet
ityaśakye subalibhiḥ sugṛhītasya kiṅkaraiḥ
tathāpyaśakye vāraṅgaṃ vakrīkṛtya dhanurjyayā
subaddhaṃ vaktrakaṭake badhnīyāt susamāhitaḥ
susaṃyatasya pañcāṅgyā vājinaḥ kaśayātha tam
tāḍayed iti mūrdhānaṃ vegenonnamayan yathā
uddharecchalyam evaṃ vā śākhāyāṃ kalpayet taroḥ
baddhvā durbalavāraṅgaṃ kuśābhiḥ śalyam āharet
śvayathugrastavāraṅgaṃ śopham utpīḍya yuktitaḥ
mudgarāhatayā nāḍyā nirghātyottuṇḍitaṃ haret
taireva cānayen mārgam amārgottuṇḍitaṃ tu yat
mṛditvā karṇināṃ karṇaṃ nāḍyāsyena nigṛhya vā
ayaskāntena niṣkarṇaṃ vivṛtāsyam ṛjusthitam
pakvāśayagataṃ śalyaṃ virekeṇa vinirharet
duṣṭavātaviṣastanyaraktatoyādi cūṣaṇaiḥ
kaṇṭhasrotogate śalye sūtraṃ kaṇṭhe praveśayet
bisenātte tataḥ śalye bisaṃ sūtraṃ samaṃ haret
nāḍyāgnitāpitāṃ kṣiptvā śalākām apsthirīkṛtām
ānayejjātuṣaṃ kaṇṭhājjatudigdhām ajātuṣam
keśondukena pītena dravaiḥ kaṇṭakam ākṣipet
sahasā sūtrabaddhena vamatas tena cetarat
aśakyaṃ mukhanāsābhyām āhartuṃ parato nudet
appānaskandhaghātābhyāṃ grāsaśalyaṃ praveśayet
sūkṣmākṣivraṇaśalyāni kṣaumavālajalair haret
apāṃ pūrṇaṃ vidhunuyād avākśirasam āyatam
vāmayeccāmukhaṃ bhasmarāśau vā nikhanen naram
karṇe 'mbupūrṇe hastena mathitvā tailavāriṇī
kṣiped adhomukhaṃ karṇaṃ hanyād vā cūṣayeta vā
kīṭe srotogate karṇaṃ pūrayellavaṇāmbunā
śuktena vā sukhoṣṇena mṛte kledaharo vidhiḥ
jātuṣaṃ hemarūpyādidhātujaṃ ca cirasthitam
ūṣmaṇā prāyaśaḥ śalyaṃ dehajena vilīyate
mṛdveṇudāruśṛṅgāsthidantavālopalāni na
viṣāṇaveṇvayastāladāruśalyaṃ cirād api
prāyo nirbhujyate taddhi pacatyāśu palāsṛjī
śalye māṃsāvagāḍhe cet sa deśo na vidahyate
tatas taṃ mardanasvedaśuddhikarṣaṇabṛṃhaṇaiḥ
tīkṣṇopanāhapānānnaghanaśastrapadāṅkanaiḥ
pācayitvā harecchalyaṃ pāṭanaiṣaṇabhedanaiḥ
śalyapradeśayantrāṇām avekṣya bahurūpatām
tais tairupāyair matimān śalyaṃ vidyāt tathāharet
athātaḥ śastrakarmavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
vraṇaḥ saṃjāyate prāyaḥ pākācchvayathupūrvakāt
tam evopacaret tasmād rakṣan pākaṃ prayatnataḥ
suśītalepasekāsramokṣasaṃśodhanādibhiḥ
śopho 'lpo 'lpoṣmaruk sāmaḥ savarṇaḥ kaṭhinaḥ sthiraḥ
pacyamāno vivarṇas tu rāgī vastirivātataḥ
sphuṭatīva sanistodaḥ sāṅgamardavijṛmbhikaḥ
saṃrambhārucidāhoṣātṛḍjvarānidratānvitaḥ
styānaṃ viṣyandayatyājyaṃ vraṇavat sparśanāsahaḥ
pakve 'lpavegatā mlāniḥ pāṇḍutā valisaṃbhavaḥ
nāmo 'nteṣūnnatir madhye kaṇḍūśophādimārdavam
spṛṣṭe pūyasya saṃcāro bhaved vastāvivāmbhasaḥ
śūlaṃ narte 'nilād dāhaḥ pittācchophaḥ kaphodayāt
rāgo raktācca pākaḥ syād ato doṣaiḥ saśoṇitaiḥ
pāke 'tivṛtte suṣiras tanutvagdoṣabhakṣitaḥ
valībhirācitaḥ śyāvaḥ śīryamāṇatanūruhaḥ
kaphajeṣu tu śopheṣu gambhīraṃ pākam etyasṛk
pakvaliṅgaṃ tato 'spaṣṭaṃ yatra syācchītaśophatā
tvaksāvarṇyaṃ rujo 'lpatvaṃ ghanasparśatvam aśmavat
raktapākam iti brūyāt taṃ prājño muktasaṃśayaḥ
alpasattve 'bale bāle pākād vātyartham uddhate
dāraṇaṃ marmasaṃdhyādisthite cānyatra pāṭanam
āmacchede sirāsnāyuvyāpado 'sṛgatisrutiḥ
rujo 'tivṛddhir daraṇaṃ visarpo vā kṣatodbhavaḥ
tiṣṭhann antaḥ punaḥ pūyaḥ sirāsnāyvasṛgāmiṣam
vivṛddho dahati kṣipraṃ tṛṇolapam ivānalaḥ
yaśchinattyāmam ajñānād yaśca pakvam upekṣate
śvapacāviva vijñeyau tāvaniścitakāriṇau
prāk śastrakarmaṇaśceṣṭaṃ bhojayed annam āturam
pānapaṃ pāyayen madyaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ yo vedanākṣamaḥ
na mūrchatyannasaṃyogān mattaḥ śastraṃ na budhyate
anyatra mūḍhagarbhāśmamukharogodarāturāt
athāhṛtopakaraṇaṃ vaidyaḥ prāṅmukham āturam
saṃmukho yantrayitvāśu nyasyen marmādi varjayan
anulomaṃ suniśitaṃ śastram ā pūyadarśanāt
sakṛd evāharettacca pāke tu sumahatyapi
pāṭayed dvyaṅgulaṃ samyag dvyaṅgulatryaṅgulāntaram
eṣitvā samyag eṣiṇyā paritaḥ sunirūpitam
aṅgulīnālavālair vā yathādeśaṃ yathāśayam
yato gatāṃ gatiṃ vidyād utsaṅgo yatra yatra ca
tatra tatra vraṇaṃ kuryāt suvibhaktaṃ nirāśayam
āyataṃ ca viśālaṃ ca yathā doṣo na tiṣṭhati
śauryam āśukriyā tīkṣṇaṃ śastram asvedavepathū
asaṃmohaśca vaidyasya śastrakarmaṇi śasyate
tiryak chindyāllalāṭabhrūdantaveṣṭakajatruṇi
kukṣikakṣākṣikūṭauṣṭhakapolagalavaṅkṣaṇe
anyatra chedanāt tiryak sirāsnāyuvipāṭanam
śastre 'vacārite vāgbhiḥ śītāmbhobhiśca rogiṇam
āśvāsya parito 'ṅgulyā paripīḍya vraṇaṃ tataḥ
kṣālayitvā kaṣāyeṇa plotenāmbho 'panīya ca
guggulvagurusiddhārthahiṅgusarjarasānvitaiḥ
dhūpayet paṭuṣaḍgranthānimbapattrair ghṛtaplutaiḥ
tilakalkājyamadhubhir yathāsvaṃ bheṣajena ca
digdhāṃ vartiṃ tato dadyāt tairevācchādayecca tām
ghṛtāktaiḥ saktubhiścordhvaṃ ghanāṃ kavalikāṃ tataḥ
nidhāya yuktyā badhnīyāt paṭṭena susamāhitam
pārśve savye 'pasavye vā nādhastān naiva copari
śucisūkṣmadṛḍhāḥ paṭṭāḥ kavalyaḥ savikeśikāḥ
dhūpitā mṛdavaḥ ślakṣṇā nirvalīkā vraṇe hitāḥ
kurvītānantaraṃ tasya rakṣāṃ rakṣoniṣiddhaye
baliṃ copaharet tebhyaḥ sadā mūrdhnā ca dhārayet
lakṣmīṃ guhām atiguhāṃ jaṭilāṃ brahmacāriṇīm
vacāṃ chattrām aticchattrāṃ dūrvāṃ siddhārthakān api
tataḥ snehadinehoktaṃ tasyācāraṃ samādiśet
divāsvapno vraṇe kaṇḍūrāgarukśophapūyakṛt
strīṇāṃ tu smṛtisaṃsparśadarśanaiścalitasrute
śukre vyavāyajān doṣān asaṃsarge 'pyavāpnuyāt
bhojanaṃ ca yathāsātmyaṃ yavagodhūmaṣaṣṭikāḥ
masūramudgatubarījīvantīsuniṣaṇṇakāḥ
bālamūlakavārtākataṇḍulīyakavāstukam
kāravellakakarkoṭapaṭolakaṭukāphalam
saindhavaṃ dāḍimaṃ dhātrī ghṛtaṃ taptahimaṃ jalam
jīrṇaśālyodanaṃ snigdham alpam uṣṇodakottaram
bhuñjāno jāṅgalair māṃsaiḥ śīghraṃ vraṇam apohati
aśitaṃ mātrayā kāle pathyaṃ yāti jarāṃ sukham
ajīrṇāt tvanilādīnāṃ vibhramo balavān bhavet
tataḥ śopharujāpākadāhānāhān avāpnuyāt
navaṃ dhānyaṃ tilān māṣān madyaṃ māṃsam ajāṅgalam
kṣīrekṣuvikṛtīramlaṃ lavaṇaṃ kaṭukaṃ tyajet
yaccānyad api viṣṭambhi vidāhi guru śītalam
vargo 'yaṃ navadhānyādir vraṇinaḥ sarvadoṣakṛt
madyaṃ tīkṣṇoṣṇarūkṣāmlam āśu vyāpādayed vraṇam
vālośīraiśca vījyeta na cainaṃ parighaṭṭayet
na tuden na ca kaṇḍūyecceṣṭamānaśca pālayet
snigdhavṛddhadvijātīnāṃ kathāḥ śṛṇvan manaḥpriyāḥ
āśāvān vyādhimokṣāya kṣipraṃ vraṇam apohati
tṛtīye 'hni punaḥ kuryād vraṇakarma ca pūrvavat
prakṣālanādi divase dvitīye nācaret tathā
tīvravyatho vigrathitaścirāt saṃrohati vraṇaḥ
snigdhāṃ rūkṣāṃ ślathāṃ gāḍhāṃ durnyastāṃ ca vikeśikām
vraṇe na dadyāt kalkaṃ vā snehāt kledo vivardhate
māṃsacchedo 'tirugraukṣyād daraṇaṃ śoṇitāgamaḥ
ślathātigāḍhadurnyāsair vraṇavartmāvagharṣaṇam
sapūtimāṃsaṃ sotsaṅgaṃ sagatiṃ pūyagarbhiṇam
vraṇaṃ viśodhayecchīghraṃ sthitā hyantar vikeśikā
vyamlaṃ tu pāṭitaṃ śophaṃ pācanaiḥ samupācaret
bhojanairupanāhaiśca nātivraṇavirodhibhiḥ
sadyaḥ sadyovraṇān sīvyed vivṛtān abhighātajān
medojāṃllikhitān granthīn hrasvāḥ pālīśca karṇayoḥ
śiro'kṣikūṭanāsauṣṭhagaṇḍakarṇorubāhuṣu
grīvālalāṭamuṣkasphiṅmeḍhrapāyūdarādiṣu
gambhīreṣu pradeśeṣu māṃsaleṣvacaleṣu ca
na tu vaṅkṣaṇakakṣādāvalpamāṃse cale vraṇān
vāyunirvāhiṇaḥ śalyagarbhān kṣāraviṣāgnijān
sīvyeccalāsthiśuṣkāsratṛṇaromāpanīya tu
pralambi māṃsaṃ vicchinnaṃ niveśya svaniveśane
saṃdhyasthi ca sthite rakte snāyvā sūtreṇa valkalaiḥ
sīvyen na dūre nāsanne gṛhṇan nālpaṃ na vā bahu
sāntvayitvā tataścārtaṃ vraṇe madhughṛtadrutaiḥ
añjanakṣaumajamaṣīphalinīśallakīphalaiḥ
salodhramadhukair digdhe yuñjyād bandhādi pūrvavat
vraṇo niḥśoṇitauṣṭho yaḥ kiṃcid evāvalikhya tam
saṃjātarudhiraṃ sīvyet saṃdhānaṃ hyasya śoṇitam
bandhanāni tu deśādīn vīkṣya yuñjīta teṣu ca
āvikājinakauśeyam uṣṇaṃ kṣaumaṃ tu śītalam
śītoṣṇaṃ tulāsaṃtānakārpāsasnāyuvalkajam
tāmrāyastrapusīsāni vraṇe medaḥkaphādhike
bhaṅge ca yuñjyāt phalakaṃ carmavalkakuśādi ca
svanāmānugatākārā bandhās tu daśa pañca ca
kośasvastikamuttolīcīnadāmānuvellitam
khaṭvāvibandhasthagikāvitānotsaṅgagoṣphaṇāḥ
yamakaṃ maṇḍalākhyaṃ ca pañcāṅgī ceti yojayet
vidadhyāt teṣu teṣveva kośam aṅguliparvasu
svastikaṃ karṇakakṣādistaneṣūktaṃ ca saṃdhiṣu
muttolīṃ meḍhragrīvādau yuñjyāccīnam apāṅgayoḥ
saṃbādhe 'ṅge tathā dāma śākhāsvevānuvellitam
khaṭvāṃ gaṇḍe hanau śaṅkhe vibandhaṃ pṛṣṭhakodare
aṅguṣṭhāṅgulimeḍhrāgre sthagikām antravṛddhiṣu
vitānaṃ pṛthulāṅgādau tathā śirasi cerayet
vilambini tathotsaṅgaṃ nāsauṣṭhacibukādiṣu
goṣphaṇaṃ saṃdhiṣu tathā yamakaṃ yamike vraṇe
vṛtte 'ṅge maṇḍalākhyaṃ ca pañcāṅgīṃ cordhvajatruṣu
yo yatra suniviṣṭaḥ syāttaṃ teṣāṃ tatra buddhimān
badhnīyād gāḍham ūrusphikkakṣāvaṅkṣaṇamūrdhasu
śākhāvadanakarṇoraḥpṛṣṭhapārśvagalodare
samaṃ mehanamuṣke ca netre saṃdhiṣu ca ślatham
badhnīyācchithilasthāne vātaśleṣmodbhave samam
gāḍham eva samasthāne bhṛśaṃ gāḍhaṃ tadāśaye
śīte vasante 'pi ca tau mokṣaṇīyau tryahāt tryahāt
pittaraktotthayor bandho gāḍhasthāne samo mataḥ
samasthāne ślatho naiva śithilasyāśaye tathā
sāyaṃ prātas tayor mokṣo grīṣme śaradi ceṣyate
abaddho daṃśamaśakaśītavātādipīḍitaḥ
duṣṭībhavecciraṃ cātra na tiṣṭhet snehabheṣajam
kṛcchreṇa śuddhiṃ rūḍhiṃ vā yāti rūḍho vivarṇatām
baddhas tu cūrṇito bhagno viśliṣṭaḥ pāṭito 'pi vā
chinnasnāyusiro 'pyāśu sukhaṃ saṃrohati vraṇaḥ
utthānaśayanādyāsu sarvehāsu na pīḍyate
udvṛttauṣṭhaḥ samutsanno viṣamaḥ kaṭhino 'tiruk
samo mṛduraruk śīghraṃ vraṇaḥ śudhyati rohati
sthirāṇām alpamāṃsānāṃ raukṣyād anuparohatām
pracchādyam auṣadhaṃ pattrair yathādoṣaṃ yathartu ca
ajīrṇataruṇācchidraiḥ samantāt suniveśitaiḥ
dhautairakarkaśaiḥ kṣīribhūrjārjunakadambajaiḥ
kuṣṭhinām agnidagdhānāṃ piṭikā madhumehinām
karṇikāśconduruviṣe kṣāradagdhā viṣānvitāḥ
bandhanīyā na māṃspāke gudapāke ca dāruṇe
śīryamāṇāḥ sarugdāhāḥ śophāvasthāvisarpiṇaḥ
arakṣayā vraṇe yasmin makṣikā nikṣipet kṛmīn
te bhakṣayantaḥ kurvanti rujāśophāsrasaṃsravān
surasādiṃ prayuñjīta tatra dhāvanapūraṇe
saptaparṇakarañjārkanimbarājādanatvacaḥ
gomūtrakalkito lepaḥ sekaḥ kṣārāmbunā hitaḥ
pracchādya māṃsapeśyā vā vraṇaṃ tān āśu nirharet
na cainaṃ tvaramāṇo 'ntaḥ sadoṣam uparohayet
so 'lpenāpyapacāreṇa bhūyo vikurute yataḥ
rūḍhe 'pyajīrṇavyāyāmavyavāyādīn vivarjayet
harṣaṃ krodhaṃ bhayaṃ cāpi yāvad ā sthairyasaṃbhavāt
ādareṇānuvartyo 'yaṃ māsān ṣaṭ sapta vā vidhiḥ
utpadyamānāsu ca tāsu tāsu vārttāsu doṣādibalānusārī
tais tairupāyaiḥ prayataścikitsed ālocayan vistaram uttaroktam
athātaḥ kṣārāgnikarmavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
sarvaśastrānuśastrāṇāṃ kṣāraḥ śreṣṭho bahūni yat
chedyabhedyādikarmāṇi kurute viṣameṣvapi
duḥkhāvacāryaśastreṣu tena siddhim ayātsu ca
atikṛcchreṣu rogeṣu yacca pāne 'pi yujyate
sa peyo 'rśo'gnisādāśmagulmodaragarādiṣu
yojyaḥ sākṣān maṣaśvitrabāhyārśaḥkuṣṭhasuptiṣu
bhagandarārbudagranthiduṣṭanāḍīvraṇādiṣu
na tūbhayo 'pi yoktavyaḥ pitte rakte cale 'bale
jvare 'tīsāre hṛnmūrdharoge pāṇḍvāmaye 'rucau
timire kṛtasaṃśuddhau śvayathau sarvagātrage
bhīrugarbhiṇyṛtumatīprodvṛttaphalayoniṣu
ajīrṇe 'nne śiśau vṛddhe dhamanīsaṃdhimarmasu
taruṇāsthisirāsnāyusevanīgalanābhiṣu
deśe 'lpamāṃse vṛṣaṇameḍhrasrotonakhāntare
vartmarogād ṛte 'kṣṇośca śītavarṣoṣṇadurdine
kālamuṣkakaśamyākakadalīpāribhadrakān
aśvakarṇamahāvṛkṣapalāśāsphotavṛkṣakān
indravṛkṣārkapūtīkanaktamālāśvamārakān
kākajaṅghām apāmārgam agnimanthāgnitilvakān
sārdrān samūlaśākhādīn khaṇḍaśaḥ parikalpitān
kośātakīścatasraśca śūkaṃ nālaṃ yavasya ca
nivāte nicayīkṛtya pṛthak tāni śilātale
prakṣipya muṣkakacaye sudhāśmāni ca dīpayet
tatas tilānāṃ kutalair dagdhvāgnau vigate pṛthak
kṛtvā sudhāśmanāṃ bhasma droṇaṃ tvitarabhasmanaḥ
muṣkakottaram ādāya pratyekaṃ jalamūtrayoḥ
gālayed ardhabhāreṇa mahatā vāsasā ca tat
yāvat picchilaraktācchas tīkṣṇo jātas tadā ca tam
gṛhītvā kṣāraniṣyandaṃ pacel lauhyāṃ vighaṭṭayan
pacyamāne tatas tasmiṃs tāḥ sudhābhasmaśarkarāḥ
śuktīḥ kṣīrapakaṃ śaṅkhanābhīścāyasabhājane
kṛtvāgnivarṇān bahuśaḥ kṣārotthe kuḍavonmite
nirvāpya piṣṭvā tenaiva pratīvāpaṃ vinikṣipet
ślakṣṇaṃ śakṛd dakṣaśikhigṛdhrakaṅkakapotajam
catuṣpātpakṣipittālamanohvālavaṇāni ca
paritaḥ sutarāṃ cāto darvyā tam avaghaṭṭayet
sabāṣpaiśca yadottiṣṭhed budbudair lehavad ghanaḥ
avatārya tadā śīto yavarāśāvayomaye
sthāpyo 'yaṃ madhyamaḥ kṣāro na tu piṣṭvā kṣipen mṛdau
nirvāpyāpanayet tīkṣṇe pūrvavat prativāpanam
tathā lāṅgalikādantīcitrakātiviṣāvacāḥ
svarjikākanakakṣīrīhiṅgupūtikapallavāḥ
tālapattrī viḍaṃ ceti saptarātrāt paraṃ tu saḥ
yojyas tīkṣṇo 'nilaśleṣmamedojeṣvarbudādiṣu
madhyeṣveṣveva madhyo 'nyaḥ pittāsragudajanmasu
balārthaṃ kṣīṇapānīye kṣārāmbu punarāvapet
nātitīkṣṇamṛduḥ ślakṣṇaḥ picchilaḥ śīghragaḥ sitaḥ
śikharī sukhanirvāpyo na viṣyandī na cātiruk
kṣāro daśaguṇaḥ śastratejasorapi karmakṛt
ācūṣann iva saṃrambhād gātram āpīḍayann iva
sarvato 'nusaran doṣān unmūlayati mūlataḥ
karma kṛtvā gatarujaḥ svayam evopaśāmyati
kṣārasādhye gade chinne likhite srāvite 'thavā
kṣāraṃ śalākayā dattvā plotaprāvṛtadehayā
mātrāśatam upekṣeta tatrārśaḥsvāvṛtānanam
hastena yantraṃ kurvīta vartmarogeṣu vartmanī
nirbhujya picunācchādya kṛṣṇabhāgaṃ vinikṣipet
padmapattratanuḥ kṣāralepo ghrāṇārbudeṣu ca
pratyādityaṃ niṣaṇṇasya samunnamyāgranāsikām
mātrā vidhāryaḥ pañcāśat tadvad arśasi karṇaje
kṣāraṃ pramārjanenānu parimṛjyāvagamya ca
sudagdhaṃ ghṛtamadhvaktaṃ tat payomastukāñjikaiḥ
nirvāpayet tataḥ sājyaiḥ svāduśītaiḥ pradehayet
abhiṣyandīni bhojyāni bhojyāni kledanāya ca
yadi ca sthiramūlatvāt kṣāradagdhaṃ na śīryate
dhānyāmlabījayaṣṭyāhvatilairālepayet tataḥ
tilakalkaḥ samadhuko ghṛtākto vraṇaropaṇaḥ
pakvajambvasitaṃ sannaṃ samyagdagdhaṃ viparyaye
tāmratātodakaṇḍvādyair durdagdhaṃ taṃ punar dahet
atidagdhe sraved raktaṃ mūrchādāhajvarādayaḥ
gude viśeṣād viṇmūtrasaṃrodho 'tipravartanam
puṃstvopaghāto mṛtyur vā gudasya śātanāddhruvam
nāsāyāṃ nāsikāvaṃśadaraṇākuñcanodbhavaḥ
bhavecca viṣayājñānaṃ tadvacchrotrādikeṣvapi
viśeṣād atra seko 'mlair lepo madhu ghṛtaṃ tilāḥ
vātapittaharā ceṣṭā sarvaiva śiśirā kriyā
amlo hi śītaḥ sparśena kṣāras tenopasaṃhitaḥ
yātyāśu svādutāṃ tasmād amlair nirvāpayettarām
viṣāgniśastrāśanimṛtyutulyaḥ kṣāro bhaved alpam atiprayuktaḥ
rogān nihanyād acireṇa ghorān sa dhīmatā samyag anuprayuktaḥ
agniḥ kṣārād api śreṣṭhas taddagdhānām asaṃbhavāt
bheṣajakṣāraśastraiśca na siddhānāṃ prasādhanāt
tvaci māṃse sirāsnāyusaṃdhyasthiṣu sa yujyate
maṣāṅgaglānimūrdhārtimanthakīlatilādiṣu
tvagdāho vartigodantasūryakāntaśarādibhiḥ
arśobhagandaragranthināḍīduṣṭavraṇādiṣu
māṃsadāho madhusnehajāmbavauṣṭhaguḍādibhiḥ
śliṣṭavartmanyasṛksrāvanīlyasamyagvyadhādiṣu
sirādidāhas taireva na dahet kṣāravāritān
antaḥśalyāsṛjo bhinnakoṣṭhān bhūrivraṇāturān
sudagdhaṃ ghṛtamadhvaktaṃ snigdhaśītaiḥ pradehayet
tasya liṅgaṃ sthite rakte śabdavallasikānvitam
pakvatālakapotābhaṃ surohaṃ nātivedanam
pramādadagdhavat sarvaṃ durdagdhātyarthadagdhayoḥ
caturdhā tat tu tucchena saha tucchasya lakṣaṇam
tvag vivarṇoṣyate 'tyarthaṃ na ca sphoṭasamudbhavaḥ
sasphoṭadāhatīvroṣaṃ durdagdham atidāhataḥ
māṃsalambanasaṃkocadāhadhūpanavedanāḥ
sirādināśas tṛṇmūrchāvraṇagāmbhīryamṛtyavaḥ
tucchasyāgnipratapanaṃ kāryam uṣṇaṃ ca bheṣajam
styāne 'sre vedanātyarthaṃ vilīne mandatā rujaḥ
durdagdhe śītam uṣṇaṃ ca yuñjyād ādau tato himam
samyagdagdhe tavakṣīrīplakṣacandanagairikaiḥ
limpet sājyāmṛtairūrdhvaṃ pittavidradhivat kriyā
atidagdhe drutaṃ kuryāt sarvaṃ pittavisarpavat
snehadagdhe bhṛśataraṃ rūkṣaṃ tatra tu yojayet
śastrakṣārāgnayo yasmān mṛtyoḥ paramam āyudham
apramatto bhiṣak tasmāt tān samyag avacārayet
samāpyate sthānam idaṃ hṛdayasya rahasyavat
atrārthāḥ sūtritāḥ sūkṣmāḥ pratanyante hi sarvataḥ
athāto garbhāvakrāntiśārīraṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
śuddhe śukrārtave sattvaḥ svakarmakleśacoditaḥ
garbhaḥ sampadyate yuktivaśād agnirivāraṇau
bījātmakair mahābhūtaiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ sattvānugaiśca saḥ
mātuścāhārarasajaiḥ kramāt kukṣau vivardhate
tejo yathārkaraśmīnāṃ sphaṭikena tiraskṛtam
nendhanaṃ dṛśyate gacchat sattvo garbhāśayaṃ tathā
kāraṇānuvidhāyitvāt kāryāṇāṃ tatsvabhāvatā
nānāyonyākṛtīḥ sattvo dhatte 'to drutalohavat
ata eva ca śukrasya bāhulyāj jāyate pumān
raktasya strī tayoḥ sāmye klībaḥ śukrārtave punaḥ
vāyunā bahuśo bhinne yathāsvaṃ bahvapatyatā
viyonivikṛtākārā jāyante vikṛtair malaiḥ
māsi māsi rajaḥ strīṇāṃ rasajaṃ sravati tryaham
vatsarād dvādaśād ūrdhvaṃ yāti pañcāśataḥ kṣayam
pūrṇaṣoḍaśavarṣā strī pūrṇaviṃśena saṃgatā
śuddhe garbhāśaye mārge rakte śukre 'nile hṛdi
vīryavantaṃ sutaṃ sūte tato nyūnābdayoḥ punaḥ
rogyalpāyuradhanyo vā garbho bhavati naiva vā
vātādikuṇapagranthipūyakṣīṇamalāhvayam
bījāsamarthaṃ reto'sraṃ svaliṅgair doṣajaṃ vadet
raktena kuṇapaṃ śleṣmavātābhyāṃ granthisaṃnibham
pūyābhaṃ raktapittābhyāṃ kṣīṇaṃ mārutapittataḥ
kṛcchrāṇyetānyasādhyaṃ tu tridoṣaṃ mūtraviṭprabham
kuryād vātādibhir duṣṭe svauṣadhaṃ kuṇape punaḥ
dhātakīpuṣpakhadiradāḍimārjunasādhitam
pāyayet sarpirathavā vipakvam asanādibhiḥ
palāśabhasmāśmabhidā granthyābhe pūyaretasi
parūṣakavaṭādibhyāṃ kṣīṇe śukrakarī kriyā
saṃśuddho viṭprabhe sarpir hiṅgusevyādisādhitam
pibed granthyārtave pāṭhāvyoṣavṛkṣakajaṃ jalam
peyaṃ kuṇapapūyāsre candanaṃ vakṣyate tu yat
guhyaroge ca tat sarvaṃ kāryaṃ sottaravastikam
śukraṃ śuklaṃ guru snigdhaṃ madhuraṃ bahalaṃ bahu
ghṛtamākṣikatailābhaṃ sadgarbhāyārtavaṃ punaḥ
lākṣārasaśaśāsrābhaṃ dhautaṃ yacca virajyate
śuddhaśukrārtavaṃ svasthaṃ saṃraktaṃ mithunaṃ mithaḥ
snehaiḥ puṃsavanaiḥ snigdhaṃ śuddhaṃ śīlitabastikam
naraṃ viśeṣāt kṣīrājyair madhurauṣadhasaṃskṛtaiḥ
nārīṃ tailena māṣaiśca pittalaiḥ samupācaret
kṣāmaprasannavadanāṃ sphuracchroṇipayodharām
srastākṣikukṣiṃ puṃskāmāṃ vidyād ṛtumatīṃ striyam
padmaṃ saṃkocam āyāti dine 'tīte yathā tathā
ṛtāvatīte yoniḥ sā śukraṃ nātaḥ pratīcchati
māsenopacitaṃ raktaṃ dhamanībhyām ṛtau punaḥ
īṣatkṛṣṇaṃ vigandhaṃ ca vāyur yonimukhān nudet
tataḥ puṣpekṣaṇād eva kalyāṇadhyāyinī tryaham
mṛjālaṅkārarahitā darbhasaṃstaraśāyinī
kṣaireyaṃ yāvakaṃ stokaṃ koṣṭhaśodhanakarṣaṇam
parṇe śarāve haste vā bhuñjīta brahmacāriṇī
caturthe 'hni tataḥ snātā śuklamālyāmbarā śuciḥ
icchantī bhartṛsadṛśaṃ putraṃ paśyet puraḥ patim
ṛtus tu dvādaśa niśāḥ pūrvās tisro 'tra ninditāḥ
ekādaśī ca yugmāsu syāt putro 'nyāsu kanyakā
upādhyāyo 'tha putrīyaṃ kurvīta vidhivad vidhim
namaskāraparāyās tu śūdrāyā mantravarjitam
avandhya evaṃ saṃyogaḥ syād apatyaṃ ca kāmataḥ
santo hyāhurapatyārthaṃ dampatyoḥ saṃgatiṃ rahaḥ
durapatyaṃ kulāṅgāro gotre jātaṃ mahatyapi
icchetāṃ yādṛśaṃ putraṃ tadrūpacaritāṃśca tau
cintayetāṃ janapadāṃs tadācāraparicchadau
karmānte ca pumān sarpiḥkṣīraśālyodanāśitaḥ
prāg dakṣiṇena pādena śayyāṃ mauhūrtikājñayā
ārohet strī tu vāmena tasya dakṣiṇapārśvataḥ
tailamāṣottarāhārā tatra mantraṃ prayojayet
oṃ āhirasy āyurasi sarvataḥ pratiṣṭhāsi dhātā tvām
dadhātu vidhātā tvāṃ dadhātu brahmavarcasā bhaveti
brahmā bṛhaspatir viṣṇuḥ somaḥ sūryas tathāśvinau
bhago 'tha mitrāvaruṇau vīraṃ dadatu me sutam
sāntvayitvā tato 'nyonyaṃ saṃviśetāṃ mudānvitau
uttānā tanmanā yoṣit tiṣṭhed aṅgaiḥ susaṃsthitaiḥ
tathā hi bījaṃ gṛhṇāti doṣaiḥ svasthānam āsthitaiḥ
liṅgaṃ tu sadyogarbhāyā yonyā bījasya saṃgrahaḥ
tṛptir gurutvaṃ sphuraṇaṃ śukrāsrānanubandhanam
hṛdayaspandanaṃ tandrā tṛḍglānī romaharṣaṇam
avyaktaḥ prathame māsi saptāhāt kalalībhavet
garbhaḥ puṃsavanānyatra pūrvaṃ vyakteḥ prayojayet
balī puruṣakāro hi daivam apyativartate
puṣye puruṣakaṃ haimaṃ rājataṃ vāthavāyasam
kṛtvāgnivarṇaṃ nirvāpya kṣīre tasyāñjaliṃ pibet
gauradaṇḍam apāmārgaṃ jīvakarṣabhasairyakān
pibet puṣye jale piṣṭān ekadvitrisamastaśaḥ
kṣīreṇa śvetabṛhatīmūlaṃ nāsāpuṭe svayam
putrārthaṃ dakṣiṇe siñced vāme duhitṛvāñchayā
payasā lakṣmaṇāmūlaṃ putrotpādasthitipradam
nāsayāsyena vā pītaṃ vaṭaśuṅgāṣṭakaṃ tathā
oṣadhīr jīvanīyāśca bāhyāntarupayojayet
upacāraḥ priyahitair bhartrā bhṛtyaiśca garbhadhṛk
navanītaghṛtakṣīraiḥ sadā cainām upācaret
ativyavāyam āyāsaṃ bhāraṃ prāvaraṇaṃ guru
akālajāgarasvapnaṃ kaṭhinotkaṭakāsanam
śokakrodhabhayodvegavegaśraddhāvidhāraṇam
upavāsādhvatīkṣṇoṣṇaguruviṣṭambhibhojanam
raktaṃ nivasanaṃ śvabhrakūpekṣāṃ madyam āmiṣam
uttānaśayanaṃ yacca striyo necchanti tat tyajet
tathā raktasrutiṃ śuddhiṃ vastim ā māsato 'ṣṭamāt
ebhir garbhaḥ sraved āmaḥ kukṣau śuṣyen mriyeta vā
vātalaiśca bhaved garbhaḥ kubjāndhajaḍavāmanaḥ
pittalaiḥ khalatiḥ piṅgaḥ śvitrī pāṇḍuḥ kaphātmabhiḥ
vyādhīṃścāsyā mṛdusukhairatīkṣṇairauṣadhair jayet
dvitīye māsi kalalād ghanaḥ peśyathavārbudam
puṃstrīklībāḥ kramāt tebhyas tatra vyaktasya lakṣaṇam
kṣāmatā garimā kukṣer mūrchā chardirarocakaḥ
jṛmbhā prasekaḥ sadanaṃ romarājyāḥ prakāśanam
amleṣṭatā stanau pīnau sastanyau kṛṣṇacūcukau
pādaśopho vidāho 'nye śraddhāśca vividhātmikāḥ
mātṛjaṃ hyasya hṛdayaṃ mātuśca hṛdayena tat
sambaddhaṃ tena garbhiṇyā neṣṭaṃ śraddhāvimānanam
deyam apyahitaṃ tasyai hitopahitam alpakam
śraddhāvighātād garbhasya vikṛtiścyutireva vā
vyaktībhavati māse 'sya tṛtīye gātrapañcakam
mūrdhā dve sakthinī bāhū sarvasūkṣmāṅgajanma ca
samam eva hi mūrdhādyair jñānaṃ ca sukhaduḥkhayoḥ
garbhasya nābhau mātuśca hṛdi nāḍī nibadhyate
yayā sa puṣṭim āpnoti kedāra iva kulyayā
caturthe vyaktatāṅgānāṃ cetanāyāśca pañcame
ṣaṣṭhe snāyusirāromabalavarṇanakhatvacām
sarvaiḥ sarvāṅgasampūrṇo bhāvaiḥ puṣyati saptame
garbheṇotpīḍitā doṣās tasmin hṛdayam āśritāḥ
kaṇḍūṃ vidāhaṃ kurvanti garbhiṇyāḥ kikkisāni ca
navanītaṃ hitaṃ tatra kolāmbumadhurauṣadhaiḥ
siddham alpapaṭusnehaṃ laghu svādu ca bhojanam
candanośīrakalkena limped ūrustanodaram
śreṣṭhayā vaiṇahariṇaśaśaśoṇitayuktayā
aśvaghnapattrasiddhena tailenābhyajya mardayet
paṭolanimbamañjiṣṭhāsurasaiḥ secayet punaḥ
dārvīmadhukatoyena mṛjāṃ ca pariśīlayet
ojo 'ṣṭame saṃcarati mātāputrau muhuḥ kramāt
tena tau mlānamuditau tatra jāto na jīvati
śiśurojo'navasthānān nārī saṃśayitā bhavet
kṣīrapeyā ca peyātra saghṛtānvāsanaṃ ghṛtam
madhuraiḥ sādhitaṃ śuddhyai purāṇaśakṛtas tathā
śuṣkamūlakakolāmlakaṣāyeṇa praśasyate
śatāhvākalkito vastiḥ satailaghṛtasaindhavaḥ
tasmiṃs tvekāhayāte 'pi kālaḥ sūterataḥ param
varṣād vikārakārī syāt kukṣau vātena dhāritaḥ
śastaśca navame māsi snigdho māṃsarasaudanaḥ
bahusnehā yavāgūr vā pūrvoktaṃ cānuvāsanam
tata eva picuṃ cāsyā yonau nityaṃ nidhāpayet
vātaghnapattrabhaṅgāmbhaḥ śītaṃ snāne 'nvahaṃ hitam
niḥsnehāṅgī na navamān māsāt prabhṛti vāsayet
prāg dakṣiṇastanastanyā pūrvaṃ tatpārśvaceṣṭinī
puṃnāmadaurhṛdapraśnaratā puṃsvapnadarśinī
unnate dakṣiṇe kukṣau garbhe ca parimaṇḍale
putraṃ sūte 'nyathā kanyāṃ yā cecchati nṛsaṃgatim
nṛtyavāditragāndharvagandhamālyapriyā ca yā
klībaṃ tatsaṃkare tatra madhyaṃ kukṣeḥ samunnatam
yamau pārśvadvayonnāmāt kukṣau droṇyām iva sthite
prāk caiva navamān māsāt sā sūtigṛham āśrayet
deśe praśaste saṃbhāraiḥ sampannaṃ sādhake 'hani
tatrodīkṣeta sā sūtiṃ sūtikāparivāritā
adyaśvaḥprasave glāniḥ kukṣyakṣiślathatā klamaḥ
adhogurutvam aruciḥ praseko bahumūtratā
vedanorūdarakaṭīpṛṣṭhahṛdvastivaṅkṣaṇe
yonibhedarujātodasphuraṇasravaṇāni ca
āvīnām anu janmātas tato garbhodakasrutiḥ
athopasthitagarbhāṃ tāṃ kṛtakautukamaṅgalām
hastasthapuṃnāmaphalāṃ svabhyaktoṣṇāmbusecitām
pāyayet saghṛtāṃ peyāṃ tanau bhūśayane sthitām
ābhugnasakthim uttānām abhyaktāṅgīṃ punaḥ punaḥ
adho nābher vimṛdnīyāt kārayej jṛmbhacaṅkramam
garbhaḥ prayātyavāg evaṃ talliṅgaṃ hṛdvimokṣataḥ
āviśya jaṭharaṃ garbho vasterupari tiṣṭhati
āvyo 'bhitvarayantyenāṃ khaṭvām āropayet tataḥ
atha saṃpīḍite garbhe yonim asyāḥ prasārayet
mṛdupūrvaṃ pravāheta bāḍham ā prasavācca sā
harṣayet tāṃ muhuḥ putrajanmaśabdajalānilaiḥ
pratyāyānti tathā prāṇāḥ sūtikleśāvasāditāḥ
dhūpayed garbhasaṅge tu yoniṃ kṛṣṇāhikañcukaiḥ
hiraṇyapuṣpīmūlaṃ ca pāṇipādena dhārayet
suvarcalāṃ viśalyāṃ vā jarāyvapatane 'pi ca
kāryam etat tathotkṣipya bāhvorenāṃ vikampayet
kaṭīm ākoṭayet pārṣṇyā sphijau gāḍhaṃ nipīḍayet
tālukaṇṭhaṃ spṛśed veṇyā mūrdhni dadyāt snuhīpayaḥ
bhūrjalāṅgalikītumbīsarpatvakkuṣṭhasarṣapaiḥ
pṛthag dvābhyāṃ samastair vā yonilepanadhūpanam
kuṣṭhatālīśakalkaṃ vā surāmaṇḍena pāyayet
yūṣeṇa vā kulatthānāṃ bālbajenāsavena vā
śatāhvāsarṣapājājīśigrutīkṣṇakacitrakaiḥ
sahiṅgukuṣṭhamadanair mūtre kṣīre ca sārṣapam
tailaṃ siddhaṃ hitaṃ pāyau yonyāṃ vāpyanuvāsanam
śatapuṣpāvacākuṣṭhakaṇāsarṣapakalkitaḥ
nirūhaḥ pātayatyāśu sasnehalavaṇo 'parām
tatsaṅge hyanilo hetuḥ sā niryātyāśu tajjayāt
kuśalā pāṇināktena haret kﾱptanakhena vā
muktagarbhāparāṃ yoniṃ tailenāṅgaṃ ca mardayet
makkallākhye śirovastikoṣṭhaśūle tu pāyayet
sucūrṇitaṃ yavakṣāraṃ ghṛtenoṣṇajalena vā
dhānyāmbu vā guḍavyoṣatrijātakarajo'nvitam
atha bālopacāreṇa bālaṃ yoṣid upācaret
sūtikā kṣudvatī tailād ghṛtād vā mahatīṃ pibet
pañcakolakinīṃ mātrām anu coṣṇaṃ guḍodakam
vātaghnauṣadhatoyaṃ vā tathā vāyur na kupyati
viśudhyati ca duṣṭāsraṃ dvitrirātram ayaṃ kramaḥ
snehāyogyā tu niḥsneham amum eva vidhiṃ bhajet
pītavatyāśca jaṭharaṃ yamakāktaṃ viveṣṭayet
jīrṇe snātā pibet peyāṃ pūrvoktauṣadhasādhitām
tryahād ūrdhvaṃ vidāryādivargakvāthena sādhitā
hitā yavāgūḥ snehāḍhyā sātmyataḥ payasāthavā
saptarātrāt paraṃ cāsyai kramaśo bṛṃhaṇaṃ hitam
dvādaśāhe 'natikrānte piśitaṃ nopayojayet
yatnenopacaret sūtāṃ duḥsādhyo hi tadāmayaḥ
garbhavṛddhiprasavarukkledāsrasrutipīḍanaiḥ
evaṃ ca māsād adhyardhānmuktāhārādiyantraṇā
gatasūtābhidhānā syāt punarārtavadarśanāt
athāto garbhavyāpadaṃ śārīraṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
garbhiṇyāḥ parihāryāṇāṃ sevayā rogato 'thavā
puṣpe dṛṣṭe 'thavā śūle bāhyāntaḥ snigdhaśītalam
sevyāmbhojahimakṣīrivalkakalkājyalepitān
dhārayed yonivastibhyām ārdrārdrān picunaktakān
śatadhautaghṛtāktāṃ strīṃ tadambhasyavagāhayet
sasitākṣaudrakumudakamalotpalakesaram
lihyāt kṣīraghṛtaṃ khādecchṛṅgāṭakakaserukam
pibet kāntābjaśālūkabālodumbaravat payaḥ
śṛtena śālikākolīdvibalāmadhukekṣubhiḥ
payasā raktaśālyannam adyāt samadhuśarkaram
rasair vā jāṅgalaiḥ śuddhivarjaṃ cāsroktam ācaret
asaṃpūrṇatrimāsāyāḥ pratyākhyāya prasādhayet
āmānvaye ca tatreṣṭaṃ śītaṃ rūkṣopasaṃhitam
upavāso ghanośīraguḍūcyaraludhānyakāḥ
durālabhāparpaṭakacandanātiviṣābalāḥ
kvathitāḥ salile pānaṃ tṛṇadhānyāni bhojanam
mudgādiyūṣairāme tu jite snigdhādi pūrvavat
garbhe nipatite tīkṣṇaṃ madyaṃ sāmarthyataḥ pibet
garbhakoṣṭhaviśuddhyartham artivismaraṇāya ca
laghunā pañcamūlena rūkṣāṃ peyāṃ tataḥ pibet
peyām amadyapā kalke sādhitāṃ pāñcakaulike
bilvādipañcakakvāthe tiloddālakataṇḍulaiḥ
māsatulyadinānyevaṃ peyādiḥ patite kramaḥ
laghurasnehalavaṇo dīpanīyayuto hitaḥ
doṣadhātuparikledaśoṣārthaṃ vidhirityayam
snehānnavastayaścordhvaṃ balyadīpanajīvanāḥ
saṃjātasāre mahati garbhe yoniparisravāt
vṛddhim aprāpnuvan garbhaḥ koṣṭhe tiṣṭhati sasphuraḥ
upaviṣṭakam āhus taṃ vardhate tena nodaram
śokopavāsarūkṣādyairathavā yonyatisravāt
vāte kruddhe kṛśaḥ śuṣyed garbho nāgodaraṃ tu tam
udaraṃ vṛddham apyatra hīyate sphuraṇaṃ cirāt
tayor bṛṃhaṇavātaghnamadhuradravyasaṃskṛtaiḥ
ghṛtakṣīrarasais tṛptirāmagarbhāṃśca khādayet
taireva ca subhikṣāyāḥ kṣobhaṇaṃ yānavāhanaiḥ
līnākhye nisphure śyenagomatsyotkrośabarhijāḥ
rasā bahughṛtā deyā māṣamūlakajā api
bālabilvaṃ tilān māṣān saktūṃśca payasā pibet
samedyamāṃsaṃ madhu vā kaṭyabhyaṅgaṃ ca śīlayet
harṣayet satataṃ cainām evaṃ garbhaḥ pravardhate
puṣṭo 'nyathā varṣagaṇaiḥ kṛcchrāj jāyeta naiva vā
udāvartaṃ tu garbhiṇyāḥ snehairāśutarāṃ jayet
yogyaiśca vastibhir hanyāt sagarbhāṃ sa hi garbhiṇīm
garbhe 'tidoṣopacayād apathyair daivato 'pi vā
mṛte 'ntarudaraṃ śītaṃ stabdhaṃ dhmātaṃ bhṛśavyatham
garbhāspando bhramatṛṣṇā kṛcchrād ucchvasanaṃ klamaḥ
aratiḥ srastanetratvam āvīnām asamudbhavaḥ
tasyāḥ koṣṇāmbusiktāyāḥ piṣṭvā yoniṃ pralepayet
guḍaṃ kiṇvaṃ salavaṇaṃ tathāntaḥ pūrayen muhuḥ
ghṛtena kalkīkṛtayā śālmalyatasipicchayā
mantrair yogair jarāyūktair mūḍhagarbho na cet patet
athāpṛcchyeśvaraṃ vaidyo yatnenāśu tam āharet
hastam abhyajya yoniṃ ca sājyaśālmalipicchayā
hastena śakyaṃ tenaiva gātraṃ ca viṣamaṃ sthitam
āñchanotpīḍasaṃpīḍavikṣepotkṣepaṇādibhiḥ
ānulomya samākarṣed yoniṃ pratyārjavāgatam
hastapādaśirobhir yo yoniṃ bhugnaḥ prapadyate
pādena yonim ekena bhugno 'nyena gudaṃ ca yaḥ
viṣkambhau nāma tau mūḍhau śastradāraṇam arhataḥ
maṇḍalāṅguliśastrābhyāṃ tatra karma praśasyate
vṛddhipattraṃ hi tīkṣṇāgraṃ na yonāvavacārayet
pūrvaṃ śiraḥkapālāni dārayitvā viśodhayet
kakṣorastālucibukapradeśe 'nyatame tataḥ
samālambya dṛḍhaṃ karṣet kuśalo garbhaśaṅkunā
abhinnaśirasaṃ tvakṣikūṭayor gaṇḍayorapi
bāhuṃ chittvāṃsasaktasya vātādhmātodarasya tu
vidārya koṣṭham antrāṇi bahir vā saṃnirasya ca
kaṭīsaktasya tadvacca tatkapālāni dārayet
yad yad vāyuvaśād aṅgaṃ sajed garbhasya khaṇḍaśaḥ
tat tacchittvāharet samyag rakṣen nārīṃ ca yatnataḥ
garbhasya hi gatiṃ citrāṃ karoti viguṇo 'nilaḥ
tatrānalpamatis tasmād avasthāpekṣam ācaret
chindyād garbhaṃ na jīvantaṃ mātaraṃ sa hi mārayet
sahātmanā na copekṣyaḥ kṣaṇam apyastajīvitaḥ
yonisaṃvaraṇabhraṃśamakkallaśvāsapīḍitām
pūtyudgārāṃ himāṅgīṃ ca mūḍhagarbhāṃ parityajet
athāpatantīm aparāṃ pātayet pūrvavad bhiṣak
evaṃ nirhṛtaśalyāṃ tu siñced uṣṇena vāriṇā
dadyād abhyaktadehāyai yonau snehapicuṃ tataḥ
yonir mṛdur bhavet tena śūlaṃ cāsyāḥ praśāmyati
dīpyakātiviṣārāsnāhiṅgvelāpañcakolakāt
cūrṇaṃ snehena kalkaṃ vā kvāthaṃ vā pāyayet tataḥ
kaṭukātiviṣāpāṭhāśākatvagghiṅgutejinīḥ
tadvacca doṣasyandārthaṃ vedanopaśamāya ca
trirātram evaṃ saptāhaṃ sneham eva tataḥ pibet
sāyaṃ pibed ariṣṭaṃ ca tathā sukṛtam āsavam
śirīṣakakubhakvāthapicūn yonau vinikṣipet
upadravāśca ye 'nye syus tān yathāsvam upācaret
payo vātaharaiḥ siddhaṃ daśāhaṃ bhojane hitam
raso daśāhaṃ ca paraṃ laghupathyālpabhojanā
svedābhyaṅgaparā snehān balātailādikān bhajet
ūrdhvaṃ caturbhyo māsebhyaḥ sā krameṇa sukhāni ca
balāmūlakaṣāyasya bhāgāḥ ṣaṭ payasas tathā
yavakolakulatthānāṃ daśamūlasya caikataḥ
niḥkvāthabhāgo bhāgaśca tailasya tu caturdaśaḥ
dvimedādārumañjiṣṭhākākolīdvayacandanaiḥ
śārivākuṣṭhatagarajīvakarṣabhasaindhavaiḥ
kālānusāryāśaileyavacāgurupunarnavaiḥ
aśvagandhāvarīkṣīraśuklāyaṣṭīvarārasaiḥ
śatāhvāśūrpaparṇyelātvakpattraiḥ ślakṣṇakalkitaiḥ
pakvaṃ mṛdvagninā tailaṃ sarvavātavikārajit
sūtikābālamarmāsthihatakṣīṇeṣu pūjitam
jvaragulmagrahonmādamūtrāghātāntravṛddhijit
dhanvantarerabhimataṃ yonirogakṣayāpaham
vastidvāre vipannāyāḥ kukṣiḥ praspandate yadi
janmakāle tataḥ śīghraṃ pāṭayitvoddharecchiśum
madhukaṃ śākabījaṃ ca payasyā suradāru ca
aśmantakaḥ kṛṣṇatilās tāmravallī śatāvarī
vṛkṣādanī payasyā ca latā sotpalaśārivā
anantā śārivā rāsnā padmā ca madhuyaṣṭikā
bṛhatīdvayakāśmaryakṣīriśuṅgatvacā ghṛtam
pṛśniparṇī balā śigruḥ śvadaṃṣṭrā madhuparṇikā
śṛṅgāṭakaṃ bisaṃ drākṣā kaśeru madhukaṃ sitā
saptaitān payasā yogān ardhaślokasamāpanān
kramāt saptasu māseṣu garbhe sravati yojayet
kapitthabilvabṛhatīpaṭolekṣunidigdhikāt
mūlaiḥ śṛtaṃ prayuñjīta kṣīraṃ māse tathāṣṭame
navame śārivānantāpayasyāmadhuyaṣṭibhiḥ
yojayed daśame māsi siddhaṃ kṣīraṃ payasyayā
athavā yaṣṭimadhukanāgarāmaradārubhiḥ
avasthitaṃ lohitam aṅganāyā vātena garbhaṃ bruvate 'nabhijñāḥ
garbhākṛtitvāt kaṭukoṣṇatīkṣṇaiḥ srute punaḥ kevala eva rakte
garbhaṃ jaḍā bhūtahṛtaṃ vadanti mūrter na dṛṣṭaṃ haraṇaṃ yatas taiḥ
ojo'śanatvād athavāvyavasthair bhūtair upekṣyeta na garbhamātā
śiro 'ntarādhir dvau bāhū sakthinīti samāsataḥ
ṣaḍaṅgam aṅgaṃ pratyaṅgaṃ tasyākṣihṛdayādikam
śabdaḥ sparśaś ca rūpaṃ ca raso gandhaḥ kramād guṇāḥ
khānilāgnyabbhuvām ekaguṇavṛddhyanvayaḥ pare
tatra khāt khāni dehe 'smin śrotraṃ śabdo viviktatā
vātāt sparśatvagucchvāsā vahner dṛgrūpapaktayaḥ
āpyā jihvārasakledā ghrāṇagandhāsthi pārthivam
mṛdv atra mātṛjaṃ raktamāṃsamajjagudādikam
paitṛkaṃ tu sthiraṃ śukradhamanyasthikacādikam
caitanaṃ cittam akṣāṇi nānāyoniṣu janma ca
sātmyajaṃ tv āyur ārogyam anālasyaṃ prabhā balam
rasajaṃ vapuṣo janma vṛttir vṛddhir alolatā
sāttvikaṃ śaucam āstikyaṃ śukladharmarucir matiḥ
rājasaṃ bahubhāṣitvaṃ mānakruddambhamatsaram
tāmasaṃ bhayam ajñānaṃ nidrālasyaṃ viṣāditā
iti bhūtamayo dehas tatra sapta tvaco 'sṛjaḥ
pacyamānāt prajāyante kṣīrāt saṃtānikā iva
dhātvāśayāntarakledo vipakvaḥ svaṃ svam ūṣmaṇā
śleṣmasnāyvaparācchannaḥ kalākhyaḥ kāṣṭhasāravat
tāḥ sapta sapta cādhārā raktasyādyaḥ kramāt pare
kaphāmapittapakvānāṃ vāyor mūtrasya ca smṛtāḥ
garbhāśayo 'ṣṭamaḥ strīṇāṃ pittapakvāśayāntare
koṣṭhāṅgāni sthitāny eṣu hṛdayaṃ kloma phupphusam
yakṛtplīhoṇḍukaṃ vṛkkau nābhiḍimbāntravastayaḥ
daśa jīvitadhāmāni śirorasanabandhanam
kaṇṭho 'sraṃ hṛdayaṃ nābhir vastiḥ śukraujasī gudam
jālāni kaṇḍarāś cāṅge pṛthak ṣoḍaśa nirdiśet
ṣaṭ kūrcāḥ sapta sīvanyo meḍhrajihvāśirogatāḥ
śastreṇa tāḥ pariharec catasro māṃsarajjavaḥ
caturdaśāsthisaṃghātāḥ sīmantā dviguṇā nava
asthnāṃ śatāni ṣaṣṭiś ca trīṇi dantanakhaiḥ saha
dhanvantaris tu trīṇy āha saṃdhīnāṃ ca śatadvayam
daśottaraṃ sahasre dve nijagādātrinandanaḥ
snāvnāṃ navaśatī pañca puṃsāṃ peśīśatāni tu
adhikā viṃśatiḥ strīṇāṃ yonistanasamāśritāḥ
daśa mūlasirā hṛtsthās tāḥ sarvaṃ sarvato vapuḥ
rasātmakaṃ vahanty ojas tannibaddhaṃ hi ceṣṭitam
sthūlamūlāḥ susūkṣmāgrāḥ pattrarekhāpratānavat
bhidyante tās tataḥ saptaśatāny āsāṃ bhavanti tu
tatraikaikaṃ ca śākhāyāṃ śataṃ tasmin na vedhayet
sirāṃ jālaṃdharāṃ nāma tisraś cābhyantarāśritāḥ
ṣoḍaśadviguṇāḥ śroṇyāṃ tāsāṃ dve dve tu vaṅkṣaṇe
dve dve kaṭīkataruṇe śastreṇāṣṭau spṛśen na tāḥ
pārśvayoḥ ṣoḍaśaikaikām ūrdhvagāṃ varjayet tayoḥ
dvādaśadviguṇāḥ pṛṣṭhe pṛṣṭhavaṃśasya pārśvayoḥ
dve dve tatrordhvagāminyau na śastreṇa parāmṛśet
pṛṣṭhavaj jaṭhare tāsāṃ mehanasyopari sthite
romarājīm ubhayato dve dve śastreṇa na spṛśet
catvāriṃśad urasy āsāṃ caturdaśa na vedhayet
stanarohitatanmūlahṛdaye tu pṛthag dvayam
apastambhākhyayor ekāṃ tathāpālāpayor api
grīvāyāṃ pṛṣṭhavat tāsāṃ nīle manye kṛkāṭike
vidhure mātṛkāś cāṣṭau ṣoḍaśeti parityajet
hanvoḥ ṣoḍaśa tāsāṃ dve saṃdhibandhanakarmaṇī
jihvāyāṃ hanuvat tāsām adho dve rasabodhane
dve ca vācaḥpravartinyau nāsāyāṃ caturuttarā
viṃśatir gandhavedinyau tāsām ekāṃ ca tālugām
ṣaṭpañcāśan nayanayor nimeṣonmeṣakarmaṇī
dve dve apāṅgayor dve ca tāsāṃ ṣaḍ iti varjayet
nāsānetrāśritāḥ ṣaṣṭir lalāṭe sthapanīśritām
tatraikāṃ dve tathāvartau catasraś ca kacāntagāḥ
saptaivaṃ varjayet tāsāṃ karṇayoḥ ṣoḍaśātra tu
dve śabdabodhane śaṅkhau sirās tā eva cāśritāḥ
dve śaṅkhasaṃdhige tāsāṃ mūrdhni dvādaśa tatra tu
ekaikāṃ pṛthag utkṣepasīmantādhipatisthitām
ity avedhyavibhāgārthaṃ pratyaṅgaṃ varṇitāḥ sirāḥ
avedhyās tatra kārtsnyena dehe 'ṣṭānavatis tathā
saṃkīrṇā grathitāḥ kṣudrā vakrāḥ saṃdhiṣu cāśritāḥ
tāsāṃ śatānāṃ saptānāṃ pādo 'sraṃ vahate pṛthak
vātapittakaphair juṣṭaṃ śuddhaṃ caivaṃ sthitā malāḥ
śarīram anugṛhṇanti pīḍayanty anyathā punaḥ
tatra śyāvāruṇāḥ sūkṣmāḥ pūrṇariktāḥ kṣaṇāt sirāḥ
praspandinyaś ca vātāsraṃ vahante pittaśoṇitam
sparśoṣṇāḥ śīghravāhinyo nīlapītāḥ kaphaṃ punaḥ
gauryaḥ snigdhāḥ sthirāḥ śītāḥ saṃsṛṣṭaṃ liṅgasaṃkare
gūḍhāḥ samasthitāḥ snigdhā rohiṇyaḥ śuddhaśoṇitam
dhamanyo nābhisaṃbaddhā viṃśatiś caturuttarā
tābhiḥ parivṛtā nābhiś cakranābhir ivārakaiḥ
tābhiś cordhvam adhas tiryag deho 'yam anugṛhyate
srotāṃsi nāsike karṇau netre pāyvāsyamehanam
stanau raktapathaś ceti nārīṇām adhikaṃ trayam
jīvitāyatanāny antaḥ srotāṃsy āhus trayodaśa
prāṇadhātumalāmbho'nnavāhīny ahitasevanāt
tāni duṣṭāni rogāya viśuddhāni sukhāya ca
svadhātusamavarṇāni vṛttasthūlāny aṇūni ca
srotāṃsi dīrghāṇy ākṛtyā pratānasadṛśāni ca
āhāraś ca vihāraś ca yaḥ syād doṣaguṇaiḥ samaḥ
dhātubhir viguṇo yaś ca srotasāṃ sa pradūṣakaḥ
atipravṛttiḥ saṅgo vā sirāṇāṃ granthayo 'pi vā
vimārgato vā gamanaṃ srotasāṃ duṣṭilakṣaṇam
bisānām iva sūkṣmāṇi dūraṃ pravisṛtāni ca
dvārāṇi srotasāṃ dehe raso yair upacīyate
vyadhe tu srotasāṃ mohakampādhmānavamijvarāḥ
pralāpaśūlaviṇmūtrarodhā maraṇam eva vā
srotoviddham ato vaidyaḥ pratyākhyāya prasādhayet
uddhṛtya śalyaṃ yatnena sadyaḥkṣatavidhānataḥ
annasya paktā pittaṃ tu pācakākhyaṃ pureritam
doṣadhātumalādīnām ūṣmety ātreyaśāsanam
tadadhiṣṭhānam annasya grahaṇād grahaṇī matā
saiva dhanvantarimate kalā pittadharāhvayā
sthitā pakvāśayadvāri bhuktamārgārgaleva sā
bhuktam āmāśaye ruddhvā sā vipācya nayaty adhaḥ
balavaty abalā tv annam āmam eva vimuñcati
grahaṇyā balam agnir hi sa cāpi grahaṇībalaḥ
dūṣite 'gnāv ato duṣṭā grahaṇī rogakāriṇī
yad annaṃ dehadhātvojobalavarṇādipoṣaṇam
tatrāgnir hetur āhārān na hy apakvād rasādayaḥ
annaṃ kāle 'bhyavahṛtaṃ koṣṭhaṃ prāṇānilāhṛtam
dravair vibhinnasaṃghātaṃ nītaṃ snehena mārdavam
saṃdhukṣitaḥ samānena pacaty āmāśayasthitam
audaryo 'gnir yathā bāhyaḥ sthālīsthaṃ toyataṇḍulam
ādau ṣaḍrasam apy annaṃ madhurībhūtam īrayet
phenībhūtaṃ kaphaṃ yātaṃ vidāhād amlatāṃ tataḥ
pittam āmāśayāt kuryāc cyavamānaṃ cyutaṃ punaḥ
agninā śoṣitaṃ pakvaṃ piṇḍitaṃ kaṭu mārutam
bhaumāpyāgneyavāyavyāḥ pañcoṣmāṇaḥ sanābhasāḥ
pañcāhāraguṇān svān svān pārthivādīn pacanty anu
yathāsvaṃ te ca puṣṇanti pakvā bhūtaguṇān pṛthak
pārthivāḥ pārthivān eva śeṣāḥ śeṣāṃś ca dehagān
kiṭṭaṃ sāraś ca tat pakvam annaṃ sambhavati dvidhā
tatrācchaṃ kiṭṭam annasya mūtraṃ vidyād ghanam śakṛt
sāras tu saptabhir bhūyo yathāsvaṃ pacyate 'gnibhiḥ
rasād raktaṃ tato māṃsaṃ māṃsān medas tato 'sthi ca
asthno majjā tataḥ śukraṃ śukrād garbhaḥ prajāyate
kaphaḥ pittaṃ malāḥ kheṣu prasvedo nakharoma ca
sneho 'kṣitvagviṣām ojo dhātūnāṃ kramaśo malāḥ
prasādakiṭṭau dhātūnāṃ pākād evaṃ dvidharcchataḥ
parasparopasaṃstambhād dhātusnehaparamparā
kecid āhur ahorātrāt ṣaḍahād apare pare
māsena yāti śukratvam annaṃ pākakramādibhiḥ
saṃtatā bhojyadhātūnāṃ parivṛttis tu cakravat
vṛṣyādīni prabhāveṇa sadyaḥ śukrādi kurvate
prāyaḥ karoty ahorātrāt karmānyad api bheṣajam
vyānena rasadhātur hi vikṣepocitakarmaṇā
yugapat sarvato 'jasraṃ dehe vikṣipyate sadā
kṣipyamāṇaḥ khavaiguṇyād rasaḥ sajati yatra saḥ
tasmin vikāraṃ kurute khe varṣam iva toyadaḥ
doṣāṇām api caivaṃ syād ekadeśaprakopaṇam
annabhautikadhātvagnikarmeti paribhāṣitam
annasya paktā sarveṣāṃ paktṝṇām adhiko mataḥ
tanmūlās te hi tadvṛddhikṣayavṛddhikṣayātmakāḥ
tasmāt taṃ vidhivad yuktair annapānendhanair hitaiḥ
pālayet prayatas tasya sthitau hy āyurbalasthitiḥ
samaḥ samāne sthānasthe viṣamo 'gnir vimārgage
pittābhimūrchite tīkṣṇo mando 'smin kaphapīḍite
samo 'gnir viṣamas tīkṣṇo mandaś caivaṃ caturvidhaḥ
yaḥ pacet samyag evānnaṃ bhuktaṃ samyak samas tv asau
viṣamo 'samyag apy āśu samyag vāpi cirāt pacet
tīkṣṇo vahniḥ pacec chīghram asamyag api bhojanam
mandas tu samyag apy annam upayuktaṃ cirāt pacet
kṛtvāsyaśoṣāṭopāntrakūjanādhmānagauravam
sahajaṃ kālajaṃ yuktikṛtaṃ dehabalaṃ tridhā
tatra sattvaśarīrotthaṃ prākṛtaṃ sahajaṃ balam
vayaḥkṛtam ṛtūtthaṃ ca kālajaṃ yuktijaṃ punaḥ
vihārāhārajanitaṃ tathorjaskarayogajam
deśo 'lpavāridrunago jāṅgalaḥ svalparogadaḥ
ānūpo viparīto 'smāt samaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ smṛtaḥ
raso jalaṃ ca dehe 'sminn ekaikāñjalivardhitam
pṛthak svaprasṛtaṃ proktam ojomastiṣkaretasām
dvāv añjalī tu stanyasya catvāro rajasaḥ striyāḥ
samadhātor idaṃ mānaṃ vidyād vṛddhikṣayāv ataḥ
yaḥ syād doṣo 'dhikas tena prakṛtiḥ saptadhoditā
vibhutvād āśukāritvād balitvād anyakopanāt
svātantryād bahurogatvād doṣāṇāṃ prabalo 'nilaḥ
prāyo 'ta eva pavanādhyuṣitā manuṣyā doṣātmakāḥ sphuṭitadhūsarakeśagātrāḥ
śītadviṣaś caladhṛtismṛtibuddhiceṣṭāsauhārdadṛṣṭigatayo 'tibahupralāpāḥ
alpavittabalajīvitanidrāḥ sannasaktacalajarjaravācaḥ
nāstikā bahubhujaḥ savilāsā gītahāsamṛgayākalilolāḥ
