vastikarma tataḥ kuryāt svedādīṃścānilāpahān
rāsnājamodāsaraladevadārurajo'nvitam
bālo lihyād ghṛtaṃ tair vā vipakvaṃ sasitopalam
pittaduṣṭe 'mṛtābhīrupaṭolīnimbacandanam
dhātrī kumāraśca pibet kvāthayitvā saśārivam
athavā triphalāmustabhūnimbakaṭurohiṇīḥ
śārivādiṃ paṭolādiṃ padmakādiṃ tathā gaṇam
ghṛtānyebhiśca siddhāni pittaghnaṃ ca virecanam
śītāṃścābhyaṅgalepādīn yuñjyācchleṣmātmake punaḥ
yaṣṭyāhvasaindhavayutaṃ kumāraṃ pāyayed ghṛtam
sindhūtthapippalīmad vā piṣṭaiḥ kṣaudrayutairatha
rāṭhapuṣpaiḥ stanau limpecchiśośca daśanacchadau
sukham evaṃ vamed bālaḥ tīkṣṇair dhātrīṃ tu vāmayet
athācaritasaṃsargī mustādiṃ kvathitaṃ pibet
tadvat tagarapṛthvīkāsuradārukaliṅgakān
athavātiviṣāmustaṣaḍgranthāpañcakolakam
stanye tridoṣamaline durgandhyāmaṃ jalopamam
vibaddham acchaṃ vicchinnaṃ phenilaṃ copaveśyate
śakṛn nānāvyathāvarṇaṃ mūtraṃ pītaṃ sitaṃ ghanam
jvarārocakatṛṭchardiśuṣkodgāravijṛmbhikāḥ
aṅgabhaṅgo 'ṅgavikṣepaḥ kūjanaṃ vepathur bhramaḥ
ghrāṇākṣimukhapākādyā jāyante 'nye 'pi taṃ gadam
kṣīrālasakam ityāhuratyayaṃ cātidāruṇam
tatrāśu dhātrīṃ bālaṃ ca vamanenopapādayet
vihitāyāṃ ca saṃsargyāṃ vacādiṃ yojayed gaṇam
niśādiṃ vāthavā mādrīpāṭhātiktāghanāmayān
pāṭhāśuṇṭhyamṛtātiktatiktādevāhvaśārivāḥ
samustamūrvendrayavāḥ stanyadoṣaharāḥ param
anubandhe yathāvyādhi pratikurvīta kālavit
dantodbhedaśca rogāṇāṃ sarveṣām api kāraṇam
viśeṣājjvaraviḍbhedakāsacchardiśirorujām
abhiṣyandasya pothakyā visarpasya ca jāyate
pṛṣṭhabhaṅge biḍālānāṃ barhiṇāṃ ca śikhodbhave
dantodbhede ca bālānāṃ na hi kiṃcinna dūyate
yathādoṣaṃ yathārogaṃ yathodrekaṃ yathābhayam
vibhajya deśakālādīṃs tatra yojyaṃ bhiṣagjitam
ta eva doṣā dūṣyāśca jvarādyā vyādhayaśca yat
atas tad eva bhaiṣajyaṃ mātrā tvasya kanīyasī
saukumāryālpakāyatvāt sarvānnānupasevanāt
snigdhā eva sadā bālā ghṛtakṣīraniṣevaṇāt
sadyas tān vamanaṃ tasmāt pāyayen matimān mṛdu
stanyasya tṛptaṃ vamayet kṣīrakṣīrānnasevinam
pītavantaṃ tanuṃ peyām annādaṃ ghṛtasaṃyutām
vastiṃ sādhye virekeṇa marśena pratimarśanam
yuñjyād virecanādīṃs tu dhātryā eva yathoditān
mūrvāvyoṣavarākolajambūtvagdārusarṣapāḥ
sapāṭhā madhunā līḍhāḥ stanyadoṣaharāḥ param
dantapālīṃ samadhunā cūrṇena pratisārayet
pippalyā dhātakīpuṣpadhātrīphalakṛtena vā
lāvatittirivallūrarajaḥ puṣparasadrutam
drutaṃ karoti bālānāṃ dantakesaravan mukham
vacādvibṛhatīpāṭhākaṭukātiviṣāghanaiḥ
madhuraiśca ghṛtaṃ siddhaṃ siddhaṃ daśanajanmani
rajanīdārusaralaśreyasībṛhatīdvayam
pṛśniparṇī śatāhvā ca līḍhaṃ mākṣikasarpiṣā
grahaṇīdīpanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ mārutasyānulomanam
atīsārajvaraśvāsakāmalāpāṇḍukāsanut
bālasya sarvarogeṣu pūjitaṃ balavarṇadam
samaṅgādhātakīlodhrakuṭannaṭabalādvayaiḥ
mahāsahākṣudrasahāmudgabilvaśalāṭubhiḥ
sakārpāsīphalais toye sādhitaiḥ sādhitaṃ ghṛtam
kṣīramastuyutaṃ hanti śīghraṃ dantodbhavodbhavān
vividhān āmayān etad vṛddhakāśyapanirmitam
dantodbhaveṣu rogeṣu na bālam atiyantrayet
svayam apyupaśāmyanti jātadantasya yadgadāḥ
atyahaḥsvapnaśītāmbuślaiṣmikastanyasevinaḥ
śiśoḥ kaphena ruddheṣu srotaḥsu rasavāhiṣu
arocakaḥ pratiśyāyo jvaraḥ kāsaśca jāyate
kumāraḥ śuṣyati tataḥ snigdhaśuklamukhekṣaṇaḥ
saindhavavyoṣaśārṅgeṣṭāpāṭhāgirikadambakān
śuṣyato madhusarpirbhyām arucyādiṣu yojayet
aśokarohiṇīyuktaṃ pañcakolaṃ ca cūrṇitam
badarīdhātakīdhātrīcūrṇaṃ vā sarpiṣā drutam
sthirāvacādvibṛhatīkākolīpippalīnataiḥ
niculotpalavarṣābhūbhārgīmustaiśca kārṣikaiḥ
siddhaṃ prasthārdham ājyasya srotasāṃ śodhanaṃ param
siṃhyaśvagandhāsurasākaṇāgarbhaṃ ca tadguṇam
yaṣṭyāhvapippalīlodhrapadmakotpalacandanaiḥ
tālīśaśārivābhyāṃ ca sādhitaṃ śoṣajid ghṛtam
śṛṅgīmadhūlikābhārgīpippalīdevadārubhiḥ
aśvagandhādvikākolīrāsnarṣabhakajīvakaiḥ
śūrpaparṇīviḍaṅgaiśca kalkitaiḥ sādhitaṃ ghṛtam
śaśottamāṅganiryūhe śuṣyataḥ puṣṭikṛt param
vacāvayaḥsthātagarakāyasthācorakaiḥ śṛtam
bastamūtrasurābhyāṃ ca tailam abhyañjane hitam
lākṣārasasamaṃ tailaprasthaṃ mastu caturguṇam
aśvagandhāniśādārukauntīkuṣṭhābdacandanaiḥ
samūrvārohiṇīrāsnāśatāhvāmadhukaiḥ samaiḥ
siddhaṃ lākṣādikaṃ nāma tailam abhyañjanād idam
balyaṃ jvarakṣayonmādaśvāsāpasmāravātanut
yakṣarākṣasabhūtaghnaṃ garbhiṇīnāṃ ca śasyate
madhunātiviṣāśṛṅgīpippalīr lehayecchiśum
ekāṃ vātiviṣāṃ kāsajvaracchardirupadrutam
pītaṃ pītaṃ vamati yaḥ stanyaṃ taṃ madhusarpiṣā
dvivārtākīphalarasaṃ pañcakolaṃ ca lehayet
pippalīpañcalavaṇaṃ kṛmijitpāribhadrakam
tadvallihyāt tathā vyoṣaṃ maṣīṃ vā romacarmaṇām
lābhataḥ śalyakaśvāvidgodharkṣaśikhijanmanām
khadirārjunatālīśakuṣṭhacandanaje rase
sakṣīraṃ sādhitaṃ sarpir vamathuṃ viniyacchati
sadanto jāyate yas tu dantāḥ prāg yasya cottarāḥ
kurvīta tasminn utpāte śāntiṃ taṃ ca dvijātaye
dadyāt sadakṣiṇaṃ bālaṃ naigameṣaṃ ca pūjayet
tālumāṃse kaphaḥ kruddhaḥ kurute tālukaṇṭakam
tena tālupradeśasya nimnatā mūrdhni jāyate
tālupātaḥ stanadveṣaḥ kṛcchrāt pānaṃ śakṛddravam
tṛḍāsyakaṇḍvakṣirujā grīvādurdharatā vamiḥ
tatrotkṣipya yavakṣārakṣaudrābhyāṃ pratisārayet
tālu tadvat kaṇāśuṇṭhīgośakṛdrasasaindhavaiḥ
śṛṅgaveraniśābhṛṅgaṃ kalkitaṃ vaṭapallavaiḥ
baddhvā gośakṛtā liptam kukūle svedayet tataḥ
rasena limpet tālvāsyaṃ netre ca pariṣecayet
harītakīvacākuṣṭhakalkaṃ mākṣikasaṃyutam
pītvā kumāraḥ stanyena mucyate tālukaṇṭakāt
malopalepāt svedād vā gude raktakaphodbhavaḥ
tāmro vraṇo 'ntaḥ kaṇḍūmān jāyate bhūryupadravaḥ
kecit taṃ mātṛkādoṣaṃ vadantyanye 'hipūtanam
pṛṣṭhārur gudakuṭṭaṃ ca kecicca tam anāmikam
tatra dhātryāḥ payaḥ śodhyaṃ pittaśleṣmaharauṣadhaiḥ
śṛtaśītaṃ ca śītāmbuyuktam antarapānakam
sakṣaudratārkṣyaśailena vraṇaṃ tena ca lepayet
triphalābadarīplakṣatvakkvāthapariṣecitam
kāsīsarocanātutthamanohvālarasāñjanaiḥ
lepayed amlapiṣṭair vā cūrṇitair vāvacūrṇayet
suślakṣṇairathavā yaṣṭīśaṅkhasauvīrakāñjanaiḥ
śārivāśaṅkhanābhibhyām asanasya tvacāthavā
rāgakaṇḍūtkaṭe kuryād raktasrāvaṃ jalaukasā
sarvaṃ ca pittavraṇajicchasyate gudakuṭṭake
pāṭhāvelladvirajanīmustabhārgīpunarnavaiḥ
sabilvatryūṣaṇaiḥ sarpiḥ vṛścikālīyutaiḥ śṛtam
lihāno mātrayā rogair mucyate mṛttikodbhavaiḥ
vyādher yadyasya bhaiṣajyaṃ stanas tena pralepitaḥ
sthito muhūrtaṃ dhauto 'nu pītas taṃ taṃ jayed gadam
athāto bālagrahapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
purā guhasya rakṣārthaṃ nirmitāḥ śūlapāṇinā
manuṣyavigrahāḥ pañca sapta strīvigrahā grahāḥ
skando viśākho meṣākhyaḥ śvagrahaḥ pitṛsaṃjñitaḥ
śakuniḥ pūtanā śītapūtanādṛṣṭipūtanā
mukhamaṇḍitikā tadvad revatī śuṣkarevatī
teṣāṃ grahīṣyatāṃ rūpaṃ pratataṃ rodanaṃ jvaraḥ
sāmānyaṃ rūpam uttrāsajṛmbhābhrūkṣepadīnatāḥ
phenasrāvordhvadṛṣṭyoṣṭhadantadaṃśaprajāgarāḥ
rodanaṃ kūjanaṃ stanyavidveṣaḥ svaravaikṛtam
nakhairakasmāt paritaḥ svadhātryaṅgavilekhanam
tatraikanayanasrāvī śiro vikṣipate muhuḥ
hataikapakṣaḥ stabdhāṅgaḥ sasvedo natakandharaḥ
dantakhādī stanadveṣī trasyan roditi visvaram
vakravaktro vaman lālāṃ bhṛśam ūrdhvaṃ nirīkṣate
vasāsṛggandhirudvigno baddhamuṣṭiśakṛcchiśuḥ
calitaikākṣigaṇḍabhrūḥ saṃraktobhayalocanaḥ
skandārtas tena vaikalyaṃ maraṇaṃ vā bhaveddhruvam
saṃjñānāśo muhuḥ keśaluñcanaṃ kandharānatiḥ
vinamya jṛmbhamāṇasya śakṛnmūtrapravartanam
phenodvamanam ūrdhvekṣā hastabhrūpādanartanam
stanasvajihvāsaṃdaṃśasaṃrambhajvarajāgarāḥ
pūyaśoṇitagandhaśca skandāpasmāralakṣaṇam
ādhmānaṃ pāṇipādasya spandanaṃ phenanirvamaḥ
tṛṇmuṣṭibandhātīsārasvaradainyavivarṇatāḥ
kūjanaṃ stananaṃ chardiḥ kāsahidhmāprajāgarāḥ
oṣṭhadaṃśāṅgasaṃkocastambhabastābhagandhatāḥ
ūrdhvaṃ nirīkṣya hasanaṃ madhye vinamanaṃ jvaraḥ
mūrchaikanetraśophaśca naigameṣagrahākṛtiḥ
kampo hṛṣitaromatvaṃ svedaścakṣurnimīlanam
bahirāyāmanaṃ jihvādaṃśo 'ntaḥkaṇṭhakūjanam
dhāvanaṃ viṭsagandhatvaṃ krośanaṃ ca śvavacchuni
romaharṣo muhus trāsaḥ sahasā rodanaṃ jvaraḥ
kāsātīsāravamathujṛmbhātṛṭśavagandhatāḥ
aṅgeṣvākṣepavikṣepaśoṣastambhavivarṇatāḥ
muṣṭibandhaḥ srutiścākṣṇor bālasya syuḥ pitṛgrahe
srastāṅgatvam atīsāro jihvātālugale vraṇāḥ
sphoṭāḥ sadāharukpākāḥ saṃdhiṣu syuḥ punaḥ punaḥ
niśyahni pravilīyante pāko vaktre gude 'pi vā
bhayaṃ śakunigandhatvaṃ jvaraśca śakunigrahe
pūtanāyāṃ vamiḥ kampas tandrā rātrau prajāgaraḥ
hidhmādhmānaṃ śakṛdbhedaḥ pipāsā mūtranigrahaḥ
srastahṛṣṭāṅgaromatvaṃ kākavat pūtigandhitā
śītapūtanayā kampo rodanaṃ tiryagīkṣaṇam
tṛṣṇāntrakūjo 'tīsāro vasāvad visragandhatā
pārśvasyaikasya śītatvam uṣṇatvam aparasya ca
andhapūtanayā chardir jvaraḥ kāso 'lpanidratā
varcaso bhedavaivarṇyadaurgandhyānyaṅgaśoṣaṇam
dṛṣṭeḥ sādātirukkaṇḍūpothakījanmaśūnatāḥ
hidhmodvegastanadveṣavaivarṇyasvaratīkṣṇatāḥ
vepathur matsyagandhatvam athavā sāmlagandhatā
mukhamaṇḍitayā pāṇipādāsyaramaṇīyatā
sirābhirasitābhābhirācitodaratā jvaraḥ
arocako 'ṅgaglapanaṃ gomūtrasamagandhatā
revatyāṃ śyāvanīlatvaṃ karṇanāsākṣimardanam
kāsahidhmākṣivikṣepavakravaktratvaraktatāḥ
bastagandho jvaraḥ śoṣaḥ purīṣaṃ haritaṃ dravam
jāyate śuṣkarevatyāṃ kramāt sarvāṅgasaṃkṣayaḥ
keśaśāto 'nnavidveṣaḥ svaradainyaṃ vivarṇatā
nānāvarṇapurīṣatvam udare granthayaḥ sirāḥ
rodanaṃ gṛdhragandhatvaṃ dīrghakālānuvartanam
udare granthayo vṛttā yasya nānāvidhaṃ śakṛt
jihvāyā nimnatā madhye śyāvaṃ tālu ca taṃ tyajet
bhuñjāno 'nnaṃ bahuvidhaṃ yo bālaḥ parihīyate
tṛṣṇāgṛhītaḥ kṣāmākṣo hanti taṃ śuṣkarevatī
hiṃsāratyarcanākāṅkṣā grahagrahaṇakāraṇam
tatra hiṃsātmake bālo mahān vā srutanāsikaḥ
kṣatajihvaḥ kvaṇed bāḍham asukhī sāśrulocanaḥ
durvarṇo hīnavacanaḥ pūtigandhiśca jāyate
kṣāmo mūtrapurīṣaṃ svaṃ mṛdnāti na jugupsate
hastau codyamya saṃrabdho hantyātmānaṃ tathā param
tadvacca śastrakāṣṭhādyairagniṃ vā dīptam āviśet
apsu majjet patet kūpe kuryād anyacca tadvidham
tṛḍdāhamohān pūyasya chardanaṃ ca pravartayet
raktaṃ ca sarvamārgebhyo riṣṭotpattiṃ ca taṃ tyajet
rahaḥstrīratisaṃlāpagandhasragbhūṣaṇapriyaḥ
hṛṣṭaḥ śāntaśca duḥsādhyo ratikāmena pīḍitaḥ
dīnaḥ parimṛśan vaktraṃ śuṣkauṣṭhagalatālukaḥ
śaṅkitaṃ vīkṣate rauti dhyāyatyāyāti dīnatām
annam annābhilāṣe 'pi dattaṃ nāti bubhukṣate
gṛhītaṃ balikāmena taṃ vidyāt sukhasādhanam
hantukāmaṃ jayeddhomaiḥ siddhamantrapravartitaiḥ
itarau tu yathākāmaṃ ratibalyādidānataḥ
atha sādhyagrahaṃ bālaṃ vivikte śaraṇe sthitam
trirahnaḥ siktasaṃmṛṣṭe sadā saṃnihitānale
vikīrṇabhūtikusumapattrabījānnasarṣape
rakṣoghnatailajvalitapradīpahatapāpmani
vyavāyamadyapiśitanivṛttaparicārake
purāṇasarpiṣābhyaktaṃ pariṣiktaṃ sukhāmbunā
sādhitena balānimbavaijayantīnṛpadrumaiḥ
pāribhadrakakaṭvaṅgajambūvaruṇakaṭtṛṇaiḥ
kapotavaṅkāpāmārgapāṭalāmadhuśigrubhiḥ
kākajaṅghāmahāśvetākapitthakṣīripādapaiḥ
sakadambakarañjaiśca dhūpaṃ snātasya cācaret
dvīpivyāghrāhisiṃharkṣacarmabhir ghṛtamiśritaiḥ
pūtidaśāṅgasiddhārthavacābhallātadīpyakaiḥ
sakuṣṭhaiḥ saghṛtair dhūpaḥ sarvagrahavimokṣaṇaḥ
sarṣapā nimbapattrāṇi mūlam aśvakhurā vacā
bhūrjapattraṃ ghṛtaṃ dhūpaḥ sarvagrahanivāraṇaḥ
anantāmrāsthitagaraṃ maricaṃ madhuro gaṇaḥ
śṛgālavinnā mustā ca kalkitais tair ghṛtaṃ pacet
daśamūlarasakṣīrayuktaṃ tad grahajit param
rāsnādvyaṃśumatīvṛddhapañcamūlabalāghanāt
kvāthe sarpiḥ pacet piṣṭaiḥ śārivāvyoṣacitrakaiḥ
pāṭhāviḍaṅgamadhukapayasyāhiṅgudārubhiḥ
sagranthikaiḥ sendrayavaiḥ śiśos tat satataṃ hitam
sarvarogagrahaharaṃ dīpanaṃ balavarṇadam
śārivāsurabhibrāhmīśaṅkhinīkuṣṭhasarṣapaiḥ
vacāśvagandhāsurasayuktaiḥ sarpir vipācayet
tannāśayed grahān sarvān pānenābhyañjanena ca
gośṛṅgacarmavālāhinirmokaṃ vṛṣadaṃśaviṭ
nimbapattrājyakaṭukāmadanaṃ bṛhatīdvayam
kārpāsāsthiyavacchāgaromadevāhvasarṣapam
mayūrapattraśrīvāsaṃ tuṣakeśaṃ sarāmaṭham
mṛdbhāṇḍe bastamūtreṇa bhāvitaṃ ślakṣṇacūrṇitam
dhūpanaṃ ca hitaṃ sarvabhūteṣu viṣamajvare
ghṛtāni bhūtavidyāyāṃ vakṣyante yāni tāni ca
yuñjyāt tathā baliṃ homaṃ snapanaṃ mantratantravit
pūtikarañjatvakpattraṃ kṣīribhyo barbarād api
tumbīviśālāralukaśamībilvakapitthataḥ
utkvāthya toyaṃ tad rātrau bālānāṃ snapanaṃ śivam
anubandhān yathākṛcchraṃ grahāpāye 'pyupadravān
bālāmayaniṣedhoktabheṣajaiḥ samupācaret
athāto bhūtavijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
lakṣayej jñānavijñānavākceṣṭābalapauruṣam
puruṣe 'pauruṣaṃ yatra tatra bhūtagrahaṃ vadet
bhūtasya rūpaprakṛtibhāṣāgatyādiceṣṭitaiḥ
yasyānukāraṃ kurute tenāviṣṭaṃ tam ādiśet
so 'ṣṭādaśavidho devadānavādivibhedataḥ
hetus tadanuṣaktau tu sadyaḥ pūrvakṛto 'thavā
prajñāparādhaḥ sutarāṃ tena kāmādijanmanā
luptadharmavratācāraḥ pūjyān apy ativartate
taṃ tathā bhinnamaryādaṃ pāpam ātmopaghātinam
devādayo 'py anughnanti grahāś chidraprahāriṇaḥ
chidraṃ pāpakriyārambhaḥ pāko 'niṣṭasya karmaṇaḥ
ekasya śūnye 'vasthānaṃ śmaśānādiṣu vā niśi
digvāsastvaṃ guror nindā rater avidhisevanam
aśucer devatārcādi parasūtakasaṃkaraḥ
homamantrabalījyānāṃ viguṇaṃ parikarma ca
samāsād dinacaryādiproktācāravyatikramaḥ
gṛhṇanti śuklapratipattrayodaśyoḥ surā naram
śuklatrayodaśīkṛṣṇadvādaśyor dānavā grahāḥ
gandharvās tu caturdaśyāṃ dvādaśyāṃ coragāḥ punaḥ
pañcamyāṃ śuklasaptamyekādaśyos tu dhaneśvarāḥ
śuklāṣṭapañcamīpaurṇamāsīṣu brahmarākṣasāḥ
kṛṣṇe rakṣaḥpiśācādyā navadvādaśaparvasu
daśāmāvāsyayor aṣṭanavamyoḥ pitaro 'pare
guruvṛddhādayaḥ prāyaḥ kālaṃ saṃdhyāsu lakṣayet
phullapadmopamamukhaṃ saumyadṛṣṭim akopanam
alpavāksvedaviṇmūtraṃ bhojanānabhilāṣiṇam
devadvijātiparamaṃ śuciṃ saṃskṛtavādinam
mīlayantaṃ cirān netre surabhiṃ varadāyinam
śuklamālyāmbarasaricchailoccabhavanapriyam
anidram apradhṛṣyaṃ ca vidyād devavaśīkṛtam
jihmadṛṣṭiṃ durātmānaṃ gurudevadvijadviṣam
nirbhayaṃ māninaṃ śūraṃ krodhanaṃ vyavasāyinam
rudraḥ skando viśākho 'ham indro 'ham iti vādinam
surāmāṃsaruciṃ vidyād daityagrahagṛhītakam
svācāraṃ surabhiṃ hṛṣṭaṃ gītanartanakāriṇam
snānodyānaruciṃ raktavastramālyānulepanam
śṛṅgāralīlābhirataṃ gandharvādhyuṣitaṃ vadet
raktākṣaṃ krodhanaṃ stabdhadṛṣṭiṃ vakragatiṃ calam
śvasantam aniśaṃ jihvālolinaṃ sṛkkiṇīliham
priyadugdhaguḍasnānam adhovadanaśāyinam
uragādhiṣṭhitaṃ vidyāt trasyantaṃ cātapatrataḥ
viplutatrastaraktākṣaṃ śubhagandhaṃ sutejasam
priyanṛtyakathāgītasnānamālyānulepanam
matsyamāṃsaruciṃ hṛṣṭaṃ tuṣṭaṃ balinam avyatham
calitāgrakaraṃ kasmai kiṃ dadāmīti vādinam
rahasyabhāṣiṇaṃ vaidyadvijātiparibhāvinam
alparoṣaṃ drutagatiṃ vidyād yakṣagṛhītakam
hāsyanṛtyapriyaṃ raudraceṣṭaṃ chidraprahāriṇam
ākrośinaṃ śīghragatiṃ devadvijabhiṣagdviṣam
ātmānaṃ kāṣṭhaśastrādyair ghnantaṃ bhoḥśabdavādinam
śāstravedapaṭhaṃ vidyād gṛhītaṃ brahmarākṣasaiḥ
sakrodhadṛṣṭiṃ bhrūkuṭīm udvahantaṃ sasaṃbhramam
praharantaṃ pradhāvantaṃ śabdantaṃ bhairavānanam
annād vināpi balinaṃ naṣṭanidraṃ niśācaram
nirlajjam aśuciṃ śūraṃ krūraṃ paruṣabhāṣiṇam
roṣaṇaṃ raktamālyastrīraktamadyāmiṣapriyam
dṛṣṭvā ca raktaṃ māṃsaṃ vālihānaṃ daśanacchadau
hasantam annakāle ca rākṣasādhiṣṭhitaṃ vadet
asvasthacittaṃ naikatra tiṣṭhantaṃ paridhāvinam
ucchiṣṭanṛtyagandharvahāsamadyāmiṣapriyam
nirbhartsanād dīnamukhaṃ rudantam animittataḥ
nakhair likhantam ātmānaṃ rūkṣadhvastavapuḥsvaram
āvedayantam duḥkhādi sambaddhābaddhabhāṣiṇam
naṣṭasmṛtiṃ śūnyaratiṃ lolaṃ nagnaṃ malīmasam
rathyācailaparīdhānaṃ tṛṇamālāvibhūṣaṇam
ārohantaṃ ca kāṣṭhāśvaṃ tathā saṃkarakūṭakam
bahvāśinaṃ piśācena vijānīyād adhiṣṭhitam
pretākṛtikriyāgandhaṃ bhītam āhāravidviṣam
tṛṇacchidaṃ ca pretena gṛhītaṃ naram ādiśet
bahupralāpaṃ kṛṣṇāsyaṃ pravilambitayāyinam
śūnapralambavṛṣaṇaṃ kūṣmāṇḍādhiṣṭhitaṃ vadet
gṛhītvā kāṣṭhaloṣṭādi bhramantaṃ cīravāsasam
nagnaṃ dhāvantam uttrastadṛṣṭiṃ tṛṇavibhūṣaṇam
śmaśānaśūnyāyatanarathyaikadrumasevinam
tilānnamadyamāṃseṣu satataṃ saktalocanam
niṣādādhiṣṭhitaṃ vidyād vadantaṃ paruṣāṇi ca
yācantam udakaṃ cānnaṃ trastalohitalocanam
ugravākyaṃ ca jānīyān naram aukiraṇārditam
gandhamālyaratiṃ satyavādinaṃ parivepinam
bahunidraṃ ca jānīyād vetālena vaśīkṛtam
aprasannadṛśaṃ dīnavadanaṃ śuṣkatālukam
calannayanapakṣmāṇaṃ nidrāluṃ mandapāvakam
apasavyaparīdhānaṃ tilamāṃsaguḍapriyam
skhaladvācaṃ ca jānīyāt pitṛgrahavaśīkṛtam
guruvṛddharṣisiddhābhiśāpacintānurūpataḥ
vyāhārāhāraceṣṭābhir yathāsvaṃ tad grahaṃ vadet
kumāravṛndānugataṃ nagnam uddhatamūrdhajam
asvasthamanasaṃ dairghyakālikaṃ sagrahaṃ tyajet
athāto bhūtapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
bhūtaṃ jayed ahiṃsecchaṃ japahomabalivrataiḥ
tapaḥśīlasamādhānadānajñānadayādibhiḥ
hiṅguvyoṣālanepālīlaśunārkajaṭājaṭāḥ
ajalomī sagolomī bhūtakeśī vacā latā
kukkuṭī sarpagandhākhyā tilāḥ kāṇavikāṇike
vajraproktā vayaḥsthā ca śṛṅgī mohanavallyapi
srotojāñjanarakṣoghnaṃ rakṣoghnaṃ cānyad auṣadham
kharāśvaśvāviduṣṭrarkṣagodhānakulaśalyakāt
dvīpimārjāragosiṃhavyāghrasāmudrasattvataḥ
carmapittadvijanakhā varge 'smin sādhayed ghṛtam
purāṇam athavā tailaṃ navaṃ tat pānanasyayoḥ
abhyaṅge ca prayoktavyam eṣāṃ cūrṇaṃ ca dhūpane
ebhiśca guṭikāṃ yuñjyād añjane sāvapīḍane
pralepe kalkam eteṣāṃ kvāthaṃ ca pariṣecane
prayogo 'yaṃ grahonmādān sāpasmārāñchamaṃ nayet
gajāhvāpippalīmūlavyoṣāmalakasarṣapān
godhānakulamārjārajhaṣapittaprapeṣitān
nāvanābhyaṅgasekeṣu vidadhīta grahāpahān
siddhārthakavacāhiṅgupriyaṅgurajanīdvayam
mañjiṣṭhā śvetakaṭabhī varā śvetādrikarṇikā
nimbasya pattraṃ bījaṃ tu naktamālaśirīṣayoḥ
surāhvaṃ tryūṣaṇaṃ sarpir gomūtre taiścaturguṇe
siddhaṃ siddhārthakaṃ nāma pāne nasye ca yojitam
grahān sarvān nihantyāśu viśeṣād āsurān grahān
kṛtyālakṣmīviṣonmādajvarāpasmārapāpma ca
ebhirevauṣadhair bastavāriṇā kalpito 'gadaḥ
pānanasyāñjanālepasnānodgharṣaṇayojitaḥ
guṇaiḥ pūrvavad uddiṣṭo rājadvāre ca siddhikṛt
siddhārthakavyoṣavacāśvagandhā niśādvayaṃ hiṅgupalāṇḍukandaḥ
bījaṃ karañjāt kusumaṃ śirīṣāt phalaṃ ca valkaṃ ca kapitthavṛkṣāt
samāṇimanthaṃ sanataṃ sakuṣṭhaṃ śyoṇākamūlaṃ kiṇihī sitā ca
bastasya mūtreṇa subhāvitaṃ tat pittena gavyena guḍān vidadhyāt
duṣṭavraṇonmādatamoniśāndhān udbandhakān vārinimagnadehān
digdhāhatān darpitasarpadaṣṭāṃs te sādhayantyañjananasyalepaiḥ
kārpāsāsthimayūrapattrabṛhatīnirmālyapiṇḍītakatvaṅmāṃsīvṛṣadaṃśaviṭtuṣavacākeśāhinirmokakaiḥ
nāgendradvijaśṛṅgahiṅgumaricais tulyaiḥ kṛtaṃ dhūpanaṃ
skandonmādapiśācarākṣasasurāveśajvaraghnaṃ param
trikaṭukadalakuṅkumagranthikakṣārasiṃhīniśādārusiddhārthayugmāmbuśakrāhvayaiḥ
sitalaśunaphalatrayośīratiktāvacātutthayaṣṭībalālohitailāśilāpadmakaiḥ
dadhitagaramadhūkasārapriyāhvāviṣākhyāviṣātārkṣyaśailaiḥ sacavyāmayaiḥ kalkitaiḥ
ghṛtam anavam aśeṣamūtrāṃśasiddhaṃ mataṃ bhūtarāvāhvayaṃ pānatas tad grahaghnaṃ param
natamadhukakarañjalākṣāpaṭolīsamaṅgāvacāpāṭalīhiṅgusiddhārthasiṃhīniśāyuglatārohiṇī
gadaśukatarupuṣpabījograyaṣṭyadrikarṇīnikumbhāgnibilvaiḥ samaiḥ kalkitair mūtravargeṇa siddhaṃ ghṛtaṃ
vidhivinihitam āśu sarvaiḥ kramair yojitaṃ hanti sarvagrahonmādakuṣṭhajvarāṃs tan mahābhūtarāvaṃ smṛtam
grahā gṛhṇanti ye yeṣu teṣāṃ teṣu viśeṣataḥ
dineṣu balihomādīn prayuñjīta cikitsakaḥ
snānavastravasāmāṃsamadyakṣīraguḍādi ca
rocate yad yadā yebhyas tat teṣām āharet tadā
ratnāni gandhamālyāni bījāni madhusarpiṣī
bhakṣyāśca sarve sarveṣāṃ sāmānyo vidhirityayam
surarṣiguruvṛddhebhyaḥ siddhebhyaśca surālaye
diśyuttarasyāṃ tatrāpi devāyopahared balim
paścimāyāṃ yathākālaṃ daityabhūtāya catvare
gandharvāya gavāṃ mārge savastrābharaṇaṃ balim
pitṛnāgagrahe nadyāṃ nāgebhyaḥ pūrvadakṣiṇe
yakṣāya yakṣāyatane saritor vā samāgame
catuṣpathe rākṣasāya bhīmeṣu gahaneṣu ca
rakṣasāṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ tu pūrvasyāṃ brahmarakṣasām
śūnyālaye piśācāya paścimāṃ diśam āsthite
śuciśuklāni mālyāni gandhāḥ kṣaireyam odanam
dadhi chattraṃ ca dhavalaṃ devānāṃ baliriṣyate
hiṅgusarṣapaṣaḍgranthāvyoṣairardhapalonmitaiḥ
caturguṇe gavāṃ mūtre ghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet
tatpānanāvanābhyaṅgair devagrahavimokṣaṇam
nasyāñjanaṃ vacāhiṅgulaśunaṃ bastavāriṇā
daitye balir bahuphalaḥ sośīrakamalotpalaḥ
nāgānāṃ sumanolājaguḍāpūpaguḍaudanaiḥ
paramānnamadhukṣīrakṛṣṇamṛnnāgakesaraiḥ
vacāpadmapurośīraraktotpaladalair baliḥ
śvetapattraṃ ca lodhraṃ ca tagaraṃ nāgasarṣapāḥ
śītena vāriṇā piṣṭaṃ nāvanāñjanayor hitam
yakṣāṇāṃ kṣīradadhyājyamiśrakaudanaguggulu
devadārūtpalaṃ padmaṃ uśīraṃ vastrakāñcanam
hiraṇyaṃ ca balir yojyo mūtrājyakṣīram ekataḥ
siddhaṃ samonmitaṃ pānanāvanābhyañjane hitam
harītakī haridre dve laśuno maricaṃ vacā
nimbapattraṃ ca bastāmbukalkitaṃ nāvanāñjanam
brahmarakṣobaliḥ siddhaṃ yavānāṃ pūrṇam āḍhakam
toyasya kumbhaḥ palalaṃ chattraṃ vastram vilepanam
gāyatrīviṃśatipalakvāthe 'rdhapalikaiḥ pacet
tryūṣaṇatriphalāhiṅguṣaḍgranthāmiśisarṣapaiḥ
sanimbapattralaśunaiḥ kuḍavān sapta sarpiṣaḥ
gomūtre triguṇe pānanasyābhyaṅgeṣu taddhitam
rakṣasāṃ palalaṃ śuklaṃ kusumaṃ miśrakaudanam
baliḥ pakvāmamāṃsāni niṣpāvā rudhirokṣitāḥ
naktamālaśirīṣatvaṅmūlapuṣpaphalāni ca
tadvacca kṛṣṇapāṭalyā bilvamūlaṃ kaṭutrikam
hiṅgvindrayavasiddhārthalaśunāmalakīphalam
nāvanāñjanayor yojyo bastamūtrayuto 'gadaḥ
ebhireva ghṛtaṃ siddhaṃ gavāṃ mūtre caturguṇe
rakṣograhān vārayate pānābhyañjananāvanaiḥ
piśācānāṃ baliḥ sīdhuḥ piṇyākaḥ palalaṃ dadhi
mūlakaṃ lavaṇaṃ sarpiḥ sabhūtaudanayāvakam
haridrādvayamañjiṣṭhāmiśisaindhavanāgaram
hiṅgupriyaṅgutrikaṭulaśunatriphalā vacā
pāṭalīśvetakaṭabhīśirīṣakusumair ghṛtam
gomūtrapādikaṃ siddhaṃ pānābhyañjanayor hitam
bastāmbupiṣṭais taireva yojyam añjananāvanam
devarṣipitṛgandharve tīkṣṇaṃ nasyādi varjayet
sarpiḥpānādi mṛdvasmin bhaiṣajyam avacārayet
ṛte piśācāt sarveṣu pratikūlaṃ ca nācaret
savaidyam āturaṃ ghnanti kruddhās te hi mahaujasaḥ
īśvaraṃ dvādaśabhujaṃ nātham āryāvalokitam
sarvavyādhicikitsāṃ ca japan sarvagrahān jayet
tathonmādān apasmārān anyaṃ vā cittaviplavam
mahāvidyāṃ ca māyūrīṃ śuciṃ taṃ śrāvayet sadā
bhūteśaṃ pūjayet sthāṇuṃ pramathākhyāṃśca tadgaṇān
japan siddhāṃśca tanmantrān grahān sarvān apohati
yaccānantarayoḥ kiṃcid vakṣyate 'dhyāyayor hitam
yaccoktam iha tat sarvaṃ prayuñjīta parasparam
athāta unmādapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
unmādāḥ ṣaṭ pṛthagdoṣanicayādhiviṣodbhavāḥ
unmādo nāma manaso doṣairunmārgagair madaḥ
śārīramānasair duṣṭairahitād annapānataḥ
vikṛtāsātmyasamalād viṣamād upayogataḥ
viṣaṇṇasyālpasattvasya vyādhivegasamudgamāt
kṣīṇasya ceṣṭāvaiṣamyāt pūjyapūjāvyatikramāt
ādhibhiścittavibhraṃśād viṣeṇopaviṣeṇa ca
ebhir hi hīnasattvasya hṛdi doṣāḥ pradūṣitāḥ
dhiyo vidhāya kāluṣyaṃ hṛtvā mārgān manovahān
unmādaṃ kurvate tena dhīvijñānasmṛtibhramāt
deho duḥkhasukhabhraṣṭo bhraṣṭasārathivad rathaḥ
bhramatyacintitārambhas tatra vātāt kṛśāṅgatā
asthāne rodanākrośahasitasmitanartanam
gītavāditravāgaṅgavikṣepāsphoṭanāni ca
asāmnā veṇuvīṇādiśabdānukaraṇaṃ muhuḥ
āsyāt phenāgamo 'jasram aṭanaṃ bahubhāṣitā
alaṅkāro 'nalaṃkārairayānair gamanodyamaḥ
gṛddhirabhyavahāryeṣu tallābhe cāvamānatā
utpiṇḍitāruṇākṣitvaṃ jīrṇe cānne gadodbhavaḥ
pittāt saṃtarjanaṃ krodho muṣṭiloṣṭādyabhidravaḥ
śītacchāyodakākāṅkṣā nagnatvaṃ pītavarṇatā
asatyajvalanajvālātārakādīpadarśanam
kaphād arocakaśchardir alpehāhāravākyatā
strīkāmatā rahaḥprītir lālāsiṅghāṇakasrutiḥ
baibhatsyaṃ śaucavidveṣo nidrā śvayathurānane
unmādo balavān rātrau bhuktamātre ca jāyate
sarvāyatanasaṃsthānasaṃnipāte tadātmakam
unmādaṃ dāruṇaṃ vidyāt taṃ bhiṣak parivarjayet
dhanakāntādināśena duḥsahenābhiṣaṅgavān
pāṇḍur dīno muhur muhyan hāheti paridevate
rodityakasmān mriyate tadguṇān bahu manyate
śokakliṣṭamanā dhyāyañjāgarūko viceṣṭate
viṣeṇa śyāvavadano naṣṭacchāyābalendriyaḥ
vegāntare 'pi saṃbhrānto raktākṣas taṃ vivarjayet
athānilaja unmāde snehapānaṃ prayojayet
pūrvam āvṛtamārge tu sasnehaṃ mṛdu śodhanam
kaphapittabhave 'pyādau vamanaṃ savirecanam
snigdhasvinnasya vastiṃ ca śirasaḥ savirecanam
tathāsya śuddhadehasya prasādaṃ labhate manaḥ
ittham apyanuvṛttau tu tīkṣṇaṃ nāvanam añjanam
harṣaṇāśvāsanottrāsabhayatāḍanatarjanam
abhyaṅgodvartanālepadhūpān pānaṃ ca sarpiṣaḥ
yuñjyāt tāni hi śuddhasya nayanti prakṛtiṃ manaḥ
hiṅgusauvarcalavyoṣair dvipalāṃśair ghṛtāḍhakam
siddhaṃ samūtram unmādabhūtāpasmāranut param
dvau prasthau svarasād brāhmyā ghṛtaprasthaṃ ca sādhitam
vyoṣaśyāmātrivṛddantīśaṅkhapuṣpīnṛpadrumaiḥ
sasaptalākrimiharaiḥ kalkitairakṣasaṃmitaiḥ
palavṛddhyā prayuñjīta paraṃ mātrā catuḥpalam
unmādakuṣṭhāpasmāraharaṃ vandhyāsutapradam
vāksvarasmṛtimedhākṛddhanyaṃ brāhmīghṛtaṃ smṛtam
varāviśālābhadrailādevadārvelavālukaiḥ
dviśārivādvirajanīdvisthirāphalinīnataiḥ
bṛhatīkuṣṭhamañjiṣṭhānāgakesaradāḍimaiḥ
vellatālīśapattrailāmālatīmukulotpalaiḥ
sadantīpadmakahimaiḥ karṣāṃśaiḥ sarpiṣaḥ pacet
prasthaṃ bhūtagrahonmādakāsāpasmārapāpmasu
pāṇḍukaṇḍūviṣe śoṣe mohe mehe gare jvare
aretasyaprajasi vā daivopahatacetasi
amedhasi skhaladvāci smṛtikāme 'lpapāvake
balyaṃ maṅgalyam āyuṣyaṃ kāntisaubhāgyapuṣṭidam
kalyāṇakam idaṃ sarpiḥ śreṣṭhaṃ puṃsavaneṣu ca
ebhyo dviśārivādīni jale paktvaikaviṃśatim
rase tasmin pacet sarpir gṛṣṭikṣīracaturguṇam
vīrādvimedākākolīkapikacchūviṣāṇibhiḥ
śūrpaparṇīyutairetan mahākalyāṇakaṃ param
bṛṃhaṇaṃ saṃnipātaghnaṃ pūrvasmād adhikaṃ guṇaiḥ
jaṭilā pūtanā keśī cāraṭī markaṭī vacā
trāyamāṇā jayā vīrā corakaḥ kaṭurohiṇī
vayaḥsthā śūkarī chattrā sāticchattrā palaṅkaṣā
mahāpuruṣadantā ca kāyasthā nākulīdvayam
kaṭambharā vṛścikālī śāliparṇī ca tair ghṛtam
siddhaṃ cāturthikonmādagrahāpasmāranāśanam
mahāpaiśācakaṃ nāma ghṛtam etad yathāmṛtam
buddhimedhāsmṛtikaraṃ bālānāṃ cāṅgavardhanam
brāhmīm aindrīṃ viḍaṅgāni vyoṣaṃ hiṅgu jaṭāṃ murām
rāsnāṃ viṣaghnāṃ laśunaṃ viśalyāṃ surasāṃ vacām
jyotiṣmatīṃ nāgavinnām anantāṃ saharītakīm
kāṅkṣīṃ ca hastimūtreṇa piṣṭvā chāyāviśoṣitā
vartir nasyāñjanālepadhūpairunmādasūdanī
avapīḍāśca vividhāḥ sarṣapāḥ snehasaṃyutāḥ
kaṭutailena cābhyaṅgo dhmāpayeccāsya tad rajaḥ
sahiṅgus tīkṣṇadhūmaśca sūtrasthānodito hitaḥ
śṛgālaśalyakolūkajalaukāvṛṣabastajaiḥ
mūtrapittaśakṛdromanakhacarmabhirācaret
dhūpadhūmāñjanābhyaṅgapradehapariṣecanam
dhūpayet satataṃ cainaṃ śvagomatsyaiḥ supūtibhiḥ
vātaśleṣmātmake prāyaḥ paittike tu praśasyate
tiktakaṃ jīvanīyaṃ ca sarpiḥ snehaśca miśrakaḥ
śītāni cānnapānāni madhurāṇi laghūni ca
vidhyet sirāṃ yathoktāṃ vā tṛptaṃ medyāmiṣasya vā
nivāte śāyayed evaṃ mucyate mativibhramāt
prakṣipyāsalile kūpe śoṣayed vā bubhukṣayā
āśvāsayet suhṛt taṃ vā vākyair dharmārthasaṃhitaiḥ
brūyād iṣṭavināśaṃ vā darśayed adbhutāni vā
baddhaṃ sarṣapatailāktaṃ nyased vottānam ātape
kapikacchvāthavā taptair lohatailajalaiḥ spṛśet
kaśābhis tāḍayitvā vā baddhaṃ śvabhre viniṣkṣipet
athavā vītaśastrāśmajane saṃtamase gṛhe
sarpeṇoddhṛtadaṃṣṭreṇa dāntaiḥ siṃhair gajaiśca tam
athavā rājapuruṣā bahir nītvā susaṃyatam
bhāpayeyur vadhenainaṃ tarjayanto nṛpājñayā
dehaduḥkhabhayebhyo hi paraṃ prāṇabhayaṃ matam
tena yāti śamaṃ tasya sarvato viplutaṃ manaḥ
siddhā kriyā prayojyeyaṃ deśakālādyapekṣayā
iṣṭadravyavināśāt tu mano yasyopahanyate
tasya tatsadṛśaprāptisāntvāśvāsaiḥ śamaṃ nayet
kāmaśokabhayakrodhaharṣerṣyālobhasaṃbhavān
parasparapratidvaṃdvairebhireva śamaṃ nayet
bhūtānubandham īkṣeta proktaliṅgādhikākṛtim
yadyunmāde tataḥ kuryād bhūtanirdiṣṭam auṣadham
baliṃ ca dadyāt palalaṃ yāvakaṃ saktupiṇḍikām
snigdhaṃ madhuram āhāraṃ taṇḍulān rudhirokṣitān
pakvāmakāni māṃsāni surāṃ maireyam āsavam
atimuktasya puṣpāṇi jātyāḥ sahacarasya ca
catuṣpathe gavāṃ tīrthe nadīnāṃ saṃgameṣu ca
nivṛttāmiṣamadyo yo hitāśī prayataḥ śuciḥ
nijāgantubhirunmādaiḥ sattvavān na sa yujyate
prasāda indriyārthānāṃ buddhyātmamanasāṃ tathā
dhātūnāṃ prakṛtisthatvaṃ vigatonmādalakṣaṇam
athāto 'pasmārapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
smṛtyapāyo hyapasmāraḥ sa dhīsattvābhisamplavāt
jāyate 'bhihate citte cintāśokabhayādibhiḥ
unmādavat prakupitaiścittadehagatair malaiḥ
hate sattve hṛdi vyāpte saṃjñāvāhiṣu kheṣu ca
tamo viśan mūḍhamatir bībhatsāḥ kurute kriyāḥ
dantān khādan vaman phenaṃ hastau pādau ca vikṣipan
paśyann asanti rūpāṇi praskhalan patati kṣitau
vijihmākṣibhruvo doṣavege 'tīte vibudhyate
kālāntareṇa sa punaścaivam eva viceṣṭate
apasmāraścaturbhedo vātādyair nicayena ca
rūpam utpatsyamāne 'smin hṛtkampaḥ śūnyatā bhramaḥ
tamaso darśanaṃ dhyānaṃ bhrūvyudāso 'kṣivaikṛtam
aśabdaśravaṇaṃ svedo lālāsiṅghāṇakasrutiḥ
avipāko 'rucir mūrchā kukṣyāṭopo balakṣayaḥ
nidrānāśo 'ṅgamardas tṛṭ svapne gānaṃ sanartanam
pānaṃ tailasya madyasya tayoreva ca mehanam
tatra vātāt sphuratsakthiḥ prapataṃśca muhur muhuḥ
apasmarati saṃjñāṃ ca labhate visvaraṃ rudan
utpiṇḍitākṣaḥ śvasiti phenaṃ vamati kampate
āvidhyati śiro dantān daśatyādhmātakandharaḥ
parito vikṣipatyaṅgaṃ viṣamaṃ vinatāṅguliḥ
rūkṣaśyāvāruṇākṣitvaṅnakhāsyaḥ kṛṣṇam īkṣate
capalaṃ paruṣaṃ rūpaṃ virūpaṃ vikṛtānanam
apasmarati pittena muhuḥ saṃjñāṃ ca vindati
pītaphenākṣivaktratvag āsphālayati medinīm
bhairavādīptaruṣitarūpadarśī tṛṣānvitaḥ
kaphāccireṇa grahaṇaṃ cireṇaiva vibodhanam
ceṣṭālpā bhūyasī lālā śuklanetranakhāsyatā
śuklābharūpadarśitvaṃ sarvaliṅgaṃ tu varjayet
athāvṛtānāṃ dhīcittahṛtkhānāṃ prākprabodhanam
tīkṣṇaiḥ kuryād apasmāre karmabhir vamanādibhiḥ
vātikaṃ vastibhūyiṣṭhaiḥ paittaṃ prāyo virecanaiḥ
ślaiṣmikaṃ vamanaprāyairapasmāram upācaret
sarvataḥ suviśuddhasya samyag āśvāsitasya ca
apasmāravimokṣārthaṃ yogān saṃśamanāñchṛṇu
gomayasvarasakṣīradadhimūtraiḥ śṛtaṃ haviḥ
apasmārajvaronmādakāmalāntakaraṃ pibet
dvipañcamūlatriphalādviniśākuṭajatvacaḥ
saptaparṇam apāmārgaṃ nīlinīṃ kaṭurohiṇīm
śamyākapuṣkarajaṭāphalgumūladurālabhāḥ
dvipalāḥ saliladroṇe paktvā pādāvaśeṣite
bhārgīpāṭhāḍhakīkumbhanikumbhavyoṣarohiṣaiḥ
mūrvābhūtikabhūnimbaśreyasīśārivādvayaiḥ
madayantyagniniculairakṣāṃśaiḥ sarpiṣaḥ pacet
prasthaṃ tadvad dravaiḥ pūrvaiḥ pañcagavyam idaṃ mahat
jvarāpasmārajaṭharabhagandaraharaṃ param
śophārśaḥkāmalāpāṇḍugulmakāsagrahāpaham
brāhmīrasavacākuṣṭhaśaṅkhapuṣpīśṛtaṃ ghṛtam
purāṇaṃ medhyam unmādālakṣmyapasmārapāpmajit
tailaprasthaṃ ghṛtaprasthaṃ jīvanīyaiḥ palonmitaiḥ
kṣīradroṇe pacet siddham apasmāravimokṣaṇam
kaṃse kṣīrekṣurasayoḥ kāśmarye 'ṣṭaguṇe rase
kārṣikair jīvanīyaiśca sarpiḥprasthaṃ vipācayet
vātapittodbhavaṃ kṣipram apasmāraṃ nihanti tat
tadvat kāśavidārīkṣukuśakvāthaśṛtaṃ payaḥ
kūṣmāṇḍasvarase sarpir aṣṭādaśaguṇe śṛtam
yaṣṭīkalkam apasmāraharaṃ dhīvāksvarapradam
kapilānāṃ gavāṃ pittaṃ nāvane paramaṃ hitam
śvaśṛgālabiḍālānāṃ siṃhādīnāṃ ca pūjitam
godhānakulanāgānāṃ pṛṣatarkṣagavām api
pitteṣu sādhitaṃ tailaṃ nasye 'bhyaṅge ca śasyate
triphalāvyoṣapītadruyavakṣāraphaṇijjakaiḥ
śryāhvāpāmārgakārañjabījais tailaṃ vipācitam
bastamūtre hitaṃ nasyaṃ cūrṇaṃ vā dhmāpayed bhiṣak
nakulolūkamārjāragṛdhrakīṭāhikākajaiḥ
tuṇḍaiḥ pakṣaiḥ purīṣaiśca dhūpam asya prayojayet
śīlayet tailalaśunaṃ payasā vā śatāvarīm
brāhmīrasaṃ kuṣṭharasaṃ vacāṃ vā madhusaṃyutām
samaṃ kruddhairapasmāro doṣaiḥ śārīramānasaiḥ
yajjāyate yataścaiṣa mahāmarmasamāśrayaḥ
tasmād rasāyanairenaṃ duścikitsyam upācaret
tadārtaṃ cāgnitoyāder viṣamāt pālayet sadā
muktaṃ manovikāreṇa tvam itthaṃ kṛtavān iti
na brūyād viṣayairiṣṭaiḥ kliṣṭaṃ ceto 'sya bṛṃhayet
athāto vartmarogavijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
sarvaroganidānoktairahitaiḥ kupitā malāḥ
acakṣuṣyair viśeṣeṇa prāyaḥ pittānusāriṇaḥ
sirābhirūrdhvaṃ prasṛtā netrāvayavam āśritāḥ
vartma saṃdhiṃ sitaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ dṛṣṭiṃ vā sarvam akṣi vā
rogān kuryuścalas tatra prāpya vartmāśrayāḥ sirāḥ
suptotthitasya kurute vartmastambhaṃ savedanam
pāṃsupūrṇābhanetratvaṃ kṛcchronmīlanam aśru ca
vimardanāt syācca śamaḥ kṛcchronmīlaṃ vadanti tat
cālayan vartmanī vāyur nimeṣonmeṣaṇaṃ muhuḥ
karotyaruṅ nimeṣo 'sau vartma yat tu nimīlyate
vimuktasaṃdhi niśceṣṭaṃ hīnaṃ vātahataṃ hi tat
kṛṣṇāḥ pittena bahvyo 'ntarvartma kumbhīkabījavat
ādhmāyante punar bhinnāḥ piṭikāḥ kumbhisaṃjñitāḥ
sadāhakledanistodaṃ raktābhaṃ sparśanākṣamam
pittena jāyate vartma pittotkliṣṭam uśanti tat
karoti kaṇḍūṃ dāhaṃ ca pittaṃ pakṣmāntam āsthitam
pakṣmaṇāṃ śātanaṃ cānu pakṣmaśātaṃ vadanti tam
pothakyaḥ piṭikāḥ śvetāḥ sarṣapābhā ghanāḥ kaphāt
śophopadeharukkaṇḍūpicchilāśrusamanvitāḥ
kaphotkliṣṭaṃ bhaved vartma stambhakledopadehavat
granthiḥ pāṇḍurarukpākaḥ kaṇḍūmān kaṭhinaḥ kaphāt
kolamātraḥ sa lagaṇaḥ kiṃcid alpas tato 'thavā
raktā raktena piṭikā tattulyapiṭikācitā
utsaṅgākhyā tathotkliṣṭaṃ rājīmat sparśanākṣamam
arśo 'dhimāṃsaṃ vartmāntaḥ stabdhaṃ snigdhaṃ sadāharuk
raktaṃ raktena tatsrāvi chinnaṃ chinnaṃ ca vardhate
madhye vā vartmano 'nte vā kaṇḍūṣārugvatī sthirā
mudgamātrāsṛjā tāmrā piṭikāñjananāmikā
doṣair vartma bahiḥ śūnaṃ yad antaḥ sūkṣmakhācitam
sasrāvam antarudakaṃ bisābhaṃ bisavartma tat
yad vartmotkliṣṭam utkliṣṭam akasmān mlānatām iyāt
raktadoṣatrayotkleśād bhavatyutkliṣṭavartma tat
śyāvavartma malaiḥ sāsraiḥ śyāvaṃ rukkledaśophavat
śliṣṭākhyaṃ vartmanī śliṣṭe kaṇḍūśvayathurāgiṇī
vartmano 'ntaḥ kharā rūkṣāḥ piṭikāḥ sikatopamāḥ
sikatāvartma kṛṣṇaṃ tu kardamaṃ kardamopamam
bahalaṃ bahalair māṃsaiḥ savarṇaiścīyate samaiḥ
kukūṇakaḥ śiśoreva dantotpattinimittajaḥ
syāt tena śiśurucchūnatāmrākṣo vīkṣaṇākṣamaḥ
savartmaśūlapaicchilyaḥ karṇanāsākṣimardanaḥ
pakṣmoparodhe saṃkoco vartmanāṃ jāyate tathā
kharatāntarmukhatvaṃ ca romṇām anyāni vā punaḥ
kaṇṭakairiva tīkṣṇāgrair ghṛṣṭaṃ tairakṣi śūyate
uṣyate cānilādidviḍ alpāhaḥ śāntiruddhṛtaiḥ
kanīnake bahirvartma kaṭhino granthirunnataḥ
tāmraḥ pakvo 'srapūyasrud alajyādhmāyate muhuḥ
vartmāntar māṃsapiṇḍābhaḥ śvayathur grathito 'rujaḥ
sāsraiḥ syād arbudo doṣair viṣamo bāhyataścalaḥ
caturviṃśatirityete vyādhayo vartmasaṃśrayāḥ
ādyo 'tra bheṣajaiḥ sādhyo dvau tato 'rśaśca varjayet
pakṣmoparodho yāpyaḥ syāccheṣāñchastreṇa sādhayet
kuṭṭayet pakṣmasadanaṃ chindyāt teṣvapi cārbudam
bhindyāllagaṇakumbhīkābisotsaṅgāñjanālajīḥ
pothakīśyāvasikatāśliṣṭotkliṣṭacatuṣṭayam
sakardamaṃ sabahalaṃ vilikhet sakukūṇakam
athāto vartmarogapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
kṛcchronmīle purāṇājyaṃ drākṣākalkāmbusādhitam
sasitaṃ yojayet snigdhaṃ nasyadhūmāñjanādi ca
kumbhīkāvartma likhitaṃ saindhavapratisāritam
yaṣṭīdhātrīpaṭolīnāṃ kvāthena pariṣecayet
nivāte 'dhiṣṭhitasyāptaiḥ śuddhasyottānaśāyinaḥ
bahiḥ koṣṇāmbutaptena sveditaṃ vartma vāsasā
nirbhujya vastrāntaritaṃ vāmāṅguṣṭhāṅgulīghṛtam
na sraṃsate calati vā vartmaivaṃ sarvatas tataḥ
maṇḍalāgreṇa tat tiryak kṛtvā śastrapadāṅkitam
likhet tenaiva pattrair vā śākaśephālikādijaiḥ
phenena toyarāśer vā picunā pramṛjann asṛk
sthite rakte sulikhitaṃ sakṣaudraiḥ pratisārayet
yathāsvam uktairanu ca prakṣālyoṣṇena vāriṇā
ghṛtena siktam abhyaktaṃ badhnīyān madhusarpiṣā
ūrdhvādhaḥ karṇayor dattvā piṇḍīṃ ca yavasaktubhiḥ
dvitīye 'hani muktasya pariṣekaṃ yathāyatham
kuryāccaturthe nasyādīn muñced evāhni pañcame
samaṃ nakhanibhaṃ śophakaṇḍūgharṣādyapīḍitam
vidyāt sulikhitaṃ vartma likhed bhūyo viparyaye
rukpakṣmavartmasadanasraṃsanānyatilekhanāt
snehasvedādikas tasminn iṣṭo vātaharaḥ kramaḥ
abhyajya navanītena śvetalodhraṃ pralepayet
eraṇḍamūlakalkena puṭapāke pacet tataḥ
svinnaṃ prakṣālitaṃ śuṣkaṃ cūrṇitaṃ poṭalīkṛtam
striyāḥ kṣīre chagalyā vā mṛditaṃ netrasecanam
śālitaṇḍulakalkena liptaṃ tadvat pariṣkṛtam
kuryān netre 'tilikhite mṛditaṃ dadhimastunā
kevalenāpi vā sekaṃ mastunā jāṅgalāśinaḥ
piṭikā vrīhivaktreṇa bhittvā tu kaṭhinonnatāḥ
niṣpīḍayed anu vidhiḥ pariśeṣas tu pūrvavat
lekhane bhedane cāyaṃ kramaḥ sarvatra vartmani
pittāsrotkliṣṭayoḥ svāduskandhasiddhena sarpiṣā
sirāvimokṣaḥ snigdhasya trivṛcchreṣṭhaṃ virecanam
likhite srutarakte ca vartmani kṣālanaṃ hitam
yaṣṭīkaṣāyaḥ sekas tu kṣīraṃ candanasādhitam
pakṣmaṇāṃ sadane sūcyā romakūpān vikuṭṭayet
grāhayed vā jalaukobhiḥ payasekṣurasena vā
vamanaṃ nāvanaṃ sarpiḥ śṛtaṃ madhuraśītalaiḥ
saṃcūrṇya puṣpakāsīsaṃ bhāvayet surasārasaiḥ
tāmre daśāhaṃ paramaṃ pakṣmaśāte tad añjanam
pothakīr likhitāḥ śuṇṭhīsaindhavapratisāritāḥ
uṣṇāmbukṣālitāḥ siñcet khadirāḍhakiśigrubhiḥ
apsiddhair dviniśāśreṣṭhāmadhukair vā samākṣikaiḥ
kaphotkliṣṭe vilikhite sakṣaudraiḥ pratisāraṇam
sūkṣmaiḥ saindhavakāsīsamanohvākaṇatārkṣyajaiḥ
vamanāñjananasyādi sarvaṃ ca kaphajiddhitam
kartavyaṃ lagaṇe 'pyetad aśāntāvagninā dahet
kukūṇe khadiraśreṣṭhānimbapattraśṛtaṃ ghṛtam
pītvā dhātrī vamet kṛṣṇāyaṣṭīsarṣapasaindhavaiḥ
abhayāpippalīdrākṣākvāthenaināṃ virecayet
mustādvirajanīkṛṣṇākalkenālepayet stanau
dhūpayet sarṣapaiḥ sājyaiḥ śuddhāṃ kvāthaṃ ca pāyayet
paṭolamustamṛdvīkāguḍūcītriphalodbhavam
śiśos tu likhitaṃ vartma srutāsṛg vāmbujanmabhiḥ
dhātryaśmantakajambūtthapattrakvāthena secayet
prāyaḥ kṣīraghṛtāśitvād bālānāṃ śleṣmajā gadāḥ
tasmād vamanam evāgre sarvavyādhiṣu pūjitam
sindhūtthakṛṣṇāpāmārgabījājyastanyamākṣikam
cūrṇo vacāyāḥ sakṣaudro madanaṃ madhukānvitam
kṣīraṃ kṣīrānnam annaṃ ca bhajataḥ kramataḥ śiśoḥ
vamanaṃ sarvarogeṣu viśeṣeṇa kukūṇake
saptalārasasiddhājyaṃ yojyaṃ cobhayaśodhanam
dviniśālodhrayaṣṭyāhvarohiṇīnimbapallavaiḥ
kukūṇake hitā vartiḥ piṣṭais tāmrarajo'nvitaiḥ
kṣīrakṣaudraghṛtopetaṃ dagdhaṃ vā lohajaṃ rajaḥ
elālaśunakatakaśaṅkhoṣaṇaphaṇijjakaiḥ
vartiḥ kukūṇapothakyoḥ surāpiṣṭaiḥ sakaṭphalaiḥ
pakṣmarodhe pravṛddheṣu śuddhadehasya romasu
utsṛjya dvau bhruvo 'dhastād bhāgau bhāgaṃ ca pakṣmataḥ
yavamātraṃ yavākāraṃ tiryak chittvārdravāsasā
apaneyam asṛk tasminn alpībhavati śoṇite
sīvyet kuṭilayā sūcyā mudgamātrāntaraiḥ padaiḥ
baddhvā lalāṭe paṭṭaṃ ca tatra sīvanasūtrakam
nātigāḍhaślathaṃ sūcyā nikṣiped atha yojayet
madhusarpiḥkavalikāṃ na cāsmin bandham ācaret
nyagrodhādikaṣāyaiśca sakṣīraiḥ secayed ruji
pañcame divase sūtram apanīyāvacūrṇayet
gairikeṇa vraṇaṃ yuñjyāt tīkṣṇaṃ nasyāñjanādi ca
dahed aśāntau nirbhujya vartmadoṣāśrayāṃ valīm
saṃdaṃśenādhikaṃ pakṣma hṛtvā tasyāśrayaṃ dahet
sūcyagreṇāgnivarṇena dāho bāhyālajeḥ punaḥ
bhinnasya kṣāravahnibhyāṃ succhinnasyārbudasya ca
athātaḥ saṃdhisitāsitarogavijñānīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
vāyuḥ kruddhaḥ sirāḥ prāpya jalābhaṃ jalavāhinīḥ
aśru srāvayate vartmaśuklasaṃdheḥ kanīnakāt
tena netraṃ sarugrāgaśophaṃ syāt sa jalāsravaḥ
kaphāt kaphāsrave śvetaṃ picchilaṃ bahalaṃ sravet
kaphena śophas tīkṣṇāgraḥ kṣārabudbudakopamaḥ
pṛthumūlabalaḥ snigdhaḥ savarṇo mṛdupicchilaḥ
mahān apākaḥ kaṇḍūmān upanāhaḥ sa nīrujaḥ
raktād raktāsrāve tāmraṃ bahūṣṇaṃ cāśru saṃsravet
vartmasaṃdhyāśrayā śukle piṭikā dāhaśūlinī
tāmrā mudgopamā bhinnā raktaṃ sravati parvaṇī
pūyāsrave malāḥ sāsrā vartmasaṃdheḥ kanīnakāt
srāvayanti muhuḥ pūyaṃ sāsraṃ tvaṅmāṃsapākataḥ
pūyālaso vraṇaḥ sūkṣmaḥ śophasaṃrambhapūrvakaḥ
kanīnasaṃdhāvādhmāyī pūyāsrāvī savedanaḥ
kanīnasyāntaralajī śopho ruktodadāhavān
apāṅge vā kanīne vā kaṇḍūṣāpakṣmapoṭavān
pūyāsrāvī kṛmigranthir granthiḥ kṛmiyuto 'rtimān
upanāhakṛmigranthipūyālasakaparvaṇīḥ
śastreṇa sādhayet pañca sālajīn āsravāṃs tyajet
pittaṃ kuryāt site bindūn asitaśyāvapītakān
malāktādarśatulyaṃ vā sarvaṃ śuklaṃ sadāharuk
rogo 'yaṃ śuktikāsaṃjñaḥ saśakṛdbhedatṛḍjvaraḥ
kaphācchukle samaṃ śvetaṃ ciravṛddhyadhimāṃsakam
śuklārma śophas tvarujaḥ savarṇo bahalo 'mṛduḥ
guruḥ snigdho 'mbubindvābho balāsagrathitaṃ smṛtaṃ
bindubhiḥ piṣṭadhavalairutsannaiḥ piṣṭakaṃ vadet
raktarājītataṃ śuklam uṣyate yat savedanam
aśophāśrūpadehaṃ ca sirotpātaḥ sa śoṇitāt
upekṣitaḥ sirotpāto rājīs tā eva vardhayan
kuryāt sāsraṃ sirāharṣaṃ tenākṣyudvīkṣaṇākṣamam
sirājāle sirājālaṃ bṛhad raktaṃ ghanonnatam
śoṇitārma samaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ padmābham adhimāṃsakam
nīruk ślakṣṇo 'rjunaṃ binduḥ śaśalohitalohitaḥ
mṛdvāśuvṛddhyaruṅmāṃsaṃ prastāri śyāvalohitam
prastāryarma malaiḥ sāsraiḥ snāvārma snāvasaṃnibham
śuṣkāsṛkpiṇḍavacchyāvaṃ yan māṃsaṃ bahalaṃ pṛthu
adhimāṃsārma tad dāhagharṣavatyaḥ sirāvṛtāḥ
kṛṣṇāsannāḥ sirāsaṃjñāḥ piṭikāḥ sarṣapopamāḥ
śuktiharṣasirotpātapiṣṭakagrathitārjunam
sādhayed auṣadhaiḥ ṣaṭkaṃ śeṣaṃ śastreṇa saptakam
navotthaṃ tad api dravyairarmoktaṃ yacca pañcadhā
tacchedyam asitaprāptaṃ māṃsasnāvasirāvṛtam
carmoddālavad ucchrāyi dṛṣṭiprāptaṃ ca varjayet
pittaṃ kṛṣṇe 'thavā dṛṣṭau śukraṃ todāśrurāgavat
chittvā tvacaṃ janayati tena syāt kṛṣṇamaṇḍalam
pakvajambūnibhaṃ kiṃcin nimnaṃ ca kṣataśukrakam
tat kṛcchrasādhyaṃ yāpyaṃ tu dvitīyapaṭalavyadhāt
tatra todādibāhulyaṃ sūcīviddhābhakṛṣṇatā
tṛtīyapaṭalacchedād asādhyaṃ nicitaṃ vraṇaiḥ
śaṅkhaśuklaṃ kaphāt sādhyaṃ nātiruk śuddhaśukrakam
ātāmrapicchilāsrasrud ātāmrapiṭikātiruk
ajāviṭsadṛśocchrāyakārṣṇyā varjyāsṛjājakā
sirāśukraṃ malaiḥ sāsrais tajjuṣṭaṃ kṛṣṇamaṇḍalam
satodadāhatāmrābhiḥ sirābhiravatanyate
animittoṣṇaśītācchaghanāsrasrucca tat tyajet
doṣaiḥ sāsraiḥ sakṛt kṛṣṇaṃ nīyate śuklarūpatām
dhavalābhropaliptābhaṃ niṣpāvārdhadalākṛti
atitīvrarujārāgadāhaśvayathupīḍitam
pākātyayena tacchukraṃ varjayet tīvravedanam
yasya vā liṅganāśo 'ntaḥ śyāvaṃ yad vā salohitam
atyutsedhāvagāḍhaṃ vā sāśru nāḍīvraṇāvṛtam
purāṇaṃ viṣamaṃ madhye vicchinnaṃ yacca śukrakam
pañcetyuktā gadāḥ kṛṣṇe sādhyāsādhyavibhāgataḥ
athātaḥ sandhisitāsitarogapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
upanāhaṃ bhiṣak svinnaṃ bhinnaṃ vrīhimukhena ca
lekhayenmaṇḍalāgreṇa tataśca pratisārayet
pippalīkṣaudrasindhūtthair badhnīyāt pūrvavat tataḥ
paṭolapattrāmalakakvāthenāścotayecca tam
parvaṇī baḍiśenāttā bāhyasaṃdhitribhāgataḥ
vṛddhipattreṇa vardhyārdhe syād aśrugatiranyathā
cikitsā cārmavat kṣaudrasaindhavapratisāritā
pūyālase sirāṃ vidhyet tatas tam upanāhayet
kurvīta cākṣipākoktaṃ sarvaṃ karma yathāvidhi
saindhavārdrakakāsīsalohatāmraiḥ sucūrṇitaiḥ
cūrṇāñjanaṃ prayuñjīta sakṣaudrair vā rasakriyām
kṛmigranthiṃ karīṣeṇa svinnaṃ bhittvā vilikhya ca
triphalākṣaudrakāsīsasaindhavaiḥ pratisārayet
pittābhiṣyandavacchuktiṃ balāsāhvayapiṣṭake
kaphābhiṣyandavan muktvā sirāvyadham upācaret
bījapūrarasāktaṃ ca vyoṣakaṭphalam añjanam
jātīmukulasindhūtthadevadārumahauṣadhaiḥ
piṣṭaiḥ prasannayā vartiḥ śophakaṇḍūghnam añjanam
raktasyandavad utpātaharṣajālārjunakriyā
sirotpāte viśeṣeṇa ghṛtamākṣikam añjanam
sirāharṣe tu madhunā ślakṣṇaghṛṣṭaṃ rasāñjanam
arjune śarkarāmastukṣaudrairāścyotanaṃ hitam
sphaṭikaḥ kuṅkumaṃ śaṅkho madhukaṃ madhunāñjanam
madhunā cāñjanaṃ śaṅkhaḥ pheno vā sitayā saha
armoktaṃ pañcadhā tatra tanu dhūmāvilaṃ ca yat
raktaṃ dadhinibhaṃ yacca śukravat tasya bheṣajam
uttānasyetarat svinnaṃ sasindhūtthena cāñjitam
rasena bījapūrasya nimīlyākṣi vimardayet
itthaṃ saṃroṣitākṣasya pracale 'rmādhimāṃsake
ghṛtasya niścalaṃ mūrdhni vartmanośca viśeṣataḥ
apāṅgam īkṣamāṇasya vṛddhe 'rmaṇi kanīnakāt
valī syād yatra tatrārma baḍiśenāvalambitam
nātyāyataṃ mucuṇḍyā vā sūcyā sūtreṇa vā tataḥ
samantān maṇḍalāgreṇa mocayed atha mokṣitam
kanīnakam upānīya caturbhāgāvaśeṣitam
chindyāt kanīnakaṃ rakṣed vāhinīścāśruvāhinīḥ
kanīnakavyadhād aśru nāḍī cākṣṇi pravartate
vṛddhe 'rmaṇi tathāpāṅgāt paśyato 'sya kanīnakam
samyakchinnaṃ madhuvyoṣasaindhavapratisāritam
uṣṇena sarpiṣā siktam abhyaktaṃ madhusarpiṣā
badhnīyāt secayen muktvā tṛtīyādidineṣu ca
karañjabījasiddhena kṣīreṇa kvathitais tathā
sakṣaudrair dviniśālodhrapaṭolīyaṣṭikiṃśukaiḥ
kuraṇṭamukulopetair muñced evāhni saptame
samyakchinne bhavet svāsthyaṃ hīnāticchedajān gadān
sekāñjanaprabhṛtibhir jayellekhanabṛṃhaṇaiḥ
sitāmanaḥśilaileyalavaṇottamanāgaram
ardhakarṣonmitaṃ tārkṣyaṃ palārdhaṃ ca madhudrutam
añjanaṃ śleṣmatimirapillaśukrārmaśoṣajit
triphalaikatamadravyatvacaṃ pānīyakalkitām
śarāvapihitāṃ dagdhvā kapāle cūrṇayet tataḥ
pṛthakśeṣauṣadharasaiḥ pṛthag eva ca bhāvitā
sā maṣī śoṣitā peṣyā bhūyo dvilavaṇānvitā
trīṇyetānyañjanānyāha lekhanāni paraṃ nimiḥ
sirājāle sirā yās tu kaṭhinā lekhanauṣadhaiḥ
na sidhyantyarmavat tāsāṃ piṭikānāṃ ca sādhanam
doṣānurodhācchukreṣu snigdharūkṣā varā ghṛtam
tiktam ūrdhvam asṛksrāvo rekasekādi ceṣyate
tris trivṛdvāriṇā pakvaṃ kṣataśukre ghṛtaṃ pibet
sirayānu hared raktaṃ jalaukobhiśca locanāt
siddhenotpalakākolīdrākṣāyaṣṭīvidāribhiḥ
sasitenājapayasā secanaṃ salilena vā
rāgāśruvedanāśāntau paraṃ lekhanam añjanam
vartayo jātimukulalākṣāgairikacandanaiḥ
prasādayanti pittāsraṃ ghnanti ca kṣataśukrakam
dantair dantivarāhoṣṭragavāśvājakharodbhavaiḥ
saśaṅkhamauktikāmbhodhiphenair maricapādikaiḥ
kṣataśukram api vyāpi dantavartir nivartayet
tamālapattraṃ godantaśaṅkhapheno 'sthi gārdabham
tāmraṃ ca vartir mūtreṇa sarvaśukrakanāśinī
ratnāni dantāḥ śṛṅgāṇi dhātavas tryūṣaṇaṃ truṭī
karañjabījaṃ laśuno vraṇasādi ca bheṣajam
savraṇāvraṇagambhīratvaksthaśukraghnam añjanam
nimnam unnamayet snehapānanasyarasāñjanaiḥ
sarujaṃ nīrujaṃ tṛptipuṭapākena śukrakam
śuddhaśukre niśāyaṣṭīśārivāśābarāmbhasā
secanaṃ lodhrapoṭalyā koṣṇāmbhomagnayāthavā
bṛhatīmūlayaṣṭyāhvatāmrasaindhavanāgaraiḥ
dhātrīphalāmbunā piṣṭair lepitaṃ tāmrabhājanam
yavājyāmalakīpattrair bahuśo dhūpayet tataḥ
tatra kurvīta guṭikās tā jalakṣaudrapeṣitāḥ
mahānīlā iti khyātāḥ śuddhaśukraharāḥ param
sthire śukre ghane cāsya bahuśo 'pahared asṛk
śiraḥkāyavirekāṃśca puṭapākāṃśca bhūriśaḥ
kuryān maricavaidehīśirīṣaphalasaindhavaiḥ
harṣaṇaṃ triphalākvāthapītena lavaṇena vā
kuryād añjanayogau vā ślokārdhagaditāvimau
śaṅkhakolāsthikatakadrākṣāmadhukamākṣikaiḥ
surādantārṇavamalaiḥ śirīṣakusumānvitaiḥ
dhātrīphaṇijjakarase kṣāro lāṅgalikodbhavaḥ
uṣitaḥ śoṣitaścūrṇaḥ śukraharṣaṇam añjanam
mudgā vā nistuṣāḥ piṣṭāḥ śaṅkhakṣaudrasamāyutāḥ
sāro madhūkānmadhumān majjā vākṣāt samākṣikā
gokharāśvoṣṭradaśanāḥ śaṅkhaḥ phenaḥ samudrajaḥ
vartirarjunatoyena hṛṣṭaśukrakanāśinī
utsannaṃ vā saśalyaṃ vā śukraṃ vālādibhir likhet
sirāśukre tvadṛṣṭighne cikitsā vraṇaśukravat
puṇḍrayaṣṭyāhvakākolīsiṃhīlohaniśāñjanam
kalkitaṃ chāgadugdhena saghṛtair dhūpitaṃ yavaiḥ
dhātrīpattraiśca paryāyād vartiratrāñjanaṃ param
aśāntāvarmavacchastram ajakākhye ca yojayet
ajakāyām asādhyāyāṃ śukre 'nyatra ca tadvidhe
vedanopaśamaṃ snehapānāsṛksrāvaṇādibhiḥ
kuryād bībhatsatāṃ jetuṃ śukrasyotsedhasādhanam
nārikelāsthibhallātatālavaṃśakarīrajam
bhasmādbhiḥ srāvayet tābhir bhāvayet karabhāsthijam
cūrṇaṃ śukreṣvasādhyeṣu tad vaivarṇyaghnam añjanam
sādhyeṣu sādhanāyālam idam eva ca śīlitam
ajakāṃ pārśvato viddhvā sūcyā visrāvya codakam
samaṃ prapīḍyāṅguṣṭhena vasārdreṇānu pūrayet
vraṇaṃ gomāṃsacūrṇena baddhaṃ baddhaṃ vimucya ca
saptarātrād vraṇe rūḍhe kṛṣṇabhāge same sthire
snehāñjanaṃ ca kartavyaṃ nasyaṃ ca kṣīrasarpiṣā
tathāpi punarādhmāne bhedacchedādikāṃ kriyām
yuktyā kuryād yathā nāticchedena syāt nimajjanam
nityaṃ ca śukreṣu śṛtaṃ yathāsvaṃ pāne ca marśe ca ghṛtaṃ vidadhyāt
na hīyate labdhabalā tathāntas tīkṣṇāñjanair dṛk satataṃ prayuktaiḥ
athāto dṛṣṭirogavijñānīyamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhurātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
sirānusāriṇi male prathamaṃ paṭalaṃ śrite
avyaktam īkṣate rūpaṃ vyaktam apyanimittataḥ
prāpte dvitīyaṃ paṭalaṃ abhūtam api paśyati
bhūtaṃ tu yatnād āsannaṃ dūre sūkṣmaṃ ca nekṣate
dūrāntikasthaṃ rūpaṃ ca viparyāsena manyate
doṣe maṇḍalasaṃsthāne maṇḍalānīva paśyati
dvidhaikaṃ dṛṣṭimadhyasthe bahudhā bahudhāsthite
dṛṣṭerabhyantaragate hrasvavṛddhaviparyayam
nāntikastham adhaḥsaṃsthe dūragaṃ nopari sthite
pārśve paśyen na pārśvasthe timirākhyo 'yam āmayaḥ
prāpnoti kācatāṃ doṣe tṛtīyapaṭalāśrite
tenordhvam īkṣate nādhas tanucailāvṛtopamam
yathāvarṇaṃ ca rajyeta dṛṣṭir hīyeta ca kramāt
tathāpyupekṣamāṇasya caturthaṃ paṭalaṃ gataḥ
liṅganāśaṃ malaḥ kurvaṃśchādayed dṛṣṭimaṇḍalam
tatra vātena timire vyāviddham iva paśyati
calāvilāruṇābhāsaṃ prasannaṃ cekṣate muhuḥ
jālāni keśān maśakān raśmīṃścopekṣite 'tra ca
kācībhūte dṛg aruṇā paśyatyāsyam anāsikam
candradīpādyanekatvaṃ vakram ṛjvapi manyate
vṛddhaḥ kāco dṛśaṃ kuryād rajodhūmāvṛtām iva
spaṣṭāruṇābhāṃ vistīrṇāṃ sūkṣmāṃ vā hatadarśanām
sa liṅganāśo vāte tu saṃkocayati dṛksirāḥ
dṛṅmaṇḍalaṃ viśatyantar gambhīrā dṛg asau smṛtā
pittaje timire vidyutkhadyotadyotadīpitam
śikhitittiripattrābhaṃ prāyo nīlaṃ ca paśyati
kāce dṛk kācanīlābhā tādṛg eva ca paśyati
arkendupariveṣāgnimarīcīndradhanūṃṣi ca
bhṛṅganīlā nirālokā dṛk snigdhā liṅganāśataḥ
dṛṣṭiḥ pittena hrasvākhyā sā hrasvā hrasvadarśinī
bhavet pittavidagdhākhyā pītā pītābhadarśanā
kaphena timire prāyaḥ snigdhaṃ śvetaṃ ca paśyati
śaṅkhendukundakusumaiḥ kumudairiva cācitam
kāce tu niṣprabhendvarkapradīpādyairivācitam
sitābhā sā ca dṛṣṭiḥ syālliṅganāśe tu lakṣyate
mūrtaḥ kapho dṛṣṭigataḥ snigdho darśananāśanaḥ
bindur jalasyeva calaḥ padminīpuṭasaṃsthitaḥ
uṣṇe saṃkocam āyāti chāyāyāṃ parisarpati
śaṅkhakundendukumudasphaṭikopamaśuklimā
raktena timire raktaṃ tamobhūtaṃ ca paśyati
kācena raktā kṛṣṇā vā dṛṣṭis tādṛk ca paśyati
liṅganāśe 'pi tādṛg dṛṅniṣprabhā hatadarśanā
saṃsargasaṃnipāteṣu vidyāt saṃkīrṇalakṣaṇān
timirādīn akasmācca taiḥ syād vyaktākulekṣaṇaḥ
timire śeṣayor dṛṣṭau citro rāgaḥ prajāyate
dyotyate nakulasyeva yasya dṛṅnicitā malaiḥ
nakulāndhaḥ sa tatrāhni citraṃ paśyati no niśi
arke 'stamastakanyastagabhastau stambham āgatāḥ
sthagayanti dṛśaṃ doṣā doṣāndhaḥ sa gado 'paraḥ
divākarakaraspṛṣṭā bhraṣṭā dṛṣṭipathān malāḥ
vilīnalīnā yacchanti vyaktam atrāhni darśanam
uṣṇataptasya sahasā śītavārinimajjanāt
tridoṣaraktasaṃpṛkto yātyūṣmordhvaṃ tato 'kṣiṇi
dāhoṣe malinaṃ śuklam ahanyāviladarśanam
rātrāvāndhyaṃ ca jāyeta vidagdhoṣṇena sā smṛtā
bhṛśam amlāśanād doṣaiḥ sāsrair yā dṛṣṭirācitā
sakledakaṇḍūkaluṣā vidagdhāmlena sā smṛtā
śokajvaraśirorogasaṃtaptasyānilādayaḥ
dhūmāvilāṃ dhūmadṛśaṃ dṛśaṃ kuryuḥ sa dhūmaraḥ
sahasaivālpasattvasya paśyato rūpam adbhutam
bhāsvaraṃ bhāskarādiṃ vā vātādyā nayanāśritāḥ
kurvanti tejaḥ saṃśoṣya dṛṣṭiṃ muṣitadarśanām
vaiḍūryavarṇāṃ stimitāṃ prakṛtisthām ivāvyathām
aupasargika ityeṣa liṅganāśo 'tra varjayet
vinā kaphālliṅganāśān gambhīrāṃ hrasvajām api
ṣaṭ kācā nakulāndhaśca yāpyāḥ śeṣāṃstu sādhayet
dvādaśeti gadā dṛṣṭau nirdiṣṭāḥ saptaviṃśatiḥ
athātastimirapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhurātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
timiraṃ kācatāṃ yāti kāco 'pyāndhyam upekṣayā
netrarogeṣvato ghoraṃ timiraṃ sādhayed drutam
tulāṃ paceta jīvantyā droṇe 'pāṃ pādaśeṣite
tatkvāthe dviguṇakṣīraṃ ghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet
prapauṇḍarīkakākolīpippalīlodhrasaindhavaiḥ
śatāhvāmadhukadrākṣāsitādāruphalatrayaiḥ
kārṣikair niśi tat pītaṃ timirāpaharaṃ param
drākṣācandanamañjiṣṭhākākolīdvayajīvakaiḥ
sitāśatāvarīmedāpuṇḍrāhvamadhukotpalaiḥ
pacejjīrṇaghṛtaprasthaṃ samakṣīraṃ picūnmitaiḥ
hanti tat kācatimiraraktarājīśirorujaḥ
paṭolanimbakaṭukādārvīsevyavarāvṛṣam
sadhanvayāsatrāyantīparpaṭaṃ pālikaṃ pṛthak
prastham āmalakānāṃ ca kvāthayen nalvaṇe 'mbhasi
tadāḍhake 'rdhapalikaiḥ piṣṭaiḥ prasthaṃ ghṛtāt pacet
mustabhūnimbayaṣṭyāhvakuṭajodīcyacandanaiḥ
sapippalīkaistat sarpir ghrāṇakarṇāsyarogajit
vidradhijvaraduṣṭārurvisarpāpacikuṣṭhanut
viśeṣācchukratimiranaktāndhyoṣṇāmladāhahṛt
triphalāṣṭapalaṃ kvāthyaṃ pādaśeṣaṃ jalāḍhake
tena tulyapayaskena triphalāpalakalkavān
ardhaprastho ghṛtāt siddhaḥ sitayā mākṣikeṇa vā
yuktaṃ pibet tat timirī tadyuktaṃ vā varārasam
yaṣṭīmadhudvikākolīvyāghrīkṛṣṇāmṛtotpalaiḥ
pālikaiḥ sasitādrākṣair ghṛtaprasthaṃ pacet samaiḥ
ajākṣīravarāvasāmārkavasvarasaiḥ pṛthak
mahātraiphalam ityetat paraṃ dṛṣṭivikārajit
traiphalenātha haviṣā lihānastriphalāṃ niśi
yaṣṭīmadhukasaṃyuktāṃ madhunā ca pariplutām
māsam ekaṃ hitāhāraḥ pibann āmalakodakam
sauparṇaṃ labhate cakṣurityāha bhagavān nimiḥ
tāpyāyohemayaṣṭyāhvasitājīrṇājyamākṣikaiḥ
saṃyojitā yathākāmaṃ timiraghnī varā varā
saghṛtaṃ vā varākvāthaṃ śīlayet timirāmayī
apūpasūpasaktūn vā triphalācūrṇasaṃyutān
pāyasaṃ vā varāyuktaṃ śītaṃ samadhuśarkaram
prātar bhaktasya vā pūrvam adyāt pathyāṃ pṛthak pṛthak
mṛdvīkāśarkarākṣaudraiḥ satataṃ timirāturaḥ
srotojāṃśāṃścatuḥṣaṣṭiṃ tāmrāyorūpyakāñcanaiḥ
yuktān pratyekam ekāṃśairandhamūṣodarasthitān
dhmāpayitvā samāvṛttaṃ tatastacca niṣecayet
rasaskandhakaṣāyeṣu saptakṛtvaḥ pṛthak pṛthak
vaiḍūryamuktāśaṅkhānāṃ tribhir bhāgair yutaṃ tataḥ
cūrṇāñjanaṃ prayuñjīta tat sarvatimirāpaham
māṃsītrijātakāyaḥkuṅkumanīlotpalābhayātutthaiḥ
sitakācaśaṅkhaphenakamaricāñjanapippalīmadhukaiḥ
candre 'śvinīsanāthe sucūrṇitairañjayed yugalaṃ akṣṇoḥ
timirārmaraktarājīkaṇḍūkācādiśamam icchan
maricavaralavaṇabhāgau bhāgau dvau kaṇasamudraphenābhyām
sauvīrabhāganavakaṃ citrāyāṃ cūrṇitaṃ kaphāmayajit
drākṣāmṛṇālīsvarase kṣīramadyavasāsu ca
pṛthak divyāpsu srotojaṃ saptakṛtvo niṣecayet
taccūrṇitaṃ sthitaṃ śaṅkhe dṛkprasādanam añjanam
śastaṃ sarvākṣirogeṣu videhapatinirmitam
nirdagdhaṃ bādarāṅgāraistutthaṃ cetthaṃ niṣecitam
kramādajāpayaḥsarpiḥkṣaudre tasmāt paladvayam
kārṣikaistāpyamaricasrotojakaṭukānataiḥ
paṭulodhraśilāpathyākaṇailāñjanaphenakaiḥ
yuktaṃ palena yaṣṭyāśca mūṣāntardhmātacūrṇitam
hanti kācārmanaktāndhyaraktarājīḥ suśīlitaḥ
cūrṇo viśeṣāt timiraṃ bhāskaro bhāskaro yathā
triṃśadbhāgā bhujaṅgasya gandhapāṣāṇapañcakam
śulbatālakayor dvau dvau vaṅgasyaiko 'ñjanāt trayam
andhamūṣīkṛtaṃ dhmātaṃ pakvaṃ vimalam añjanam
timirāntakaraṃ loke dvitīya iva bhāskaraḥ
gomūtre chagaṇarase 'mlakāñjike ca strīstanye haviṣi viṣe ca mākṣike ca
yat tutthaṃ jvalitam anekaśo niṣiktaṃ tat kuryād garuḍasamaṃ narasya cakṣuḥ
śreṣṭhājalaṃ bhṛṅgarasaṃ saviṣājyam ajāpayaḥ
yaṣṭīrasaṃ ca yat sīsaṃ saptakṛtvaḥ pṛthak pṛthak
taptaṃ taptaṃ pāyitaṃ tacchalākā netre yuktā sāñjanānañjanā vā
taimiryārmasrāvapaicchilyapaillaṃ kaṇḍūṃ jāḍyaṃ raktarājīṃ ca hanti
rasendrabhujagau tulyau tayostulyam athāñjanam
īṣatkarpūrasaṃyuktam añjanaṃ timirāpaham
yo gṛdhrastaruṇaraviprakāśagallastasyāsyaṃ samayamṛtasya gośakṛdbhiḥ
nirdagdhaṃ samaghṛtam añjanaṃ ca peṣyaṃ yogo 'yaṃ nayanabalaṃ karoti gārdhram
kṛṣṇasarpavadane sahaviṣkaṃ dagdham añjananiḥsṛtadhūmam
cūrṇitaṃ naladapattravimiśraṃ bhinnatāram api rakṣati cakṣuḥ
kṛṣṇasarpaṃ mṛtaṃ nyasya caturaścāpi vṛścikān
kṣīrakumbhe trisaptāhaṃ kledayitvā pramanthayet
tatra yannavanītaṃ syāt puṣṇīyāt tena kukkuṭam
andhastasya purīṣeṇa prekṣate dhruvam añjanāt
kṛṣṇasarpavasā śaṅkhaḥ katakāt phalam añjanam
rasakriyeyam acirād andhānāṃ darśanapradā
maricāni daśārdhapicustāpyāt tutthāt palaṃ picur yaṣṭyāḥ
kṣīrārdradagdham añjanam apratisārākhyam uttamaṃ timire
akṣabījamaricāmalakatvaktutthayaṣṭimadhukair jalapiṣṭaiḥ
chāyayaiva guṭikāḥ pariśuṣkā nāśayanti timirāṇyacireṇa
maricāmalakajalodbhavatutthāñjanatāpyadhātubhiḥ kramavṛddhaiḥ
ṣaṇmākṣika iti yogastimirārmakledakācakaṇḍūhantā
ratnāni rūpyaṃ sphaṭikaṃ suvarṇaṃ sroto'ñjanaṃ tāmram ayaḥ saśaṅkhaṃ
kucandanaṃ lohitagairikaṃ ca cūrṇāñjanaṃ sarvadṛgāmayaghnam
tilatailam akṣatailaṃ bhṛṅgasvaraso 'sanācca niryūhaḥ
āyasapātravipakvaṃ karoti dṛṣṭer balaṃ nasyam
doṣānurodhena ca naikaśastaṃ snehāsravisrāvaṇarekanasyaiḥ
upācared añjanamūrdhavastivastikriyātarpaṇalepasekaiḥ
sāmānyaṃ sādhanam idaṃ pratidoṣam ataḥ śṛṇu
vātaje timire tatra daśamūlāmbhasā ghṛtam
kṣīre caturguṇe śreṣṭhākalkapakvaṃ pibet tataḥ
triphalāpañcamūlānāṃ kaṣāyaṃ kṣīrasaṃyutam
eraṇḍatailasaṃyuktaṃ yojayecca virecanam
samūlajālajīvantītulāṃ droṇe 'mbhasaḥ pacet
aṣṭabhāgasthite tasmiṃstailaprasthaṃ payaḥsame
balātritayajīvantīvarīmūlaiḥ palonmitaiḥ
yaṣṭīpalaiścaturbhiśca lohapātre vipācayet
loha eva sthitaṃ māsaṃ nāvanād ūrdhvajatrujān
vātapittāmayān hanti tad viśeṣād dṛgāśrayān
keśāsyakandharāskandhapuṣṭilāvaṇyakāntidam
sitairaṇḍajaṭāsiṃhīphaladāruvacānataiḥ
ghoṣayā bilvamūlaiśca tailaṃ pakvaṃ payo'nvitam
nasyaṃ sarvordhvajatrūtthavātaśleṣmāmayārtijit
vasāñjane ca vaiyāghrī vārāhī vā praśasyate
gṛdhrāhikukkuṭotthā vā madhukenānvitā pṛthak
pratyañjane ca srotojaṃ rasakṣīraghṛte kramāt
niṣiktaṃ pūrvavad yojyaṃ timiraghnam anuttamam
na ced evaṃ śamaṃ yāti tatastarpaṇam ācaret
śatāhvākuṣṭhanaladakākolīdvayayaṣṭibhiḥ
prapauṇḍarīkasaralapippalīdevadārubhiḥ
sarpiraṣṭaguṇakṣīraṃ pakvaṃ tarpaṇam uttamam
medasastadvad aiṇeyād dugdhasiddhāt khajāhatāt
uddhṛtaṃ sādhitaṃ tejo madhukośīracandanaiḥ
śvāvicchalyakagodhānāṃ dakṣatittiribarhiṇām
pṛthak pṛthag anenaiva vidhinā kalpayed vasām
prasādanaṃ snehanaṃ ca puṭapākaṃ prayojayet
vātapīnasavaccātra nirūhaṃ sānuvāsanam
pittaje timire sarpir jīvanīyaphalatrayaiḥ
vipācitaṃ pāyayitvā snigdhasya vyadhayet sirām
śarkarailātrivṛccūrṇair madhuyuktair virecayet
suśītān sekalepādīn yuñjyān netrāsyamūrdhasu
śārivāpadmakośīramuktāśābaracandanaiḥ
vartiḥ śastāñjane cūrṇastathā pattrotpalāñjanaiḥ
sanāgapuṣpakarpūrayaṣṭyāhvasvarṇagairikaiḥ
sauvīrāñjanatutthakaśṛṅgīdhātrīphalasphaṭikakarpūram
pañcāṃśaṃ pañcāṃśaṃ tryaṃśam athaikāṃśam añjanaṃ timiraghnam
nasyaṃ cājyaṃ śṛtaṃ kṣīrajīvanīyasitotpalaiḥ
śleṣmodbhave 'mṛtākvāthavarākaṇaśṛtaṃ ghṛtam
vidhyet sirāṃ pītavato dadyāccānu virecanam
kvāthaṃ pūgābhayāśuṇṭhīkṛṣṇākumbhanikumbhajam
hrīveradārudviniśākṛṣṇākalkaiḥ payo'nvitaiḥ
dvipañcamūlaniryūhe tailaṃ pakvaṃ ca nāvanam
śaṅkhapriyaṅgunepālīkaṭutrikaphalatrikaiḥ
dṛgvaimalyāya vimalā vartiḥ syāt kokilā punaḥ
kṛṣṇaloharajovyoṣasaindhavatriphalāñjanaiḥ
śaśagokharasiṃhoṣṭradvijā lālāṭam asthi ca
śvetagovālamaricaśaṅkhacandanaphenakam
piṣṭaṃ stanyājyadugdhābhyāṃ vartistimiraśukrajit
raktaje pittavat siddhiḥ śītaiścāsraṃ prasādayet
drākṣayā naladalodhrayaṣṭibhiḥ śaṅkhatāmrahimapadmapadmakaiḥ
sotpalaiśchagaladugdhavartitair asrajaṃ timiram āśu naśyati
saṃsargasaṃnipātotthe yathādoṣodayaṃ kriyā
siddhaṃ madhūkakṛmijinmaricāmaradārubhiḥ
sakṣīraṃ nāvanaṃ tailaṃ piṣṭair lepo mukhasya ca
natanīlotpalānantāyaṣṭyāhvasuniṣaṇṇakaiḥ
sādhitaṃ nāvane tailaṃ śirovastau ca śasyate
dadyād uśīraniryūhe cūrṇitaṃ kaṇasaindhavam
tat srutaṃ saghṛtaṃ bhūyaḥ pacet kṣaudraṃ ghane kṣipet
śīte cāsmin hitam idaṃ sarvaje timire 'ñjanam
asthīni majjapūrṇāni sattvānāṃ rātricāriṇām
srotojāñjanayuktāni vahatyambhasi vāsayet
māsaṃ viṃśatirātraṃ vā tataścoddhṛtya śoṣayet
sameṣaśṛṅgīpuṣpāṇi sayaṣṭyāhvāni tānyanu
cūrṇitānyañjanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ timire sāṃnipātike
kāce 'pyeṣā kriyā muktvā sirāṃ yantranipīḍitāḥ
āndhyāya syur malā dadyāt srāvye tvasre jalaukasaḥ
guḍaḥ pheno 'ñjanaṃ kṛṣṇā maricaṃ kuṅkumād rajaḥ
rasakriyeyaṃ sakṣaudrā kācayāpanam añjanam
nakulāndhe tridoṣotthe taimiryavihito vidhiḥ
rasakriyā ghṛtakṣaudragomayasvarasadrutaiḥ
tārkṣyagairikatālīśair niśāndhe hitam añjanam
dadhnā vighṛṣṭaṃ maricaṃ rātryandhe 'ñjanam uttamam
karañjikotpalasvarṇagairikāmbhojakesaraiḥ
piṣṭair gomayatoyena vartir doṣāndhanāśinī
ajāmūtreṇa vā kauntīkṛṣṇāsrotojasaindhavaiḥ
kālānusārītrikaṭutriphalālamanaḥśilāḥ
saphenāśchāgadugdhena rātryandhe vartayo hitāḥ
saṃniveśya yakṛnmadhye pippalīradahan pacet
tāḥ śuṣkā madhunā ghṛṣṭā niśāndhe śreṣṭham añjanam
khādecca plīhayakṛtī māhiṣe tailasarpiṣā
ghṛte siddhāni jīvantyāḥ pallavāni ca bhakṣayet
tathātimuktakairaṇḍaśephālyabhīrujāni ca
bhṛṣṭaṃ ghṛtaṃ kumbhayoneḥ pattraiḥ pāne ca pūjitam
dhūmarākhyāmlapittoṣṇavidāhe jīrṇasarpiṣā
snigdhaṃ virecayecchītaiḥ śītair dihyācca sarvataḥ
gośakṛdrasadugdhājyair vipakvaṃ śasyate 'ñjanam
svarṇagairikatālīśacūrṇāvāpā rasakriyā
medāśābarakānantāmañjiṣṭhādārviyaṣṭibhiḥ
kṣīrāṣṭāṃśaṃ ghṛtaṃ pakvaṃ satailaṃ nāvanaṃ hitam
tarpaṇaṃ kṣīrasarpiḥ syād aśāmyati sirāvyadhaḥ
cintābhighātabhīśokaraukṣyāt sotkaṭakāsanāt
virekanasyavamanapuṭapākādivibhramāt
vidagdhāhāravamanāt kṣuttṛṣṇādividhāraṇāt
akṣirogāvasānācca paśyet timirarogivat
yathāsvaṃ tatra yuñjīta doṣādīn vīkṣya bheṣajam
sūryoparāgānalavidyudādivilokanenopahatekṣaṇasya
saṃtarpaṇaṃ snigdhahimādi kāryaṃ tathāñjanaṃ hema ghṛtena ghṛṣṭam
cakṣūrakṣāyāṃ sarvakālaṃ manuṣyair yatnaḥ kartavyo jīvite yāvad icchā
vyartho loko 'yaṃ tulyarātriṃdivānāṃ puṃsām andhānāṃ vidyamāne 'pi vitte
triphalā rudhirasrutir viśuddhir manaso nirvṛtirañjanaṃ sanasyam
śakunāśanatā sapādapūjā ghṛtapānaṃ ca sadaiva netrarakṣā
ahitād aśanāt sadā nivṛttir bhṛśabhāsvaccalasūkṣmavīkṣaṇācca
muninā niminopadiṣṭam etat paramaṃ rakṣaṇam īkṣaṇasya puṃsām
athāto liṅganāśapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
vidhyet sujātaṃ niṣprekṣyaṃ liṅganāśaṃ kaphodbhavam
āvartakyādibhiḥ ṣaḍbhir vivarjitam upadravaiḥ
so 'saṃjāto hi viṣamo dadhimastunibhastanuḥ
śalākayāvakṛṣṭo 'pi punarūrdhvaṃ prapadyate
karoti vedanāṃ tīvrāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ ca sthagayet punaḥ
śleṣmalaiḥ pūryate cāśu so 'nyaiḥ sopadravaścirāt
ślaiṣmiko liṅganāśo hi sitatvācchleṣmaṇaḥ sitaḥ
tasyānyadoṣābhibhavād bhavatyānīlatā gadaḥ
tatrāvartacalā dṛṣṭirāvartakyaruṇāsitā
śarkarārkapayoleśaniciteva ghanāti ca
rājīmatī dṛṅ nicitā śāliśūkābharājibhiḥ
viṣamacchinnadagdhābhā saruk chinnāṃśukā smṛtā
dṛṣṭiḥ kāṃsyasamacchāyā candrakī candrakākṛtiḥ
chattrābhā naikavarṇā ca chattrakī nāma nīlikā
na vidhyed asirārhāṇāṃ na tṛṭpīnasakāsinām
nājīrṇibhīruvamitaśiraḥkarṇākṣiśūlinām
atha sādhāraṇe kāle śuddhasaṃbhojitātmanaḥ
deśe prakāśe pūrvāhṇe bhiṣag jānūccapīṭhagaḥ
yantritasyopaviṣṭasya svinnākṣasya mukhānilaiḥ
aṅguṣṭhamṛdite netre dṛṣṭau dṛṣṭvotplutaṃ malam
svāṃ nāsāṃ prekṣamāṇasya niṣkampaṃ mūrdhni dhārite
kṛṣṇād ardhāṅgulaṃ muktvā tathārdhārdham apāṅgataḥ
tarjanīmadhyamāṅguṣṭhaiḥ śalākāṃ niścalaṃ dhṛtām
daivacchidraṃ nayet pārśvād ūrdhvam āmanthayan iva
savyaṃ dakṣiṇahastena netraṃ savyena cetarat
vidhyet suviddhe śabdaḥ syād aruk cāmbulavasrutiḥ
sāntvayann āturaṃ cānu netraṃ stanyena secayet
śalākāyāstato 'greṇa nirlikhen netramaṇḍalam
abādhamānaḥ śanakair nāsāṃ prati nudaṃstataḥ
ucchiṅghanāccāpahared dṛṣṭimaṇḍalagaṃ kapham
sthire doṣe cale vāti svedayed akṣi bāhyataḥ
atha dṛṣṭeṣu rūpeṣu śalākām āharecchanaiḥ
ghṛtāplutaṃ picuṃ dattvā baddhākṣaṃ śāyayet tataḥ
viddhād anyena pārśvena tam uttānaṃ dvayor vyadhe
nivāte śayane 'bhyaktaśiraḥpādaṃ hite ratam
kṣavathuṃ kāsam udgāraṃ ṣṭhīvanaṃ pānam ambhasaḥ
adhomukhasthitiṃ snānaṃ dantadhāvanabhakṣaṇam
saptāhaṃ nācaret snehapītavaccātra yantraṇā
śaktito laṅghayet seko ruji koṣṇena sarpiṣā
savyoṣāmalakaṃ vāṭyam aśnīyāt saghṛtaṃ dravam
vilepīṃ vā tryahāccāsya kvāthair muktvākṣi secayet
vātaghnaiḥ saptame tvahni sarvathaivākṣi mocayet
yantraṇām anurudhyeta dṛṣṭer ā sthairyalābhataḥ
rūpāṇi sūkṣmadīptāni sahasā nāvalokayet
śopharāgarujādīnām adhimanthasya codbhavaḥ
ahitair vedhadoṣācca yathāsvaṃ tān upācaret
kalkitāḥ saghṛtā dūrvāyavagairikaśārivāḥ
mukhālepe prayoktavyā rujārāgopaśāntaye
sasarṣapāstilāstadvan mātuluṅgarasāplutāḥ
payasyāśārivāpattramañjiṣṭhāmadhuyaṣṭibhiḥ
ajākṣīrayutair lepaḥ sukhoṣṇaḥ śarmakṛt param
lodhrasaindhavamṛdvīkāmadhukaiśchāgalaṃ payaḥ
śṛtam āścyotanaṃ yojyaṃ rujārāgavināśanam
madhukotpalakuṣṭhair vā drākṣālākṣāsitānvitaiḥ
vātaghnasiddhe payasi śṛtaṃ sarpiścaturguṇe
padmakādipratīvāpaṃ sarvakarmasu śasyate
sirāṃ tathānupaśame snigdhasvinnasya mokṣayet
manthoktāṃ ca kriyāṃ kuryād vedhe rūḍhe 'ñjanaṃ mṛdu
āḍhakīmūlamaricaharitālarasāñjanaiḥ
viddhe 'kṣṇi saguḍā vartir yojyā divyāmbupeṣitā
jātīśirīṣadhavameṣaviṣāṇipuṣpavaiḍūryamauktikaphalaṃ payasā supiṣṭam
ājena tāmram amunā pratanu pradigdhaṃ saptāhataḥ punaridaṃ payasaiva piṣṭam
piṇḍāñjanaṃ hitam anātapaśuṣkam akṣṇi viddhe prasādajananaṃ balakṛcca dṛṣṭeḥ
srotojavidrumaśilāmbudhiphenatīkṣṇairasyaiva tulyam uditaṃ guṇakalpanābhiḥ
athātaḥ sarvākṣirogavijñānīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
vātena netre 'bhiṣyaṇṇe nāsānāho 'lpaśophatā
śaṅkhākṣibhrūlalāṭasya todasphuraṇabhedanam
śuṣkālpā dūṣikā śītam acchaṃ cāśru calā rujaḥ
nimeṣonmeṣaṇaṃ kṛcchrājjantūnām iva sarpaṇam
akṣyādhmātam ivābhāti sūkṣmaiḥ śalyairivācitam
snigdhoṣṇaiścopaśamanaṃ so 'bhiṣyanda upekṣitaḥ
adhimantho bhavet tatra karṇayor nadanaṃ bhramaḥ
araṇyeva ca mathyante lalāṭākṣibhruvādayaḥ
hatādhimanthaḥ so 'pi syāt pramādāt tena vedanāḥ
anekarūpā jāyante vraṇo dṛṣṭau ca dṛṣṭihā
manyākṣiśaṅkhato vāyuranyato vā pravartayan
vyathāṃ tīvrām apaicchilyarāgaśophaṃ vilocanam
saṃkocayati paryaśru so 'nyatovātasaṃjñitaḥ
tadvajjihmaṃ bhavennetram ūnaṃ vā vātaparyaye
dāho dhūmāyanaṃ śophaḥ śyāvatā vartmano bahiḥ
antaḥkledo 'śru pītoṣṇaṃ rāgaḥ pītābhadarśanam
kṣārokṣitakṣatākṣitvaṃ pittābhiṣyandalakṣaṇam
jvaladaṅgārakīrṇābhaṃ yakṛtpiṇḍasamaprabham
adhimanthe bhaven netraṃ syande tu kaphasaṃbhave
jāḍyaṃ śopho mahān kaṇḍūr nidrānnānabhinandanam
sāndrasnigdhabahuśvetapicchāvad dūṣikāśrutā
adhimanthe nataṃ kṛṣṇam unnataṃ śuklamaṇḍalam
praseko nāsikādhmānaṃ pāṃsupūrṇam ivekṣaṇam
raktāśrurājīdūṣīkāraktamaṇḍaladarśanam
raktasyandena nayanaṃ sapittasyandalakṣaṇam
manthe 'kṣi tāmraparyantam utpāṭanasamānaruk
rāgeṇa bandhūkanibhaṃ tāmyati sparśanākṣamam
asṛṅnimagnāriṣṭābhaṃ kṛṣṇam agnyābhadarśanam
adhimanthā yathāsvaṃ ca sarve syandādhikavyathāḥ
śaṅkhadantakapoleṣu kapāle cātirukkarāḥ
vātapittāturaṃ gharṣatodabhedopadehavat
rūkṣadāruṇavartmākṣi kṛcchronmīlanimīlanam
vikūṇanaviśuṣkatvaśītecchāśūlapākavat
uktaḥ śuṣkādipāko 'yaṃ saśophaḥ syāt tribhir malaiḥ
saraktaistatra śopho 'tirugdāhaṣṭhīvanādimān
pakvodumbarasaṃkāśaṃ jāyate śuklamaṇḍalam
aśrūṣṇaśītaviśadapicchilācchaghanaṃ muhuḥ
alpaśophe 'lpaśophastu pāko 'nyair lakṣaṇaistathā
akṣipākātyaye śophaḥ saṃrambhaḥ kaluṣāśrutā
kaphopadigdham asitaṃ sitaṃ prakledarāgavat
dāho darśanasaṃrodho vedanāścānavasthitāḥ
annasāro 'mlatāṃ nītaḥ pittaraktolbaṇair malaiḥ
sirābhir netram ārūḍhaḥ karoti śyāvalohitam
saśophadāhapākāśru bhṛśaṃ cāviladarśanam
amloṣito 'yam ityuktā gadāḥ ṣoḍaśa sarvagāḥ
hatādhimantham eteṣu sākṣipākātyayaṃ tyajet
vātodbhūtaḥ pañcarātreṇa dṛṣṭiṃ saptāhena śleṣmajāto 'dhimanthaḥ
raktotpanno hanti tadvat trirātrān mithyācārāt paittikaḥ sadya eva
athātaḥ sarvākṣirogapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
prāgrūpa eva syandeṣu tīkṣṇaṃ gaṇḍūṣanāvanam
kārayed upavāsaṃ ca kopād anyatra vātajāt
dāhopadeharāgāśruśophaśāntyai biḍālakam
kuryāt sarvatra pattrailāmaricasvarṇagairikaiḥ
sarasāñjanayaṣṭyāhvanatacandanasaindhavaiḥ
saindhavaṃ nāgaraṃ tārkṣyaṃ bhṛṣṭaṃ maṇḍena sarpiṣaḥ
vātaje ghṛtabhṛṣṭaṃ vā yojyaṃ śabaradeśajam
māṃsīpadmakakālīyayaṣṭyāhvaiḥ pittaraktayoḥ
manohvāphalinīkṣaudraiḥ kaphe sarvaistu sarvaje
sitamaricabhāgam ekaṃ caturmanohvaṃ dviraṣṭaśābarakam
saṃcūrṇya vastrabaddhaṃ prakupitamātre 'vaguṇṭhanaṃ netre
āraṇyāśchagaṇarase paṭāvabaddhāḥ susvinnā nakhavituṣīkṛtāḥ kulatthāḥ
taccūrṇaṃ sakṛd avacūrṇanānniśīthe netrāṇāṃ vidhamati sadya eva kopam
ghoṣābhayātutthakayaṣṭilodhrair mūtī susūkṣmaiḥ ślathavastrabaddhaiḥ
tāmrasthadhānyāmlanimagnamūrtirartiṃ jayatyakṣiṇi naikarūpām
ṣoḍaśabhiḥ salilapalaiḥ palaṃ tathaikaṃ kaṭaṅkaṭeryāḥ siddham
seko 'ṣṭabhāgaśiṣṭaḥ kṣaudrayutaḥ sarvadoṣakupite netre
vātapittakaphasaṃnipātajāṃ netrayor bahuvidhām api vyathām
śīghram eva jayati prayojitaḥ śigrupallavarasaḥ samākṣikaḥ
taruṇam urubūkapattraṃ mūlaṃ ca vibhidya siddham āje kṣīre
vātābhiṣyandarujaṃ sadyo vinihanti saktupiṇḍikā coṣṇā
āścyotanaṃ mārutaje kvātho bilvādibhir hitaḥ
koṣṇaḥ sahairaṇḍajaṭābṛhatīmadhuśigrubhiḥ
hrīveravakraśārṅgaṣṭodumbaratvakṣu sādhitam
sāmbhasā payasājena śūlāścyotanam uttamam
mañjiṣṭhārajanīlākṣādrākṣarddhimadhukotpalaiḥ
kvāthaḥ saśarkaraḥ śītaḥ secanaṃ raktapittajit
kaseruyaṣṭyāhvarajastāntave śithilaṃ sthitam
apsu divyāsu nihitaṃ hitaṃ syande 'srapittaje
puṇḍrayaṣṭīniśāmūtī plutā stanye saśarkare
chāgadugdhe 'thavā dāharugrāgāśrunivartanī
śvetalodhraṃ samadhukaṃ ghṛtabhṛṣṭaṃ sucūrṇitam
vastrasthaṃ stanyamṛditaṃ pittaraktābhighātajit
nāgaratriphalānimbavāsālodhrarasaḥ kaphe
koṣṇam āścyotanaṃ miśrair bheṣajaiḥ sāṃnipātike
sarpiḥ purāṇaṃ pavane pitte śarkarayānvitam
vyoṣasiddhaṃ kaphe pītvā yavakṣārāvacūrṇitam
srāvayed rudhiraṃ bhūyastataḥ snigdhaṃ virecayet
ānūpavesavāreṇa śirovadanalepanam
uṣṇena śūle dāhe tu payaḥsarpiryutair himaiḥ
timirapratiṣedhaṃ ca vīkṣya yuñjyād yathāyatham
ayam eva vidhiḥ sarvo manthādiṣvapi śasyate
aśāntau sarvathā manthe bhruvorupari dāhayet
rūpyaṃ rūkṣeṇa godadhnā limpennīlatvam āgate
śuṣke tu mastunā vartir vātākṣyāmayanāśinī
sumanaḥkorakāḥ śaṅkhastriphalā madhukaṃ balā
pittaraktāpahā vartiḥ piṣṭā divyena vāriṇā
saindhavaṃ triphalā vyoṣaṃ śaṅkhanābhiḥ samudrajaḥ
phena aileyakaṃ sarjo vartiḥ śleṣmākṣiroganut
prapauṇḍarīkaṃ yaṣṭyāhvaṃ dārvī cāṣṭapalaṃ pacet
jaladroṇe rase pūte punaḥ pakve ghane kṣipet
puṣpāñjanād daśapalaṃ karṣaṃ ca maricāt tataḥ
kṛtaścūrṇo 'thavā vartiḥ sarvābhiṣyandasaṃbhavān
hanti rāgarujāgharṣān sadyo dṛṣṭiṃ prasādayet
ayaṃ pāśupato yogo rahasyaṃ bhiṣajāṃ param
śuṣkākṣipāke haviṣaḥ pānam akṣṇośca tarpaṇam
ghṛtena jīvanīyena nasyaṃ tailena vāṇunā
pariṣeko hitaścātra payaḥ koṣṇaṃ sasaindhavam
sarpiryuktaṃ stanyapiṣṭam añjanaṃ ca mahauṣadham
vasā vānūpasattvotthā kiṃcitsaindhavanāgarā
ghṛtāktān darpaṇe ghṛṣṭān keśān mallakasaṃpuṭe
dagdhvājyapiṣṭā lohasthā sā maṣī śreṣṭham añjanam
saśophe vālpaśophe ca snigdhasya vyadhayet sirām
rekaḥ snigdhe punar drākṣāpathyākvāthatrivṛdghṛtaiḥ
śvetalodhraṃ ghṛte bhṛṣṭaṃ cūrṇitaṃ tāntavasthitam
uṣṇāmbunā vimṛditaṃ sekaḥ śūlaharaḥ param
dārvīprapauṇḍarīkasya kvātho vāścyotane hitaḥ
tāmraṃ lohe mūtraghṛṣṭaṃ prayuktaṃ netre sarpirdhūpitaṃ vedanāghnam
tāmre ghṛṣṭo gavyadadhnaḥ saro vā yuktaḥ kṛṣṇāsaindhavābhyāṃ variṣṭhaḥ
śaṅkhaṃ tāmre stanyaghṛṣṭaṃ ghṛtāktaiḥ śamyāḥ pattrair dhūpitaṃ tad yavaiśca
netre yuktaṃ hanti saṃdhāvasaṃjñaṃ kṣipraṃ gharṣaṃ vedanāṃ cātitīvrām
udumbaraphalaṃ lohe ghṛṣṭaṃ stanyena dhūpitam
sājyaiḥ śamīchadair dāhaśūlarāgāśruharṣajit
śigrupallavaniryāsaḥ sughṛṣṭastāmrasaṃpuṭe
ghṛtena dhūpito hanti śophagharṣāśruvedanāḥ
tilāmbhasā mṛtkapālaṃ kāṃsye ghṛṣṭaṃ sudhūpitam
nimbapattrair ghṛtābhyaktair gharṣaśūlāśrurāgajit
saṃdhāvenāñjite netre vigatauṣadhavedane
stanyenāścyotanaṃ kāryaṃ triḥ paraṃ nāñjayecca taiḥ
tālīśapattracapalānataloharajo'ñjanaiḥ
jātīmukulakāsīsasaindhavair mūtrapeṣitaiḥ
tāmram ālipya saptāhaṃ dhārayet peṣayet tataḥ
mūtreṇaivānu guṭikāḥ kāryāśchāyāviśoṣitāḥ
tāḥ stanyaghṛṣṭā gharṣāśruśophakaṇḍūvināśanāḥ
vyāghrītvaṅmadhukaṃ tāmrarajo 'jākṣīrakalkitam
śamyāmalakapattrājyadhūpitaṃ śopharukpraṇut
amloṣite prayuñjīta pittābhiṣyandasādhanam
utkliṣṭāḥ kaphapittāsranicayotthāḥ kukūṇakaḥ
pakṣmoparodhaṃ śuṣkākṣipākaḥ pūyālaso bisaḥ
pothakyamloṣito 'lpākhyaḥ syandamanthā vinānilāt
ete 'ṣṭādaśa pillākhyā dīrghakālānubandhinaḥ
cikitsā pṛthag eteṣāṃ svaṃsvam uktātha vakṣyate
pillībhūteṣu sāmānyād atha pillākhyarogiṇaḥ
snigdhasya charditavataḥ sirāvyadhahṛtāsṛjaḥ
viriktasya ca vartmānu nirlikhed ā viśuddhitaḥ
tutthakasya palaṃ śvetamaricāni ca viṃśatiḥ
triṃśatā kāñjikapalaiḥ piṣṭvā tāmre nidhāpayet
pillān apillān kurute bahuvarṣotthitān api
tat sekenopadehāśrukaṇḍūśophāṃśca nāśayet
karañjabījaṃ surasaṃ sumanaḥkorakāṇi ca
saṃkṣudya sādhayet kvāthe pūte tatra rasakriyā
añjanaṃ pillabhaiṣajyaṃ pakṣmaṇāṃ ca prarohaṇam
rasāñjanaṃ sarjaraso rītipuṣpaṃ manaḥśilā
samudrapheno lavaṇaṃ gairikaṃ maricāni ca
añjanaṃ madhunā piṣṭaṃ kledakaṇḍūghnam uttamam
abhayārasapiṣṭaṃ vā tagaraṃ pillanāśanam
bhāvitaṃ bastamūtreṇa sasnehaṃ devadāru ca
saindhavatriphalākṛṣṇākaṭukāśaṅkhanābhayaḥ
satāmrarajaso vartiḥ pillaśukrakanāśinī
puṣpakāsīsacūrṇo vā surasārasabhāvitaḥ
tāmre daśāhaṃ tat paillyapakṣmaśātajid añjanam
alaṃ ca sauvīrakam añjanaṃ ca tābhyāṃ samaṃ tāmrarajaḥ susūkṣmam
pilleṣu romāṇi niṣevito 'sau cūrṇaḥ karotyekaśalākayāpi
lākṣānirguṇḍībhṛṅgadārvīrasena śreṣṭhaṃ kārpāsaṃ bhāvitaṃ saptakṛtvaḥ
dīpaḥ prajvālyaḥ sarpiṣā tatsamutthā śreṣṭhā pillānāṃ ropaṇārthe maṣī sā
vartmāvalekhaṃ bahuśastadvacchoṇitamokṣaṇam
punaḥ punar virekaṃ ca nityam āścyotanāñjanam
nāvanaṃ dhūmapānaṃ ca pillarogāturo bhajet
pūyālase tvaśānte 'nte dāhaḥ sūkṣmaśalākayā
caturṇavatirityakṣṇo hetulakṣaṇasādhanaiḥ
parasparam asaṃkīrṇāḥ kārtsnyena gaditā gadāḥ
sarvadā ca niṣeveta svastho 'pi nayanapriyaḥ
purāṇayavagodhūmaśāliṣaṣṭikakodravān
mudgādīn kaphapittaghnān bhūrisarpiḥpariplutān
śākaṃ caivaṃvidhaṃ māṃsaṃ jāṅgalaṃ dāḍimaṃ sitām
saindhavaṃ triphalāṃ drākṣāṃ vāri pāne ca nābhasam
ātapatraṃ padatrāṇaṃ vidhivad doṣaśodhanam
varjayed vegasaṃrodham ajīrṇādhyaśanāni ca
krodhaśokadivāsvapnarātrijāgaraṇātapān
vidāhi viṣṭambhakaraṃ yaccehāhārabheṣajam
dve pādamadhye pṛthusaṃniveśe sire gate te bahudhā ca netre
tā mrakṣaṇodvartanalepanādīn pādaprayuktānnayane nayanti
malauṣṇyasaṃghaṭṭanapīḍanādyaistā dūṣayante nayanāni duṣṭāḥ
bhajet sadā dṛṣṭihitāni tasmād upānadabhyañjanadhāvanāni
athātaḥ karṇarogavijñānīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
pratiśyāyajalakrīḍākarṇakaṇḍūyanair marut
mithyāyogena śabdasya kupito 'nyaiśca kopanaiḥ
prāpya śrotrasirāḥ kuryācchūlaṃ srotasi vegavat
ardhāvabhedakaṃ stambhaṃ śiśirānabhinandanam
cirācca pākaṃ pakvaṃ tu lasīkām alpaśaḥ sravet
śrotraṃ śūnyam akasmācca syāt saṃcāravicāravat
śūlaṃ pittāt sadāhoṣāśītecchāśvayathujvaram
āśupākaṃ prapakvaṃ ca sapītalasikāsruti
sā lasīkā spṛśed yad yat tat tat pākam upaiti ca
kaphācchirohanugrīvāgauravaṃ mandatā rujaḥ
kaṇḍūḥ śvayathuruṣṇecchā pākācchvetaghanasrutiḥ
karoti śravaṇe śūlam abhighātādidūṣitam
raktaṃ pittasamānārti kiṃcid vādhikalakṣaṇam
śūlaṃ samuditair doṣaiḥ saśophajvaratīvraruk
paryāyād uṣṇaśītecchaṃ jāyate śrutijāḍyavat
pakvaṃ sitāsitāraktaghanapūyapravāhi ca
śabdavāhisirāsaṃsthe śṛṇoti pavane muhuḥ
nādān akasmād vividhān karṇanādaṃ vadanti tam
śleṣmaṇānugato vāyur nādo vā samupekṣitaḥ
uccaiḥ kṛcchrācchrutiṃ kuryād badhiratvaṃ krameṇa ca
vātena śoṣitaḥ śleṣmā śroto limpet tato bhavet
ruggauravaṃ pidhānaṃ ca sa pratīnāhasaṃjñitaḥ
kaṇḍūśophau kaphācchrotre sthirau tatsaṃjñayā smṛtau
kapho vidagdhaḥ pittena sarujaṃ nīrujaṃ tvapi
ghanapūtibahukledaṃ kurute pūtikarṇakam
vātādidūṣitaṃ śrotraṃ māṃsāsṛkkledajā rujam
khādanto jantavaḥ kuryustīvrāṃ sa kṛmikarṇakaḥ
śrotrakaṇḍūyanājjāte kṣate syāt pūrvalakṣaṇaḥ
vidradhiḥ pūrvavaccānyaḥ śopho 'rśo 'rbudam īritam
teṣu ruk pūtikarṇatvaṃ badhiratvaṃ ca bādhate
garbhe 'nilāt saṃkucitā śaṣkulī kucikarṇakaḥ
eko nīrug aneko vā garbhe māṃsāṅkuraḥ sthiraḥ
pippalī pippalīmānaḥ saṃnipātād vidārikā
savarṇaḥ sarujaḥ stabdhaḥ śvayathuḥ sa upekṣitaḥ
kaṭutailanibhaṃ pakvaḥ sravet kṛcchreṇa rohati
saṃkocayati rūḍhā ca sā dhruvaṃ karṇaśaṣkulīm
sirāsthaḥ kurute vāyuḥ pālīśoṣaṃ tadāhvayam
kṛśā dṛḍhā ca tantrīvat pālī vātena tantrikā
sukumāre cirotsargāt sahasaiva pravardhite
karṇe śophaḥ saruk pālyām aruṇaḥ paripoṭavān
paripoṭaḥ sa pavanād utpātaḥ pittaśoṇitāt
gurvābharaṇabhārādyaiḥ śyāvo rugdāhapākavān
śvayathuḥ sphoṭapiṭikārāgoṣākledasaṃyutaḥ
pālyāṃ śopho 'nilakaphāt sarvato nirvyathaḥ sthiraḥ
stabdhaḥ savarṇaḥ kaṇḍūmān unmantho galliraśca saḥ
durviddhe vardhite karṇe sakaṇḍūdāhapākaruk
śvayathuḥ saṃnipātotthaḥ sa nāmnā duḥkhavardhanaḥ
kaphāsṛkkṛmijāḥ sūkṣmāḥ sakaṇḍūkledavedanāḥ
lihyuḥ pālīm upekṣitāḥ lehyākhyāḥ piṭikāstā hi
pippalī sarvajaṃ śūlaṃ vidārī kucikarṇakaḥ
eṣām asādhyā yāpyaikā tantrikānyāṃstu sādhayet
pañcaviṃśatirityuktāḥ karṇarogā vibhāgataḥ
athātaḥ karṇarogapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
karṇaśūle pavanaje pibed rātrau rasāśitaḥ
vātaghnasādhitaṃ sarpiḥ karṇaṃ svinnaṃ ca pūrayet
pattrāṇāṃ pṛthag aśvatthabilvārkairaṇḍajanmanām
tailasindhūtthadigdhānāṃ svinnānāṃ puṭapākataḥ
rasaiḥ kavoṣṇaistadvacca mūlakasyāralorapi
gaṇe vātahare 'mleṣu mūtreṣu ca vipācitaḥ
mahāsneho drutaṃ hanti sutīvrām api vedanām
mahataḥ pañcamūlasya kāṣṭhāt kṣaumeṇa veṣṭitāt
tailasiktāt pradīptāgrāt snehaḥ sadyo rujāpahaḥ
yojyaścaivaṃ bhadrakāṣṭhāt kuṣṭhāt kāṣṭhācca sāralāt
vātavyādhipratiśyāyavihitaṃ hitam atra ca
varjayecchirasā snānaṃ śītāmbhaḥpānam ahnyapi
pittaśūle sitāyuktaghṛtasnigdhaṃ virecayet
drākṣāyaṣṭīśṛtaṃ stanyaṃ śasyate karṇapūraṇam
yaṣṭyanantāhimośīrakākolīlodhrajīvakaiḥ
mṛṇālabisamañjiṣṭhāśārivābhiśca sādhayet
yaṣṭīmadhurasaprasthakṣīradviprasthasaṃyutam
tailasya kuḍavaṃ nasyapūraṇābhyañjanairidam
nihanti śūladāhoṣāḥ kevalaṃ kṣaudram eva vā
yaṣṭyādibhiśca saghṛtaiḥ karṇau dihyāt samantataḥ
vāmayet pippalīsiddhasarpiḥsnigdhaṃ kaphodbhave
dhūmanāvanagaṇḍūṣasvedān kuryāt kaphāpahān
laśunārdrakaśigrūṇāṃ muraṅgyā mūlakasya ca
kadalyāḥ svarasaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kaduṣṇaḥ karṇapūraṇe
arkāṅkurān amlapiṣṭāṃstailāktāṃllavaṇānvitān
saṃnidhāya snuhīkāṇḍe korite tacchadāvṛtān
svedayet puṭapākena sa rasaḥ śūlajit param
rasena bījapūrasya kapitthasya ca pūrayet
śuktena pūrayitvā vā phenenānvavacūrṇayet
ajāvimūtravaṃśatvaksiddhaṃ tailaṃ ca pūraṇam
siddhaṃ vā sārṣapaṃ tailaṃ hiṅgutumburunāgaraiḥ
raktaje pittavat kāryaṃ sirāṃ cāśu vimokṣayet
pakve pūyavahe karṇe dhūmagaṇḍūṣanāvanam
yuñjyān nāḍīvidhānaṃ ca duṣṭavraṇaharaṃ ca yat
srotaḥ pramṛjya digdhaṃ tu dvau kālau picuvartibhiḥ
pureṇa dhūpayitvā tu mākṣikeṇa prapūrayet
surasādigaṇakvāthaphāṇitāktāṃ ca yojayet
picuvartiṃ susūkṣmaiśca taccūrṇairavacūrṇayet
śūlakledagurutvānāṃ vidhireṣa nivartakaḥ
priyaṅgumadhukāmbaṣṭhādhātakyutpalaparṇibhiḥ
mañjiṣṭhālodhralākṣābhiḥ kapitthasya rasena ca
pacet tailaṃ tad āsrāvaṃ nigṛhṇātyāśu pūraṇāt
nādabādhiryayoḥ kuryād vātaśūloktam auṣadham
śleṣmānubandhe śleṣmāṇam prāg jayed vamanādibhiḥ
eraṇḍaśigruvaruṇamūlakāt pattraje rase
caturguṇe pacet tailaṃ kṣīre cāṣṭaguṇonmite
yaṣṭyāhvākṣīrakākolīkalkayuktaṃ nihanti tat
nādabādhiryaśūlāni nāvanābhyaṅgapūraṇaiḥ
pakvaṃ prativiṣāhiṅgumiśitvaksvarjikoṣaṇaiḥ
saśuktaiḥ pūraṇāt tailaṃ ruksrāvāśrutinādanut
karṇanāde hitaṃ tailaṃ sarṣapotthaṃ ca pūraṇe
śuṣkamūlakakhaṇḍānāṃ kṣāro hiṅgu mahauṣadham
śatapuṣpāvacākuṣṭhadāruśigrurasāñjanam
sauvarcalayavakṣārasvarjikaudbhidasaindhavam
bhūrjagranthiviḍaṃ mustā madhuśuktaṃ caturguṇam
mātuluṅgarasastadvat kadalīsvarasaśca taiḥ
pakvaṃ tailaṃ jayatyāśu sukṛcchrān api pūraṇāt
kaṇḍūṃ kledaṃ ca bādhiryapūtikarṇatvarukkṛmīn
kṣāratailam idaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ mukhadantāmayeṣu ca
atha suptāviva syātāṃ karṇau raktaṃ haret tataḥ
saśophakledayor mandaśruter vamanam ācaret
bādhiryaṃ varjayed bālavṛddhayościrajaṃ ca yat
pratīnāhe parikledya snehasvedair viśodhayet
karṇaśodhanakenānu karṇaṃ tailasya pūrayet
saśuktasaindhavamadhor mātuluṅgarasasya vā
śodhanād rūkṣatotpattau ghṛtamaṇḍasya pūraṇam
kramo 'yaṃ malapūrṇe 'pi karṇe kaṇḍvāṃ kaphāpaham
nasyādi tadvacchophe 'pi kaṭūṣṇaiścātra lepanam
karṇasrāvoditaṃ kuryāt pūtikṛmiṇakarṇayoḥ
pūraṇaṃ kaṭutailena viśeṣāt kṛmikarṇake
vamipūrvā hitā karṇavidradhau vidradhikriyā
pittotthakarṇaśūloktaṃ kartavyaṃ kṣatavidradhau
arśo'rbudeṣu nāsāvad āmā karṇavidārikā
karṇavidradhivat sādhyā yathādoṣodayena ca
pālīśoṣe 'nilaśrotraśūlavan nasyalepanam
svedaṃ ca kuryāt svinnāṃ ca pālīm udvartayet tilaiḥ
priyālabījayaṣṭyāhvahayagandhāyavānvitaiḥ
tataḥ puṣṭikaraiḥ snehairabhyaṅgaṃ nityam ācaret
śatāvarīvājigandhāpayasyairaṇḍajīvakaiḥ
tailaṃ vipakvaṃ sakṣīraṃ pālīnāṃ puṣṭikṛt param
kalkena jīvanīyena tailaṃ payasi pācitam
ānūpamāṃsakvāthe ca pālīpoṣaṇavardhanam
pālīṃ chittvātisaṃkṣīṇāṃ śeṣāṃ saṃdhāya poṣayet
yāpyaivaṃ tantrikākhyāpi paripoṭe 'pyayaṃ vidhiḥ
utpāte śītalair lepo jalaukohṛtaśoṇite
jambvāmrapallavabalāyaṣṭīlodhratilotpalaiḥ
sadhānyāmlaiḥ samañjiṣṭhaiḥ sakadambaiḥ saśārivaiḥ
siddham abhyañjane tailaṃ visarpoktaghṛtāni ca
unmanthe 'bhyañjanaṃ tailaṃ godhākarkavasānvitam
tālapattryaśvagandhārkavākucīphalasaindhavaiḥ
surasālāṅgalībhyāṃ ca siddhaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ ca nāvanam
durviddhe 'śmantajambvāmrapattrakvāthena secitām
tailena pālīṃ svabhyaktāṃ suślakṣṇairavacūrṇayet
cūrṇair madhukamañjiṣṭhāprapuṇḍrāhvaniśodbhavaiḥ
lākṣāviḍaṅgasiddhaṃ ca tailam abhyañjane hitam
svinnāṃ gomayajaiḥ piṇḍair bahuśaḥ parilehikām
viḍaṅgasārairālimped urabhrīmūtrakalkitaiḥ
kauṭajeṅgudakārañjabījaśamyākavalkalaiḥ
athavābhyañjanaṃ tair vā kaṭutailaṃ vipācayet
sanimbapattramaricamadanair lehikāvraṇe
chinnaṃ tu karṇaṃ śuddhasya bandham ālocya yaugikam
śuddhāsraṃ lāgayellagne sadyaśchinne viśodhanam
atha grathitvā keśāntaṃ kṛtvā chedanalekhanam
niveśya saṃdhiṃ suṣamaṃ na nimnaṃ na samunnatam
abhyajya madhusarpirbhyāṃ picuplotāvaguṇṭhitam
sūtreṇāgāḍhaśithilaṃ baddhvā cūrṇairavākiret
śoṇitasthāpanair vraṇyam ācāraṃ cādiśet tataḥ
saptāhād āmatailāktaṃ śanairapanayet picum
surūḍhaṃ jātaromāṇaṃ śliṣṭasaṃdhiṃ samaṃ sthiram
suvarṣmāṇam arogaṃ ca śanaiḥ karṇaṃ vivardhayet
jalaśūkaḥ svayaṅguptā rajanyau bṛhatīphalam
aśvagandhābalāhastipippalīgaurasarṣapāḥ
mūlaṃ kośātakāśvaghnarūpikāsaptaparṇajam
chucchundarī kālamṛtā gṛhaṃ madhukarīkṛtam
jatūkā jalajanmā ca tathā śabarakandakam
ebhiḥ kalkaiḥ kharaṃ pakvaṃ satailaṃ māhiṣaṃ ghṛtam
hastyaśvamūtreṇa param abhyaṅgāt karṇavardhanam
atha kuryād vayaḥsthasya chinnāṃ śuddhasya nāsikām
chindyān nāsāsamaṃ pattraṃ tattulyaṃ ca kapolataḥ
tvaṅmāṃsaṃ nāsikāsanne rakṣaṃs tattanutāṃ nayet
sīvyed gaṇḍaṃ tataḥ sūcyā sevinyā picuyuktayā
nāsāchede 'tha likhite parivartyopari tvacam
kapolavadhraṃ saṃdadhyāt sīvyen nāsāṃ ca yatnataḥ
nāḍībhyām utkṣiped antaḥ sukhocchvāsapravṛttaye
āmatailena siktvānu pattaṅgamadhukāñjanaiḥ
śoṇitasthāpanaiścānyaiḥ suślakṣṇairavacūrṇayet
tato madhughṛtābhyaktaṃ baddhvācārikam ādiśet
jñātvāvasthāntaraṃ kuryāt sadyovraṇavidhiṃ tataḥ
chindyād rūḍhe 'dhikaṃ māṃsaṃ nāsopāntācca carma tat
sīvyet tataśca suślakṣṇaṃ hīnaṃ saṃvardhayet punaḥ
niveśite yathānyāsaṃ sadyaśchinne 'pyayaṃ vidhiḥ
nāḍīyogād vinauṣṭhasya nāsāsaṃdhānavad vidhiḥ
athāto nāsārogavijñānīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
avaśyāyānilarajobhāṣyātisvapnajāgaraiḥ
nīcātyuccopadhānena pītenānyena vāriṇā
atyambupānaramaṇacchardibāṣpagrahādibhiḥ
kruddhā vātolbaṇā doṣā nāsāyāṃ styānatāṃ gatāḥ
janayanti pratiśyāyaṃ vardhamānaṃ kṣayapradam
tatra vātāt pratiśyāye mukhaśoṣo bhṛśaṃ kṣavaḥ
ghrāṇoparodhanistodadantaśaṅkhaśirovyathāḥ
kīṭikā iva sarpantīr manyate parito bhruvau
svarasādaścirāt pākaḥ śiśirācchakaphasrutiḥ
pittāt tṛṣṇājvaraghrāṇapiṭikāsaṃbhavabhramāḥ
nāsāgrapāko rūkṣoṣṇatāmrapītakaphasrutiḥ
kaphāt kāso 'ruciḥ śvāso vamathur gātragauravam
mādhuryaṃ vadane kaṇḍūḥ snigdhaśuklakaphasrutiḥ
sarvajo lakṣaṇaiḥ sarvairakasmād vṛddhiśāntimān
duṣṭaṃ nāsāsirāḥ prāpya pratiśyāyaṃ karotyasṛk
urasaḥ suptatā tāmranetratvaṃ śvāsapūtitā
kaṇḍūḥ śrotrākṣināsāsu pittoktaṃ cātra lakṣaṇam
sarva eva pratiśyāyā duṣṭatāṃ yāntyupekṣitāḥ
yathoktopadravādhikyāt sa sarvendriyatāpanaḥ
sāgnisādajvaraśvāsakāsoraḥpārśvavedanaḥ
kupyatyakasmād bahuśo mukhadaurgandhyaśophakṛt
nāsikākledasaṃśoṣaśuddhirodhakaro muhuḥ
pūyopamāsitāraktagrathitaśleṣmasaṃsrutiḥ
mūrchanti cātra kṛmayo dīrghasnigdhasitāṇavaḥ
pakvaliṅgāni teṣvaṅgalāghavaṃ kṣavathoḥ śamaḥ
śleṣmā sacikkaṇaḥ pīto 'jñānaṃ ca rasagandhayoḥ
tīkṣṇāghrāṇopayogārkaraśmisūtratṛṇādibhiḥ
vātakopibhiranyair vā nāsikātaruṇāsthani
vighaṭṭite 'nilaḥ kruddho ruddhaḥ śṛṅgāṭakaṃ vrajet
nivṛttaḥ kurute 'tyarthaṃ kṣavathuṃ sa bhṛśakṣavaḥ
śoṣayan nāsikāsrotaḥ kaphaṃ ca kurute 'nilaḥ
śūkapūrṇābhanāsātvaṃ kṛcchrād ucchvasanaṃ tataḥ
smṛto 'sau nāsikāśoṣo nāsānāhe tu jāyate
naddhatvam iva nāsāyāḥ śleṣmaruddhena vāyunā
niḥśvāsocchvāsasaṃrodhāt srotasī saṃvṛte iva
pacen nāsāpuṭe pittaṃ tvaṅmāṃsaṃ dāhaśūlavat
sa ghrāṇapākaḥ srāvastu tatsaṃjñaḥ śleṣmasaṃbhavaḥ
accho jalopamo 'jasraṃ viśeṣānniśi jāyate
kaphaḥ pravṛddho nāsāyāṃ ruddhvā srotāṃsyapīnasam
kuryāt saghurghuraśvāsaṃ pīnasādhikavedanam
averiva sravatyasya praklinnā tena nāsikā
ajasraṃ picchilaṃ pītaṃ pakvaṃ siṅghāṇakaṃ ghanam
raktena nāsā dagdheva bāhyāntaḥsparśanāsahā
bhaveddhūmopamocchvāsā sā dīptir dahatīva ca
tālumūle malair duṣṭair māruto mukhanāsikāt
śleṣmā ca pūtir nirgacchet pūtināsaṃ vadanti tam
nicayād abhighātād vā pūyāsṛṅ nāsikā sravet
tat pūyaraktam ākhyātaṃ śirodāharujākaram
pittaśleṣmāvaruddho 'ntar nāsāyāṃ śoṣayen marut
kaphaṃ sa śuṣkaḥ puṭatāṃ prāpnoti puṭakaṃ tu tat
arśo'rbudāni vibhajed doṣaliṅgair yathāyatham
sarveṣu kṛcchrocchvasanaṃ pīnasaḥ pratataṃ kṣutiḥ
