glānir moho 'tisāro vā tacchaṅkāviṣam ucyate
tudyate saviṣo daṃśaḥ kaṇḍūśopharujānvitaḥ
dahyate grathitaḥ kiṃcid viparītastu nirviṣaḥ
pūrve darvīkṛtāṃ vege duṣṭaṃ śyāvībhavatyasṛk
śyāvatā tena vaktrādau sarpantīva ca kīṭakāḥ
dvitīye granthayo vege tṛtīye mūrdhni gauravam
dṛgrodho daṃśavikledaścaturthe ṣṭhīvanaṃ vamiḥ
saṃdhiviśleṣaṇaṃ tandrā pañcame parvabhedanam
dāho hidhmā ca ṣaṣṭhe tu hṛtpīḍā gātragauravam
mūrchāvipāko 'tīsāraḥ prāpya śukraṃ tu saptame
skandhapṛṣṭhakaṭībhaṅgaḥ sarvaceṣṭānivartanam
atha maṇḍalidaṣṭasya duṣṭaṃ pītībhavatyasṛk
tena pītāṅgatā dāho dvitīye śvayathūdbhavaḥ
tṛtīye daṃśavikledaḥ svedastṛṣṇā ca jāyate
caturthe jvaryate dāhaḥ pañcame sarvagātragaḥ
daṣṭasya rājilair duṣṭaṃ pāṇḍutāṃ yāti śoṇitam
pāṇḍutā tena gātrāṇāṃ dvitīye gurutāti ca
tṛtīye daṃśavikledo nāsikākṣimukhasravāḥ
caturthe garimā mūrdhno manyāstambhaśca pañcame
gātrabhaṅgo jvaraḥ śītaḥ śeṣayoḥ pūrvavad vadet
kuryāt pañcasu vegeṣu cikitsāṃ na tataḥ param
jalāplutā ratikṣīṇā bhītā nakulanirjitāḥ
śītavātātapavyādhikṣuttṛṣṇāśramapīḍitāḥ
tūrṇaṃ deśāntarāyātā vimuktaviṣakañcukāḥ
kuśauṣadhikaṇṭakavad ye caranti ca kānanam
deśaṃ ca divyādhyuṣitaṃ sarpāste 'lpaviṣā matāḥ
śmaśānaciticaityādau pañcamīpakṣasaṃdhiṣu
aṣṭamīnavamīsaṃdhyāmadhyarātridineṣu ca
yāmyāgneyamaghāśleṣāviśākhāpūrvanairṛte
nairṛtākhye muhūrte ca daṣṭaṃ marmasu ca tyajet
daṣṭamātraḥ sitāsyākṣaḥ śīryamāṇaśiroruhaḥ
stabdhajihvo muhur mūrchan śītocchvāso na jīvati
hidhmā śvāso vamiḥ kāso daṣṭamātrasya dehinaḥ
jāyante yugapad yasya sa hṛcchūlī na jīvati
phenaṃ vamati niḥsaṃjñaḥ śyāvapādakarānanaḥ
nāsāvasādo bhaṅgo 'ṅge viḍbhedaḥ ślathasaṃdhitā
viṣapītasya daṣṭasya digdhenābhihatasya ca
bhavantyetāni rūpāṇi samprāpte jīvitakṣaye
na nasyaiścetanā tīkṣṇair na kṣatāt kṣatajāgamaḥ
daṇḍāhatasya no rājī prayātasya yamāntikam
ato 'nyathā tu tvarayā pradīptāgāravad bhiṣak
rakṣan kaṇṭhagatān prāṇān viṣam āśu śamaṃ nayet
mātrāśataṃ viṣaṃ sthitvā daṃśe daṣṭasya dehinaḥ
dehaṃ prakramate dhātūn rudhirādīn pradūṣayan
etasminn antare karma daṃśasyotkartanādikam
kuryācchīghraṃ yathā dehe viṣavallī na rohati
daṣṭamātro daśed āśu tam eva pavanāśinam
loṣṭaṃ mahīṃ vā daśanaiśchittvā cānu sasaṃbhramam
niṣṭhīvena samālimped daṃśaṃ karṇamalena vā
daṃśasyopari badhnīyād ariṣṭāṃ caturaṅgule
kṣaumādibhir veṇikayā siddhair mantraiśca mantravit
ambuvat setubandhena bandhena stabhyate viṣam
na vahanti sirāścāsya viṣaṃ bandhābhipīḍitāḥ
niṣpīḍyānūddhared daṃśaṃ marmasaṃdhyagataṃ tathā
na jāyate viṣād vego bījanāśād ivāṅkuraḥ
daṃśaṃ maṇḍalināṃ muktvā pittalatvād athāparam
prataptair hemalohādyair dahed āśūlmukena vā
karoti bhasmasāt sadyo vahniḥ kiṃ nāma tu kṣatam
ācūṣet pūrṇavaktro vā mṛdbhasmāgadagomayaiḥ
pracchāyāntarariṣṭāyāṃ māṃsalaṃ tu viśeṣataḥ
aṅgaṃ sahaiva daṃśena lepayed agadair muhuḥ
candanośīrayuktena salilena ca secayet
viṣe pravisṛte vidhyet sirāṃ sā paramā kriyā
rakte nirhriyamāṇe hi kṛtsnaṃ nirhriyate viṣam
durgandhaṃ saviṣaṃ raktam agnau caṭacaṭāyate
yathādoṣaṃ viśuddhaṃ ca pūrvavallakṣayed asṛk
sirāsvadṛśyamānāsu yojyāḥ śṛṅgajalaukasaḥ
śoṇitaṃ srutaśeṣaṃ ca pravilīnaṃ viṣoṣmaṇā
lepasekaiḥ subahuśaḥ stambhayed bhṛśaśītalaiḥ
askanne viṣavegāddhi mūrchāyamadahṛddravāḥ
bhavanti tān jayecchītair vījeccāromaharṣataḥ
skanne tu rudhire sadyo viṣavegaḥ praśāmyati
viṣaṃ karṣati tīkṣṇatvāddhṛdayaṃ tasya guptaye
pibed ghṛtaṃ ghṛtakṣaudram agadaṃ vā ghṛtāplutam
hṛdayāvaraṇe cāsya śleṣmā hṛdyupacīyate
pravṛttagauravotkleśahṛllāsaṃ vāmayet tataḥ
dravaiḥ kāñjikakaulatthatailamadyādivarjitaiḥ
vamanair viṣahṛdbhiśca naivaṃ vyāpnoti tad vapuḥ
bhujaṅgadoṣaprakṛtisthānavegaviśeṣataḥ
susūkṣmaṃ samyag ālocya viśiṣṭāṃ cācaret kriyām
sindhuvāritamūlāni śvetā ca girikarṇikā
pānaṃ darvīkarair daṣṭe nasyaṃ madhu sapākalam
kṛṣṇasarpeṇa daṣṭasya limped daṃśaṃ hṛte 'sṛji
cāraṭīnākulībhyāṃ vā tīkṣṇamūlaviṣeṇa vā
pānaṃ ca kṣaudramañjiṣṭhāgṛhadhūmayutaṃ ghṛtam
taṇḍulīyakakāśmaryakiṇihīgirikarṇikāḥ
mātuluṅgī sitā śeluḥ pānanasyāñjanair hitaḥ
agadaḥ phaṇināṃ ghore viṣe rājīmatām api
samāḥ sugandhāmṛdvīkāśvetākhyāgajadantikāḥ
ardhāṃśaṃ saurasaṃ pattraṃ kapitthaṃ bilvadāḍimam
sakṣaudro maṇḍaliviṣe viśeṣād agado hitaḥ
pañcavalkavarāyaṣṭīnāgapuṣpailavālukam
jīvakarṣabhakau śītaṃ sitā padmakam utpalam
sakṣaudro himavān nāma hanti maṇḍalināṃ viṣam
lepācchvayathuvīsarpavisphoṭajvaradāhahā
kāśmaryaṃ vaṭaśuṅgāni jīvakarṣabhakau sitā
mañjiṣṭhā madhukaṃ ceti daṣṭo maṇḍalinā pibet
vaṃśatvagbījakaṭukāpāṭalībījanāgaram
śirīṣabījātiviṣe mūlaṃ gāvedhukaṃ vacā
piṣṭo govāriṇāṣṭāṅgo hanti gonasajaṃ viṣam
kaṭukātiviṣākuṣṭhagṛhadhūmahareṇukāḥ
sakṣaudravyoṣatagarā ghnanti rājīmatāṃ viṣam
nikhanet kāṇḍacitrāyā daṃśaṃ yāmadvayaṃ bhuvi
uddhṛtya pracchitaṃ sarpirdhānyamṛdbhyāṃ pralepayet
pibet purāṇaṃ ca ghṛtaṃ varācūrṇāvacūrṇitam
jīrṇe virikto bhuñjīta yavānnaṃ sūpasaṃskṛtam
karavīrārkakusumamūlalāṅgalikākaṇāḥ
kalkayed āranālena pāṭhāmaricasaṃyutāḥ
eṣa vyantaradaṣṭānām agadaḥ sārvakārmikaḥ
śirīṣapuṣpasvarase saptāhvaṃ maricaṃ sitam
bhāvitaṃ sarpadaṣṭānāṃ pānanasyāñjane hitam
dvipalaṃ natakuṣṭhābhyāṃ ghṛtakṣaudraṃ catuḥpalam
api takṣakadaṣṭānāṃ pānam etat sukhapradam
atha darvīkṛtāṃ vege pūrve visrāvya śoṇitam
agadaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ saṃyuktaṃ tvaritaṃ pibet
dvitīye vamanaṃ kṛtvā tadvad evāgadaṃ pibet
viṣāpahe prayuñjīta tṛtīye 'ñjananāvane
pibeccaturthe pūrvoktāṃ yavāgūṃ vamane kṛte
ṣaṣṭhapañcamayoḥ śītair digdhaṃ siktam abhīkṣṇaśaḥ
pāyayed vamanaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ yavāgūṃ ca viṣāpahaiḥ
agadaṃ saptame tīkṣṇaṃ yuñjyād añjananasyayoḥ
kṛtvāvagāḍhaṃ śastreṇa mūrdhni kākapadaṃ tataḥ
māṃsaṃ sarudhiraṃ tasya carma vā tatra nikṣipet
tṛtīye vamitaḥ peyāṃ vege maṇḍalināṃ pibet
atīkṣṇam agadaṃ ṣaṣṭhe gaṇaṃ vā padmakādikam
ādye 'vagāḍhaṃ pracchāya vege daṣṭasya rājilaiḥ
alābunā hared raktaṃ pūrvavaccāgadaṃ pibet
ṣaṣṭhe 'ñjanaṃ tīkṣṇatamam avapīḍaṃ ca yojayet
anukteṣu ca vegeṣu kriyāṃ darvīkaroditām
garbhiṇībālavṛddheṣu mṛduṃ vidhyet sirāṃ na ca
tvaṅ manohvā niśe vakraṃ rasaḥ śārdūlajo nakhaḥ
tamālaḥ kesaraṃ śītaṃ pītaṃ taṇḍulavāriṇā
hanti sarvaviṣāṇyetad vajraṃ vajram ivāsurān
bilvasya mūlaṃ surasasya puṣpaṃ phalaṃ karañjasya nataṃ surāhvam
phalatrikaṃ vyoṣaniśādvayaṃ ca bastasya mūtreṇa susūkṣmapiṣṭam
bhujaṅgalūtonduravṛścikādyair viṣūcikājīrṇagarajvaraiśca
ārtān narān bhūtavidharṣitāṃśca svasthīkarotyañjanapānanasyaiḥ
pralepādyaiśca niḥśeṣaṃ daṃśād apyuddhared viṣam
bhūyo vegāya jāyeta śeṣaṃ dūṣīviṣāya vā
viṣāpāye 'nilaṃ kruddhaṃ snehādibhirupācaret
tailamadyakulatthāmlavarjyaiḥ pavananāśanaiḥ
pittaṃ pittajvaraharaiḥ kaṣāyasnehavastibhiḥ
samākṣikeṇa vargeṇa kapham āragvadhādinā
sitā vaigandhiko drākṣā payasyā madhukaṃ madhu
pānaṃ samantrapūtāmbu prokṣaṇaṃ sāntvaharṣaṇam
sarpāṅgābhihate yuñjyāt tathā śaṅkāviṣārdite
karketanaṃ marakataṃ vajraṃ vāraṇamauktikam
vaiḍūryaṃ gardabhamaṇiṃ picukaṃ viṣamūṣikām
himavadgirisambhūtāṃ somarājīṃ punarnavām
tathā droṇāṃ mahādroṇāṃ mānasīṃ sarpajaṃ maṇim
viṣāṇi viṣaśāntyarthaṃ vīryavanti ca dhārayet
chattrī jharjharapāṇiśca cared rātrau viśeṣataḥ
tacchāyāśabdavitrastāḥ praṇaśyanti bhujaṅgamāḥ
athātaḥ kīṭalūtādiviṣapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
sarpāṇām eva viṇmūtraśukrāṇḍaśavakothajāḥ
doṣair vyastaiḥ samastaiśca yuktāḥ kīṭāścaturvidhāḥ
daṣṭasya kīṭair vāyavyair daṃśastodarujolbaṇaḥ
āgneyairalpasaṃsrāvo dāharāgavisarpavān
pakvapīluphalaprakhyaḥ kharjūrasadṛśo 'thavā
kaphādhikair mandarujaḥ pakvodumbarasaṃnibhaḥ
srāvāḍhyaḥ sarvaliṅgastu vivarjyaḥ sāṃnipātikaiḥ
vegāśca sarpavacchopho vardhiṣṇur visraraktatā
śiro'kṣigauravaṃ mūrchā bhramaḥ śvāso 'tivedanā
sarveṣāṃ karṇikā śopho jvaraḥ kaṇḍūrarocakaḥ
vṛścikasya viṣaṃ tīkṣṇam ādau dahati vahnivat
ūrdhvam ārohati kṣipraṃ daṃśe paścāt tu tiṣṭhati
daṃśaḥ sadyo 'tiruk śyāvastudyate sphuṭatīva ca
te gavādiśakṛtkothād digdhadaṣṭādikothataḥ
sarpakothācca sambhūtā mandamadhyamahāviṣāḥ
mandāḥ pītāḥ sitāḥ śyāvā rūkṣāḥ karburamecakāḥ
romaśā bahuparvāṇo lohitāḥ pāṇḍurodarāḥ
dhūmrodarāstriparvāṇo madhyāstu kapilāruṇāḥ
piśaṅgāḥ śabarāścitrāḥ śoṇitābhā mahāviṣāḥ
agnyābhā dvyekaparvāṇo raktāsitasitodarāḥ
tair daṣṭaḥ śūnarasanaḥ stabdhagātro jvarārditaḥ
khair vamañchoṇitaṃ kṛṣṇam indriyārthān asaṃvidan
svidyan mūrchan viśuṣkāsyo vihvalo vedanāturaḥ
viśīryamāṇamāṃsaśca prāyaśo vijahātyasūn
ucciṭiṅgastu vaktreṇa daśatyabhyadhikavyathaḥ
sādhyato vṛścikāt stambhaṃ śephaso hṛṣṭaromatām
karoti sekam aṅgānāṃ daṃśaḥ śītāmbuneva ca
uṣṭradhūmaḥ sa evokto rātricārācca rātrikaḥ
vātapittottarāḥ kīṭāḥ ślaiṣmikāḥ kaṇabhondurāḥ
prāyo vātolbaṇaviṣā vṛścikāḥ soṣṭradhūmakāḥ
yasya yasyaiva doṣasya liṅgādhikyaṃ pratarkayet
tasya tasyauṣadhaiḥ kuryād viparītaguṇaiḥ kriyām
hṛtpīḍordhvānilastambhaḥ sirāyāmo 'sthiparvaruk
ghūrṇanodveṣṭanaṃ gātraśyāvatā vātike viṣe
saṃjñānāśoṣṇaniśvāsau hṛddāhaḥ kaṭukāsyatā
māṃsāvadaraṇaṃ śopho raktapītaśca paittike
chardyarocakahṛllāsaprasekotkleśapīnasaiḥ
saśaityamukhamādhuryair vidyācchleṣmādhikaṃ viṣam
piṇyākena vraṇālepastailābhyaṅgaśca vātike
svedo nāḍīpulākādyair bṛṃhaṇaśca vidhir hitaḥ
paittikaṃ stambhayet sekaiḥ pradehaiścātiśītalaiḥ
lekhanacchedanasvedavamanaiḥ ślaiṣmikaṃ jayet
kīṭānāṃ triprakārāṇāṃ traividhyena kriyā hitā
svedālepanasekāṃstu koṣṇān prāyo 'vacārayet
anyatra mūrchitād daṃśapākataḥ kothato 'thavā
nṛkeśāḥ sarṣapāḥ pītā guḍo jīrṇaśca dhūpanam
viṣadaṃśasya sarvasya kāśyapaḥ param abravīt
viṣaghnaṃ ca vidhiṃ sarvaṃ kuryāt saṃśodhanāni ca
sādhayet sarpavad daṣṭān viṣograiḥ kīṭavṛścikaiḥ
taṇḍulīyakatulyāṃśāṃ trivṛtāṃ sarpiṣā pibet
yāti kīṭaviṣaiḥ kampaṃ na kailāsa ivānilaiḥ
kṣīrivṛkṣatvagālepaḥ śuddhe kīṭaviṣāpahaḥ
muktālepo varaḥ śophatodadāhajvarapraṇut
vacāhiṅguviḍaṅgāni saindhavaṃ gajapippalī
pāṭhā prativiṣā vyoṣaṃ kāśyapena vinirmitam
daśāṅgam agadaṃ pītvā sarvakīṭaviṣaṃ jayet
sadyo vṛścikajaṃ daṃśaṃ cakratailena secayet
vidārigandhāsiddhena kavoṣṇenetareṇa vā
lavaṇottamayuktena sarpiṣā vā punaḥ punaḥ
siñcet koṣṇāranālena sakṣīralavaṇena vā
upanāho ghṛte bhṛṣṭaḥ kalko 'jājyāḥ sasaindhavaḥ
ādaṃśaṃ sveditaṃ cūrṇaiḥ pracchāya pratisārayet
rajanīsaindhavavyoṣaśirīṣaphalapuṣpajaiḥ
mātuluṅgāmlagomūtrapiṣṭaṃ ca surasāgrajam
lepaḥ sukhoṣṇaśca hitaḥ piṇyāko gomayo 'pi vā
pāne sarpir madhuyutaṃ kṣīraṃ vā bhūriśarkaram
pārāvataśakṛt pathyā tagaraṃ viśvabheṣajam
bījapūrarasonmiśraḥ paramo vṛścikāgadaḥ
saśaivaloṣṭradaṃṣṭrā ca hanti vṛścikajaṃ viṣam
hiṅgunā haritālena mātuluṅgarasena ca
lepāñjanābhyāṃ guṭikā paramaṃ vṛścikāpahā
karañjārjunaśelūnāṃ kaṭabhyāḥ kuṭajasya ca
śirīṣasya ca puṣpāṇi mastunā daṃśalepanam
yo muhyati praśvasiti pralapatyugravedanaḥ
tasya pathyāniśākṛṣṇāmañjiṣṭhātiviṣoṣaṇam
sālābuvṛntaṃ vārtākarasapiṣṭaṃ pralepanam
sarvatra cogrāliviṣe pāyayed dadhisarpiṣī
vidhyet sirāṃ vidadhyācca vamanāñjananāvanam
uṣṇasnigdhāmlamadhuraṃ bhojanaṃ cānilāpaham
nāgaraṃ gṛhakapotapurīṣaṃ bījapūrakaraso haritālam
saindhavaṃ ca vinihantyagado 'yaṃ lepato 'likulajaṃ viṣam āśu
ante vṛścikadaṣṭānāṃ samudīrṇe bhṛśaṃ viṣe
viṣeṇālepayed daṃśam ucciṭiṅge 'pyayaṃ vidhiḥ
nāgapurīṣacchattraṃ rohiṣamūlaṃ ca śelutoyena
kuryād guṭikāṃ lepād iyam aliviṣanāśanī śreṣṭhā
arkasya dugdhena śirīṣabījaṃ trir bhāvitaṃ pippalicūrṇamiśram
eṣo 'gado hanti viṣāṇi kīṭabhujaṅgalūtonduravṛścikānām
śirīṣapuṣpaṃ sakarañjabījaṃ kāśmīrajaṃ kuṣṭhamanaḥśile ca
eṣo 'gado rātrikavṛścikānāṃ saṃkrāntikārī kathito jinena
kīṭebhyo dāruṇatarā lūtāḥ ṣoḍaśa tā jaguḥ
aṣṭāviṃśatirityeke tato 'pyanye tu bhūyasīḥ
sahasraraśmyanucarā vadantyanye sahasraśaḥ
bahūpadravarūpā tu lūtaikaiva viṣātmikā
rūpāṇi nāmatastasyā durjñeyānyatisaṃkarāt
nāsti sthānavyavasthā ca doṣato 'taḥ pracakṣate
kṛcchrasādhyā pṛthagdoṣairasādhyā nicayena sā
taddaṃśaḥ paittiko dāhatṛṭsphoṭajvaramohavān
bhṛśoṣmā raktapītābhaḥ kledī drākṣāphalopamaḥ
ślaiṣmikaḥ kaṭhinaḥ pāṇḍuḥ parūṣakaphalākṛtiḥ
nidrāṃ śītajvaraṃ kāsaṃ kaṇḍūṃ ca kurute bhṛśam
vātikaḥ paruṣaḥ śyāvaḥ parvabhedajvarapradaḥ
tadvibhāgaṃ yathāsvaṃ ca doṣaliṅgair vibhāvayet
asādhyāyāṃ tu hṛnmohaśvāsahidhmāśirograhāḥ
śvetapītāsitāraktāḥ piṭikāḥ śvayathūdbhavaḥ
vepathur vamathur dāhastṛḍ āndhyaṃ vakranāsatā
śyāvauṣṭhavaktradantatvaṃ pṛṣṭhagrīvāvabhañjanam
pakvajambūsavarṇaṃ ca daṃśāt sravati śoṇitam
sarvāpi sarvajā prāyo vyapadeśastu bhūyasā
tīkṣṇamadhyāvaratvena sā tridhā hantyupekṣitā
saptāhena daśāhena pakṣeṇa ca paraṃ kramāt
lūtādaṃśaśca sarvo 'pi dadrūmaṇḍalasaṃnibhaḥ
sito 'sito 'ruṇaḥ pītaḥ śyāvo vā mṛdurunnataḥ
madhye kṛṣṇo 'thavā śyāvaḥ paryante jālakāvṛtaḥ
visarpavāñchophayutas tapyate bahuvedanaḥ
jvarāśupākavikledakothāvadaraṇānvitaḥ
kledena yat spṛśatyaṅgaṃ tatrāpi kurute vraṇam
śvāsadaṃṣṭrāśakṛnmūtraśukralālānakhārtavaiḥ
aṣṭābhirudvamatyeṣā viṣaṃ vaktrād viśeṣataḥ
lūtā nābher daśatyūrdhvam ūrdhvaṃ cādhaśca kīṭakāḥ
taddūṣitaṃ ca vastrādi dehe pṛktaṃ vikārakṛt
dinārdhaṃ lakṣyate naiva daṃśo lūtāviṣodbhavaḥ
sūcīvyadhavad ābhāti tato 'sau prathame 'hani
avyaktavarṇaḥ pracalaḥ kiṃcitkaṇḍūrujānvitaḥ
dvitīye 'bhyunnato 'nteṣu piṭikairiva vācitaḥ
vyaktavarṇo nato madhye kaṇḍūmān granthisaṃnibhaḥ
tṛtīye sajvaro romaharṣakṛd raktamaṇḍalaḥ
śarāvarūpastodāḍhyo romakūpeṣu sāsravaḥ
mahāṃścaturthe śvayathustāpaśvāsabhramapradaḥ
vikārān kurute tāṃstān pañcame viṣakopajān
ṣaṣṭhe vyāpnoti marmāṇi saptame hanti jīvitam
iti tīkṣṇaṃ viṣaṃ madhyaṃ hīnaṃ ca vibhajed ataḥ
ekaviṃśatirātreṇa viṣaṃ śāmyati sarvathā
athāśu lūtādaṣṭasya śastreṇādaṃśam uddharet
dahecca jāmbavauṣṭhādyair na tu pittottaraṃ dahet
karkaśaṃ bhinnaromāṇaṃ marmasaṃdhyādisaṃśritam
prasṛtaṃ sarvato daṃśaṃ na chindīta dahen na ca
lepayed dagdham agadair madhusaindhavasaṃyutaiḥ
suśītaiḥ secayeccānu kaṣāyaiḥ kṣīrivṛkṣajaiḥ
sarvato 'pahared raktaṃ śṛṅgādyaiḥ sirayāpi vā
sekalepāstataḥ śītā bodhiśleṣmātakākṣakaiḥ
phalinīdviniśākṣaudrasarpirbhiḥ padmakāhvayaḥ
aśeṣalūtākīṭānām agadaḥ sārvakārmikaḥ
haridrādvayapattaṅgamañjiṣṭhānatakesaraiḥ
sakṣaudrasarpiḥ pūrvasmād adhikaścampakāhvayaḥ
tadvad gomayaniṣpīḍaśarkarāghṛtamākṣikaiḥ
apāmārgamanohvāladārvīdhyāmakagairikaiḥ
natailākuṣṭhamaricayaṣṭyāhvaghṛtamākṣikaiḥ
agado mandaro nāma tathānyo gandhamādanaḥ
natalodhravacākaṭvīpāṭhailāpattrakuṅkumaiḥ
viṣaghnaṃ bahudoṣeṣu prayuñjīta viśodhanam
yaṣṭyāhvamadanāṅkollajālinīsindhuvārikāḥ
kaphe jyeṣṭhāmbunā pītvā viṣam āśu samudvamet
śirīṣapattratvaṅmūlaphalaṃ vāṅkollamūlavat
virecayecca triphalānīlinītrivṛtādibhiḥ
nivṛtte dāhaśophādau karṇikāṃ pātayed vraṇāt
kusumbhapuṣpaṃ godantaḥ svarṇakṣīrī kapotaviṭ
trivṛtā saindhavaṃ dantī karṇikāpātanaṃ tathā
mūlam uttaravāruṇyā vaṃśanirlekhasaṃyutam
tadvacca saindhavaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ dantī kaṭukadaugdhikam
rājakośātakīmūlaṃ kiṇvo vā mathitodbhavaḥ
karṇikāpātasamaye bṛṃhayecca viṣāpahaiḥ
snehakāryam aśeṣaṃ ca sarpiṣaiva samācaret
viṣasya vṛddhaye tailam agneriva tṛṇolupam
hrīveravaikaṅkatagopakanyāmustāśamīcandanaṭuṇṭukāni
śaivālanīlotpalavakrayaṣṭītvaṅnākulīpadmakarāṭhamadhyam
rajanīghanasarpalocanākaṇaśuṇṭhīkaṇamūlacitrakāḥ
varuṇāgurubilvapāṭalīpicumandāmayaśelukesaram
bilvacandananatotpalaśuṇṭhīpippalīniculavetasakuṣṭham
śuktiśākavarapāṭalibhārgīsindhuvārakaraghāṭavarāṅgam
pittakaphānilalūtāḥ pānāñjananasyalepasekena
agadavarā vṛttasthāḥ kugatīriva vārayantyete
lodhraṃ sevyaṃ padmakaṃ padmareṇuḥ kālīyākhyaṃ candanaṃ yacca raktam
kāntāpuṣpaṃ dugdhinīkā mṛṇālaṃ lūtāḥ sarvā ghnanti sarvakriyābhiḥ
athāto mūṣikālarkaviṣapratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
lālanaścapalaḥ putro hasiraścikkiro 'jiraḥ
kaṣāyadantaḥ kulakaḥ kokilaḥ kapilo 'sitaḥ
aruṇaḥ śabaraḥ śvetaḥ kapotaḥ palitonduraḥ
chucchundaro rasālākhyo daśāṣṭau ceti mūṣikāḥ
śukraṃ patati yatraiṣāṃ śukradigdhaiḥ spṛśanti vā
yad aṅgam aṅgaistatrāsre dūṣite pāṇḍutāṃ gate
granthayaḥ śvayathuḥ koṭho maṇḍalāni bhramo 'ruciḥ
śītajvaro 'tiruk sādo vepathuḥ parvabhedanam
romaharṣaḥ srutir mūrchā dīrghakālānubandhanam
śleṣmānubaddhabahvākhupotakacchardanaṃ satṛṭ
vyavāyyākhuviṣaṃ kṛcchraṃ bhūyo bhūyaśca kupyati
mūrchāṅgaśophavaivarṇyakledaśabdāśrutijvarāḥ
śirogurutvaṃ lālāsṛkchardiścāsādhyalakṣaṇam
śūnavastiṃ vivarṇauṣṭham ākhvābhair granthibhiścitam
chucchundarasagandhaṃ ca varjayed ākhudūṣitam
śunaḥ śleṣmolbaṇā doṣāḥ saṃjñāṃ saṃjñāvahāśritāḥ
muṣṇantaḥ kurvate kṣobhaṃ dhātūnām atidāruṇam
lālāvān andhabadhiraḥ sarvataḥ so 'bhidhāvati
srastapucchahanuskandhaḥ śiroduḥkhī natānanaḥ
daṃśastena vidaṣṭasya suptaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ kṣaratyasṛk
hṛcchirorugjvarastambhatṛṣṇāmūrchodbhavo 'nu ca
anenānye 'pi boddhavyā vyālā daṃṣṭrāprahāriṇaḥ
śṛgālāśvatarāśvarkṣadvīpivyāghravṛkādayaḥ
kaṇḍūnistodavaivarṇyasuptikledajvarabhramāḥ
vidāharāgarukpākaśophagranthivikuñcanam
daṃśāvadaraṇaṃ sphoṭāḥ karṇikā maṇḍalāni ca
sarvatra saviṣe liṅgaṃ viparītaṃ tu nirviṣe
daṣṭo yena tu tacceṣṭārutaṃ kurvan vinaśyati
paśyaṃstam eva cākasmād ādarśasalilādiṣu
yo 'dbhyas trasyed adaṣṭo 'pi śabdasaṃsparśadarśanaiḥ
jalasaṃtrāsanāmānaṃ daṣṭaṃ tam api varjayet
ākhunā daṣṭamātrasya daṃśaṃ kāṇḍena dāhayet
darpaṇenāthavā tīvrarujā syāt karṇikānyathā
dagdhaṃ visrāvayed daṃśaṃ pracchitaṃ ca pralepayet
śirīṣarajanīvakrakuṅkumāmṛtavallibhiḥ
agāradhūmamañjiṣṭhārajanīlavaṇottamaiḥ
lepo jayatyākhuviṣaṃ karṇikāyāśca pātanaḥ
tato 'mlaiḥ kṣālayitvānu toyairanu ca lepayet
pālindīśvetakaṭabhībilvamūlaguḍūcibhiḥ
anyaiśca viṣaśophaghnaiḥ sirāṃ vā mokṣayed drutam
chardanaṃ nīlinīkvāthaiḥ śukākhyāṅkollayorapi
kośātakyāḥ śukākhyāyāḥ phalaṃ jīmūtakasya ca
madanasya ca saṃcūrṇya dadhnā pītvā viṣaṃ vamet
vacāmadanajīmūtakuṣṭhaṃ vā mūtrapeṣitam
pūrvakalpena pātavyaṃ sarvonduraviṣāpaham
virecanaṃ trivṛnnīlītriphalākalka iṣyate
śirovirecane sāraḥ śirīṣasya phalāni ca
añjanaṃ gomayaraso vyoṣasūkṣmarajo'nvitaḥ
kapitthagomayaraso madhumān avalehanam
taṇḍulīyakamūlena siddhaṃ pāne hitaṃ ghṛtam
dviniśākaṭabhīraktāyaṣṭyāhvair vāmṛtānvitaiḥ
āsphotamūlasiddhaṃ vā pañcakāpittham eva vā
sindhuvāraṃ nataṃ śigrubilvamūlaṃ punarnavā
vacāśvadaṃṣṭrājīmūtam eṣāṃ kvāthaṃ samākṣikam
pibecchālyodanaṃ dadhnā bhuñjāno mūṣikārditaḥ
takreṇa śarapuṅkhāyā bījaṃ saṃcūrṇya vā pibet
aṅkollamūlakalko vā bastamūtreṇa kalkitaḥ
pānālepanayor yuktaḥ sarvākhuviṣanāśanaḥ
kapitthamadhyatilakatilāṅkollajaṭāḥ pibet
gavāṃ mūtreṇa payasā mañjarīṃ tilakasya vā
athavā sairyakān mūlaṃ sakṣaudraṃ taṇḍulāmbunā
kaṭukālābuvinyastaṃ pītaṃ vāmbu niśoṣitam
sindhuvārasya mūlāni biḍālāsthi viṣaṃ natam
jalapiṣṭo 'gado hanti nasyādyairākhujaṃ viṣam
saśeṣaṃ mūṣikaviṣaṃ prakupyatyabhradarśane
yathāyathaṃ vā kāleṣu doṣāṇāṃ vṛddhihetuṣu
tatra sarve yathāvasthaṃ prayojyāḥ syurupakramāḥ
yathāsvaṃ ye ca nirdiṣṭāstathā dūṣīviṣāpahāḥ
daṃśaṃ tvalarkadaṣṭasya dagdham uṣṇena sarpiṣā
pradihyād agadaistaistaiḥ purāṇaṃ ca ghṛtaṃ pibet
arkakṣīrayutaṃ cāsya yojyam āśu virecanam
aṅkollottaramūlāmbu tripalaṃ sahaviḥpalam
pibet sadhattūraphalāṃ śvetāṃ vāpi punarnavām
aikadhyaṃ palalaṃ tailaṃ rūpikāyāḥ payo guḍaḥ
bhinatti viṣam ālarkaṃ ghanavṛndam ivānilaḥ
samantraṃ sauṣadhīratnaṃ snapanaṃ ca prayojayet
catuṣpādbhir dvipādbhir vā nakhadantaparikṣatam
śūyate pacyate rāgajvarasrāvarujānvitam
somavalko 'śvakarṇaśca gojihvā haṃsapādikā
rajanyau gairikaṃ lepo nakhadantaviṣāpahaḥ
dīrgham āyuḥ smṛtiṃ medhām ārogyaṃ taruṇaṃ vayaḥ
prabhāvarṇasvaraudāryaṃ dehendriyabalodayam
vāksiddhiṃ vṛṣatāṃ kāntim avāpnoti rasāyanāt
lābhopāyo hi śastānāṃ rasādīnāṃ rasāyanam
pūrve vayasi madhye vā tat prayojyaṃ jitātmanaḥ
snigdhasya srutaraktasya viśuddhasya ca sarvathā
aviśuddhe śarīre hi yukto rāsāyano vidhiḥ
vājīkaro vā maline vastre raṅga ivāphalaḥ
rasāyanānāṃ dvividhaṃ prayogam ṛṣayo viduḥ
kuṭīprāveśikaṃ mukhyaṃ vātātapikam anyathā
pure prāpyopakaraṇe harmyanirvātanirbhaye
diśy udīcyāṃ śubhe deśe trigarbhāṃ sūkṣmalocanām
dhūmātaparajovyālastrīmūrkhādyavilaṅghitām
sajjavaidyopakaraṇāṃ sumṛṣṭāṃ kārayet kuṭīm
atha puṇye 'hni sampūjya pūjyāṃs tāṃ praviśec chuciḥ
tatra saṃśodhanaiḥ śuddhaḥ sukhī jātabalaḥ punaḥ
brahmacārī dhṛtiyutaḥ śraddadhāno jitendriyaḥ
dānaśīladayāsatyavratadharmaparāyaṇaḥ
devatānusmṛtau yukto yuktasvapnaprajāgaraḥ
priyauṣadhaḥ peśalavāg ārabheta rasāyanam
harītakīm āmalakaṃ saindhavaṃ nāgaraṃ vacām
haridrāṃ pippalīṃ vellaṃ guḍaṃ coṣṇāmbunā pibet
snigdhasvinno naraḥ pūrvaṃ tena sādhu viricyate
tataḥ śuddhaśarīrāya kṛtasaṃsarjanāya ca
trirātraṃ pañcarātraṃ vā saptāhaṃ vā ghṛtānvitam
dadyād yāvakam ā śuddheḥ purāṇaśakṛto 'thavā
itthaṃ saṃskṛtakoṣṭhasya rasāyanam upāharet
yasya yad yaugikaṃ paśyet sarvam ālocya sātmyavit
pathyāsahasraṃ triguṇadhātrīphalasamanvitam
pañcānāṃ pañcamūlānāṃ sārdhaṃ palaśatadvayam
jale daśaguṇe paktvā daśabhāgasthite rase
āpothya kṛtvā vyasthīni vijayāmalakāny atha
vinīya tasmin niryūhe yojayet kuḍavāṃśakam
tvagelāmustarajanīpippalyagurucandanam
maṇḍūkaparṇīkanakaśaṅkhapuṣpīvacāplavam
yaṣṭyāhvayaṃ viḍaṅgaṃ ca cūrṇitaṃ tulayādhikam
sitopalārdhabhāraṃ ca pātrāṇi trīṇi sarpiṣaḥ
dve ca tailāt pacet sarvaṃ tad agnau lehatāṃ gatam
avatīrṇaṃ himaṃ yuñjyād viṃśaiḥ kṣaudraśatais tribhiḥ
tataḥ khajena mathitaṃ nidadhyād ghṛtabhājane
yā noparundhyād āhāram ekaṃ mātrāsya sā smṛtā
ṣaṣṭikaḥ payasā cātra jīrṇe bhojanam iṣyate
vaikhānasā vālakhilyās tathā cānye tapodhanāḥ
brahmaṇā vihitaṃ dhanyam idaṃ prāśya rasāyanam
tandrāśramaklamavalīpalitāmayavarjitāḥ
medhāsmṛtibalopetā babhūvur amitāyuṣaḥ
abhayāmalakasahasraṃ nirāmayaṃ pippalīsahasrayutam
taruṇapalāśakṣāradravīkṛtaṃ sthāpayed bhāṇḍe
upayukte ca kṣāre chāyāsaṃśuṣkacūrṇitaṃ yojyam
pādāṃśena sitāyāś caturguṇābhyāṃ madhughṛtābhyām
tad ghṛtakumbhe bhūmau nidhāya ṣaṇmāsasaṃstham uddhṛtya
prāhṇe prāśya yathānalam ucitāhāro bhavet satatam
ity upayuñjyāśeṣaṃ varṣaśatam anāmayo jarārahitaḥ
jīvati balapuṣṭivapuḥsmṛtimedhādyanvito viśeṣeṇa
nīrujārdrapalāśasya chinne śirasi tat kṣatam
antar dvihastaṃ gambhīraṃ pūryam āmalakair navaiḥ
āmūlaṃ veṣṭitaṃ darbhaiḥ padminīpaṅkalepitam
ādīpya gomayair vanyair nirvāte svedayet tataḥ
svinnāni tāny āmalakāni tṛptyā khāden naraḥ kṣaudraghṛtānvitāni
kṣīraṃ śṛtaṃ cānu pibet prakāmaṃ tenaiva varteta ca māsam ekam
varjyāni varjyāni ca tatra yatnāt spṛśyaṃ ca śītāmbu na pāṇināpi
ekādaśāhe 'sya tato vyatīte patanti keśā daśanā nakhāś ca
athālpakair eva dinaiḥ surūpaḥ strīṣv akṣayaḥ kuñjaratulyavīryaḥ
viśiṣṭamedhābalabuddhisattvo bhavaty asau varṣasahasrajīvī
daśamūlabalāmustajīvakarṣabhakotpalam
parṇinyau pippalī śṛṅgī medā tāmalakī truṭī
jīvantī joṅgakaṃ drākṣā pauṣkaraṃ candanaṃ śaṭhī
punarnavarddhikākolīkākanāsāmṛtādvayam
vidārī vṛṣamūlaṃ ca tad aikadhyaṃ palonmitam
jaladroṇe pacet pañca dhātrīphalaśatāni ca
pādaśeṣaṃ rasaṃ tasmād vyasthīny āmalakāni ca
gṛhītvā bharjayet tailaghṛtād dvādaśabhiḥ palaiḥ
matsyaṇḍikātulārdhena yuktaṃ tal lehavat pacet
snehārdhaṃ madhu siddhe tu tavakṣīryāś catuḥpalam
pippalyā dvipalaṃ dadyāc caturjātaṃ kaṇārdhitam
ato 'valehayen mātrāṃ kuṭīsthaḥ pathyabhojanaḥ
ity eṣa cyavanaprāśo yaṃ prāśya cyavano muniḥ
jarājarjarito 'py āsīn nārīnayananandanaḥ
kāsaṃ śvāsaṃ jvaraṃ śoṣaṃ hṛdrogaṃ vātaśoṇitam
mūtraśukrāśrayān doṣān vaisvaryaṃ ca vyapohati
bālavṛddhakṣatakṣīṇakṛśānām aṅgavardhanaḥ
medhāṃ smṛtiṃ kāntim anāmayatvam āyuḥprakarṣaṃ pavanānulomyam
strīṣu praharṣaṃ balam indriyāṇām agneś ca kuryād vidhinopayuktaḥ
madhukena tavakṣīryā pippalyā sindhujanmanā
pṛthag lohaiḥ suvarṇena vacayā madhusarpiṣā
sitayā vā samā yuktā samāyuktā rasāyanam
triphalā sarvarogaghnī medhāyuḥsmṛtibuddhidā
maṇḍūkaparṇyāḥ svarasaṃ yathāgni kṣīreṇa yaṣṭīmadhukasya cūrṇam
rasaṃ guḍūcyāḥ sahamūlapuṣpyāḥ kalkaṃ prayuñjīta ca śaṅkhapuṣpyāḥ
āyuḥpradāny āmayanāśanāni balāgnivarṇasvaravardhanāni
medhyāni caitāni rasāyanāni medhyā viśeṣeṇa tu śaṅkhapuṣpī
naladaṃ kaṭurohiṇī payasyā madhukaṃ candanasārivogragandhāḥ
triphalā kaṭukatrayaṃ haridre sapaṭolaṃ lavaṇaṃ ca taiḥ supiṣṭaiḥ
triguṇena rasena śaṅkhapuṣpyāḥ sapayaskaṃ ghṛtanalvaṇaṃ vipakvam
upayujya bhavej jaḍo 'pi vāgmī śrutadhārī pratibhānavān arogaḥ
peṣyair mṛṇālabisakesarapattrabījaiḥ siddhaṃ sahemaśakalaṃ payasā ca sarpiḥ
pañcāravindam iti tat prathitaṃ pṛthivyāṃ prabhraṣṭapauruṣabalapratibhair niṣevyam
yan nālakandadalakesaravad vipakvaṃ nīlotpalasya tad api prathitaṃ dvitīyam
sarpiś catuṣkuvalayaṃ sahiraṇyapattraṃ medhyaṃ gavām api bhavet kimu mānuṣāṇām
brāhmīvacāsaindhavaśaṅkhapuṣpīmatsyākṣakabrahmasuvarcalaindryaḥ
vaidehikā ca triyavāḥ pṛthak syur yavau suvarṇasya tilo viṣasya
sarpiṣaś ca palam ekata etad yojayet pariṇate ca ghṛtāḍhyam
bhojanaṃ samadhu vatsaram evaṃ śīlayann adhikadhīsmṛtimedhaḥ
atikrāntajarāvyādhitandrālasyaśramaklamaḥ
jīvaty abdaśataṃ pūrṇaṃ śrītejaḥkāntidīptimān
viśeṣataḥ kuṣṭhakilāsagulmaviṣajvaronmādagarodarāṇi
atharvamantrādikṛtāś ca kṛtyāḥ śāmyanty anenātibalāś ca vātāḥ
śaranmukhe nāgabalāṃ puṣyayoge samuddharet
akṣamātraṃ tato mūlāc cūrṇitāt payasā pibet
lihyān madhughṛtābhyāṃ vā kṣīravṛttir anannabhuk
evaṃ varṣaprayogena jīved varṣaśataṃ balī
phalonmukho gokṣurakaḥ samūlaś chāyāviśuṣkaḥ suvicūrṇitāṅgaḥ
subhāvitaḥ svena rasena tasmān mātrāṃ parāṃ prāsṛtikīṃ pibed yaḥ
kṣīreṇa tenaiva ca śālim aśnan jīrṇe bhavet sa dvitulopayogāt
śaktaḥ surūpaḥ subhagaḥ śatāyuḥ kāmī kakudmān iva gokulasthaḥ
vārāhīkandam ārdrārdraṃ kṣīreṇa kṣīrapaḥ pibet
māsaṃ niranno māsaṃ ca kṣīrānnādo jarāṃ jayet
tatkandaślakṣṇacūrṇaṃ vā svarasena subhāvitam
ghṛtakṣaudraplutaṃ lihyāt tatpakvaṃ vā ghṛtaṃ pibet
tadvad vidāryatibalābalāmadhukavāyasīḥ
śreyasīśreyasīyuktāpathyādhātrīsthirāmṛtāḥ
maṇḍūkīśaṅkhakusumāvājigandhāśatāvarīḥ
upayuñjīta medhādhīvayaḥsthairyabalapradāḥ
yathāsvaṃ citrakaḥ puṣpair jñeyaḥ pītasitāsitaiḥ
yathottaraṃ sa guṇavān vidhinā ca rasāyanam
chāyāśuṣkaṃ tato mūlaṃ māsaṃ cūrṇīkṛtaṃ lihan
sarpiṣā madhusarpirbhyāṃ piban vā payasā yatiḥ
ambhasā vā hitānnāśī śataṃ jīvati nīrujaḥ
medhāvī balavān kānto vapuṣmān dīptapāvakaḥ
tailena līḍho māsena vātān hanti sudustarān
mūtreṇa śvitrakuṣṭhāni pītas takreṇa pāyujān
bhallātakāni puṣṭāni dhānyarāśau nidhāpayet
grīṣme saṃgṛhya hemante svādusnigdhahimair vapuḥ
saṃskṛtya tāny aṣṭaguṇe salile 'ṣṭau vipācayet
aṣṭāṃśaśiṣṭaṃ tatkvāthaṃ sakṣīraṃ śītalaṃ pibet
vardhayet pratyahaṃ cānu tatraikaikam aruṣkaram
saptarātratrayaṃ yāvat trīṇi trīṇi tataḥ param
ā catvāriṃśatas tāni hrāsayed vṛddhivat tataḥ
sahasram upayuñjīta saptāhair iti saptabhiḥ
yantritātmā ghṛtakṣīraśāliṣaṣṭikabhojanaḥ
tadvat triguṇitaṃ kālaṃ prayogānte 'pi cācaret
āśiṣo labhate 'pūrvā vahner dīptiṃ viśeṣataḥ
pramehakṛmikuṣṭhārśomedodoṣavivarjitaḥ
piṣṭasvedanam arujaiḥ pūrṇaṃ bhallātakair vijarjaritaiḥ
bhūminikhāte kumbhe pratiṣṭhitaṃ kṛṣṇamṛlliptam
parivāritaṃ samantāt pacet tato gomayāgninā mṛdunā
tatsvaraso yaś cyavate gṛhṇīyāt taṃ dine 'nyasmin
amum upayujya svarasaṃ madhvaṣṭamabhāgikaṃ dviguṇasarpiḥ
pūrvavidhiyantritātmā prāpnoti guṇān sa tān eva
puṣṭāni pākena paricyutāni bhallātakāny āḍhakasaṃmitāni
ghṛṣṭveṣṭikācūrṇakaṇair jalena prakṣālya saṃśoṣya ca mārutena
jarjarāṇi vipacej jalakumbhe pādaśeṣaghṛtagālitaśītam
tadrasaṃ punar api śrapayeta kṣīrakumbhasahitaṃ caraṇasthe
sarpiḥ pakvaṃ tatra tulyapramāṇaṃ yuñjyāt svecchaṃ śarkarayā rajobhiḥ
ekībhūtaṃ tat khajakṣobhaṇena sthāpyaṃ dhānye saptarātraṃ suguptam
tam amṛtarasapākaṃ yaḥ prage prāśam aśnann anupibati yatheṣṭaṃ vāri dugdhaṃ rasaṃ vā
smṛtimatibalamedhāsattvasārair upetaḥ kanakanicayagauraḥ so 'śnute dīrgham āyuḥ
droṇe 'mbhaso vraṇakṛtāṃ triśatād vipakvāt kvāthāḍhake palasamais tilatailapātram
tiktāviṣādvayavarāgirijanmatārkṣyaiḥ siddhaṃ paraṃ nikhilakuṣṭhanibarhaṇāya
sahāmalakaśuktibhir dadhisareṇa tailena vā guḍena payasā ghṛtena yavasaktubhir vā saha
tilena saha mākṣikeṇa palalena sūpena vā vapuṣkaram aruṣkaraṃ paramamedhyam āyuṣkaram
bhallātakāni tīkṣṇāni pākīny agnisamāni ca
bhavanty amṛtakalpāni prayuktāni yathāvidhi
kaphajo na sa rogo 'sti na vibandho 'sti kaścana
yaṃ na bhallātakaṃ hanyāc chīghram agnibalapradam
vātātapavidhāne 'pi viśeṣeṇa vivarjayet
kulatthadadhiśuktāni tailābhyaṅgāgnisevanam
vṛkṣās tubarakā nāma paścimārṇavatīrajāḥ
vīcītaraṃgavikṣobhamārutoddhūtapallavāḥ
tebhyaḥ phalāny ādadīta supakvāny ambudāgame
majjñaḥ phalebhyaś cādāya śoṣayitvāvacūrṇya ca
tilavat pīḍayed droṇyāṃ kvāthayed vā kusumbhavat
tattailaṃ saṃbhṛtaṃ bhūyaḥ paced ā salilakṣayāt
avatārya karīṣe ca pakṣamātraṃ nidhāpayet
snigdhasvinno hṛtamalaḥ pakṣād uddhṛtya tat tataḥ
caturthabhaktāntaritaḥ prātaḥ pāṇitalaṃ pibet
mantreṇānena pūtasya tailasya divase śubhe
majjasāra mahāvīrya sarvān dhātūn viśodhaya
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇis tvām ājñāpayate 'cyutaḥ
tenāsyordhvam adhastāc ca doṣā yānty asakṛt tataḥ
sāyam asnehalavaṇāṃ yavāgūṃ śītalāṃ pibet
pañcāhāni pibet tailam itthaṃ varjyān vivarjayan
pakṣaṃ mudgarasānnāśī sarvakuṣṭhair vimucyate
tad eva khadirakvāthe triguṇe sādhu sādhitam
nihitaṃ pūrvavat pakṣaṃ piben māsaṃ suyantritaḥ
tenābhyaktaśarīraś ca kurvann āhāram īritam
anenāśu prayogeṇa sādhayet kuṣṭhinaṃ naram
sarpirmadhuyutaṃ pītaṃ tad eva khadirād vinā
pakṣaṃ māṃsarasāhāraṃ karoti dviśatāyuṣam
tad eva nasye pañcāśad divasān upayojitam
vapuṣmataṃ śrutadharaṃ karoti triśatāyuṣam
pañcāṣṭau sapta daśa vā pippalīr madhusarpiṣā
rasāyanaguṇānveṣī samām ekāṃ prayojayet
tisras tisras tu pūrvāhṇe bhuktvāgre bhojanasya ca
pippalyaḥ kiṃśukakṣārabhāvitā ghṛtabharjitāḥ
prayojyā madhusammiśrā rasāyanaguṇaiṣiṇā
kramavṛddhyā daśāhāni daśapaippalikaṃ dinam
vardhayet payasā sārdhaṃ tathaivāpanayet punaḥ
jīrṇauṣadhaś ca bhuñjīta ṣaṣṭikaṃ kṣīrasarpiṣā
pippalīnāṃ sahasrasya prayogo 'yaṃ rasāyanam
piṣṭās tā balibhiḥ peyāḥ śṛtā madhyabalair naraiḥ
tadvac ca chāgadugdhena dve sahasre prayojayet
ebhiḥ prayogaiḥ pippalyaḥ kāsaśvāsagalagrahān
yakṣmamehagrahaṇyarśaḥpāṇḍutvaviṣamajvarān
ghnanti śophaṃ vamiṃ hidhmāṃ plīhānaṃ vātaśoṇitam
bilvārdhamātreṇa ca pippalīnāṃ pātraṃ pralimped ayaso niśāyām
prātaḥ pibet tat salilāñjalibhyāṃ varṣaṃ yatheṣṭāśanapānaceṣṭaḥ
śuṇṭhīviḍaṅgatriphalāguḍūcī yaṣṭīharidrātibalābalāś ca
mustāsurāhvāgurucitrakāś ca saugandhikaṃ paṅkajam utpalāni
dhavāśvakarṇāsanabālapattrasārās tathā pippalivat prayojyāḥ
lohopaliptāḥ pṛthag eva jīvet samāḥ śataṃ vyādhijarāvimuktaḥ
kṣīrāñjalibhyāṃ ca rasāyanāni yuktāny amūny āyasalepanāni
kurvanti pūrvoktaguṇaprakarṣam āyuḥprakarṣaṃ dviguṇaṃ tataś ca
asanakhadirayūṣair bhāvitāṃ somarājīṃ madhughṛtaśikhipathyālohacūrṇair upetām
śaradam avalihānaḥ pāriṇāmān vikārāṃs tyajati mitahitāśī tadvad āhārajātān
tīvreṇa kuṣṭhena parītamūrtir yaḥ somarājīṃ niyamena khādet
saṃvatsaraṃ kṛṣṇatiladvitīyāṃ sa somarājīṃ vapuṣātiśete
ye somarājyā vituṣīkṛtāyāś cūrṇair upetāt payasaḥ sujātāt
uddhṛtya sāraṃ madhunā lihanti takraṃ tad evānupibanti cānte
kuṣṭhinaḥ śīryamāṇāṅgās te jātāṅgulināsikāḥ
bhānti vṛkṣā iva punaḥ prarūḍhanavapallavāḥ
rāhor amṛtacauryeṇa lūnād ye patitā galāt
amṛtasya kaṇā bhūmau te laśunatvam āgatāḥ
dvijā nāśnanti tam ato daityadehasamudbhavam
sākṣād amṛtasambhūter grāmaṇīḥ sa rasāyanam
śīlayellaśunaṃ śīte vasante 'pi kapholbaṇaḥ
ghanodaye 'pi vātārtaḥ sadā vā grīṣmalīlayā
snigdhaśuddhatanuḥ śītamadhuropaskṛtāśayaḥ
taduttaṃsāvataṃsābhyāṃ carcitānucarājiraḥ
tasya kandān vasantānte himavacchakadeśajān
apanītatvaco rātrau timayen madirādibhiḥ
tatkalkasvarasaṃ prātaḥ śucitāntavapīḍitam
madirāyāḥ surūḍhāyās tribhāgena samanvitam
madyasyānyasya takrasya mastunaḥ kāñjikasya vā
tatkāla eva vā yuktaṃ yuktam ālocya mātrayā
tailasarpirvasāmajjakṣīramāṃsarasaiḥ pṛthak
kvāthena vā yathāvyādhi rasaṃ kevalam eva vā
pibed gaṇḍūṣamātraṃ prāk kaṇṭhanālīviśuddhaye
pratataṃ svedanaṃ cānu vedanāyāṃ praśasyate
śītāmbusekaḥ sahasā vamimūrchāyayor mukhe
śeṣaṃ pibet klamāpāye sthiratāṃ gata ojasi
vidāhaparihārāya paraṃ śītānulepanaḥ
dhārayet sāmbukaṇikā muktākarpūramālikāḥ
kuḍavo 'sya parā mātrā tadardhaṃ kevalasya tu
palaṃ piṣṭasya tanmajjñaḥ sabhaktaṃ prāk ca śīlayet
jīrṇaśālyodanaṃ jīrṇe śaṅkhakundendupāṇḍuram
bhuñjīta yūṣair payasā rasair vā dhanvacāriṇām
madyam ekaṃ pibet tatra tṛṭprabandhe jalānvitam
amadyapas tvāranālaṃ phalāmbu parisikthakām
tatkalkaṃ vā samaghṛtaṃ ghṛtapātre khajāhatam
sthitaṃ daśāhād aśnīyāt tadvad vā vasayā samam
vikañcukaprājyarasonagarbhān saśūlyamāṃsān vividhopadaṃśān
nimardakān vā ghṛtaśuktayuktān prakāmam adyāllaghu tuccham aśnan
pittaraktavinirmuktasamastāvaraṇāvṛte
śuddhe vā vidyate vāyau na dravyaṃ laśunāt param
priyāmbuguḍadugdhasya māṃsamadyāmlavidviṣaḥ
atitikṣor ajīrṇaṃ ca laśuno vyāpade dhruvam
pittakopabhayād ante yuñjyān mṛdu virecanam
rasāyanaguṇān evaṃ paripūrṇān samaśnute
grīṣme 'rkataptā girayo jatutulyaṃ vamanti yat
hemādiṣaḍdhāturasaṃ procyate tacchilājatu
sarvaṃ ca tiktakaṭukaṃ nātyuṣṇaṃ kaṭu pākataḥ
chedanaṃ ca viśeṣeṇa lauhaṃ tatra praśasyate
gomūtragandhi kṛṣṇaṃ guggulvābhaṃ viśarkaraṃ mṛtsnam
snigdham anamlakaṣāyaṃ mṛdu guru ca śilājatu śreṣṭham
vyādhivyādhitasātmyaṃ samanusmaran bhāvayed ayaḥpātre
prāk kevalajaladhautaṃ śuṣkaṃ kvāthais tato bhāvyam
samagirijam aṣṭaguṇite niṣkvāthyaṃ bhāvanauṣadhaṃ toye
tanniryūhe 'ṣṭāṃśe pūtoṣṇe prakṣiped girijam
tat samarasatāṃ yātaṃ saṃśuṣkaṃ prakṣiped rase bhūyaḥ
svaiḥ svair evaṃ kvāthair bhāvyaṃ vārān bhavet sapta
atha snigdhasya śuddhasya ghṛtaṃ tiktakasādhitam
tryahaṃ yuñjīta girijam ekaikena tathā tryaham
phalatrayasya yūṣeṇa paṭolyā madhukasya ca
yogaṃ yogyaṃ tatas tasya kālāpekṣaṃ prayojayet
śilājam evaṃ dehasya bhavatyatyupakārakam
guṇān samagrān kurute sahasā vyāpadaṃ na ca
ekatrisaptasaptāhaṃ karṣam ardhapalaṃ palam
hīnamadhyottamo yogaḥ śilājasya kramān mataḥ
saṃskṛtaṃ saṃskṛte dehe prayuktaṃ girijāhvayam
yuktaṃ vyastaiḥ samastair vā tāmrāyorūpyahemabhiḥ
kṣīreṇāloḍitaṃ kuryācchīghraṃ rāsāyanaṃ phalam
kulatthān kākamācīṃ ca kapotāṃśca sadā tyajet
na so 'sti rogo bhuvi sādhyarūpo jatvaśmajaṃ yaṃ na jayet prasahya
tatkālayogair vidhivat prayuktaṃ svasthasya corjāṃ vipulāṃ dadhāti
kuṭīpraveśaḥ kṣaṇināṃ paricchadavatāṃ hitaḥ
ato 'nyathā tu ye teṣāṃ sauryamārutiko vidhiḥ
vātātapasahā yogā vakṣyante 'to viśeṣataḥ
sukhopacārā bhraṃśe 'pi ye na dehasya bādhakāḥ
śītodakaṃ payaḥ kṣaudraṃ ghṛtam ekaikaśo dviśaḥ
triśaḥ samastam athavā prāk pītaṃ sthāpayed vayaḥ
guḍena madhunā śuṇṭhyā kṛṣṇayā lavaṇena vā
dve dve khādan sadā pathye jīved varṣaśataṃ sukhī
harītakīṃ sarpiṣi sampratāpya samaśnatas tat pibato ghṛtaṃ ca
bhaveccirasthāyi balaṃ śarīre sakṛt kṛtaṃ sādhu yathā kṛtajñe
dhātrīrasakṣaudrasitāghṛtāni hitāśanānāṃ lihatāṃ narāṇām
praṇāśam āyānti jarāvikārā granthā viśālā iva durgṛhītāḥ
dhātrīkṛmighnāsanasāracūrṇaṃ satailasarpirmadhulohareṇu
niṣevamāṇasya bhaven narasya tāruṇyalāvaṇyam avipraṇaṣṭam
lauhaṃ rajo vellabhavaṃ ca sarpiḥkṣaudradrutaṃ sthāpitam abdamātram
samudgake bījakasārakﾱpte lihan balī jīvati kṛṣṇakeśaḥ
viḍaṅgabhallātakanāgarāṇi ye 'śnanti sarpirmadhusaṃyutāni
jarānadīṃ rogataraṃgiṇīṃ te lāvaṇyayuktāḥ puruṣās taranti
khadirāsanayūṣabhāvitāyās triphalāyā ghṛtamākṣikaplutāyāḥ
niyamena narā niṣevitāro yadi jīvantyarujaḥ kim atra citram
bījakasya rasam aṅgulihāryaṃ śarkarāṃ madhu ghṛtaṃ triphalāṃ ca
śīlayatsu puruṣeṣu jarattā svāgatāpi vinivartata eva
punarnavasyārdhapalaṃ navasya piṣṭaṃ pibed yaḥ payasārdhamāsam
māsadvayaṃ tattriguṇaṃ samāṃ vā jīrṇo 'pi bhūyaḥ sa punarnavaḥ syāt
mūrvābṛhatyaṃśumatībalānām uśīrapāṭhāsanasārivāṇām
kālānusāryāgurucandanānāṃ vadanti paunarnavam eva kalpam
śatāvarīkalkakaṣāyasiddhaṃ ye sarpir aśnanti sitādvitīyam
tāñjīvitādhvānam abhiprapannān na vipralumpanti vikāracaurāḥ
pītāśvagandhā payasārdhamāsaṃ ghṛtena tailena sukhāmbunā vā
kṛśasya puṣṭiṃ vapuṣo vidhatte bālasya sasyasya yathā suvṛṣṭiḥ
dine dine kṛṣṇatilaprakuñcaṃ samaśnatāṃ śītajalānupānam
poṣaḥ śarīrasya bhavatyanalpo dṛḍhībhavanty ā maraṇācca dantāḥ
cūrṇaṃ śvadaṃṣṭrāmalakāmṛtānāṃ lihan sasarpir madhubhāgamiśram
vṛṣaḥ sthiraḥ śāntavikāraduḥkhaḥ samāḥ śataṃ jīvati kṛṣṇakeśaḥ
sārdhaṃ tilair āmalakāni kṛṣṇair akṣāṇi saṃkṣudya harītakīr vā
ye 'dyur mayūrā iva te manuṣyā ramyaṃ parīṇāmam avāpnuvanti
śilājatukṣaudraviḍaṅgasarpirlohābhayāpāradatāpyabhakṣaḥ
āpūryate durbaladehadhātus tripañcarātreṇa yathā śaśāṅkaḥ
ye māsam ekaṃ svarasaṃ pibanti dine dine bhṛṅgarajaḥsamuttham
kṣīrāśinas te balavīryayuktāḥ samāḥ śataṃ jīvitam āpnuvanti
māsaṃ vacām apyupasevamānāḥ kṣīreṇa tailena ghṛtena vāpi
bhavanti rakṣobhir adhṛṣyarūpā medhāvino nirmalamṛṣṭavākyāḥ
maṇḍūkaparṇīm api bhakṣayanto bhṛṣṭāṃ ghṛte māsam anannabhakṣāḥ
jīvanti kālaṃ vipulaṃ pragalbhās tāruṇyalāvaṇyaguṇodayasthāḥ
lāṅgalītriphalālohapalapañcāśatā kṛtam
mārkavasvarase ṣaṣṭyā guṭikānāṃ śatatrayam
chāyāviśuṣkaṃ guṭikārdham adyāt pūrvaṃ samastām api tāṃ krameṇa
bhajed viriktaḥ kramaśaśca maṇḍaṃ peyāṃ vilepīṃ rasakaudanaṃ ca
sarpiḥsnigdhaṃ māsam ekaṃ yatātmā māsād ūrdhvaṃ sarvathā svairavṛttiḥ
varjyaṃ yatnāt sarvakālaṃ tvajīrṇaṃ varṣeṇaivaṃ yogam evopayuñjyāt
bhavati vigatarogo yo 'pyasādhyāmayārtaḥ prabalapuruṣakāraḥ śobhate yo 'pi vṛddhaḥ
upacitapṛthugātraśrotranetrādiyuktas taruṇa iva samānāṃ pañca jīvecchatāni
gāyatrīśikhiśiṃśipāsanaśivāvellākṣakāruṣkarān
piṣṭvāṣṭādaśasaṃguṇe 'mbhasi dhṛtān khaṇḍaiḥ sahāyomayaiḥ
pātre lohamaye tryahaṃ ravikarair āloḍayan pācayet
agnau cānu mṛdau salohaśakalaṃ pādasthitaṃ tat pacet
pūtasyāṃśaḥ kṣīrato 'ṃśastathāṃśau bhārgān niryāsād dvau varāyās trayo 'ṃśāḥ
aṃśāś catvāraś ceha haiyaṃgavīnād ekīkṛtyaitat sādhayet kṛṣṇalauhe
vimalakhaṇḍasitāmadhubhiḥ pṛthag yutam ayuktam idaṃ yadi vā ghṛtam
svarucibhojanapānaviceṣṭito bhavati nā palaśaḥ pariśīlayan
śrīmān nirdhūtapāpmā vanamahiṣabalo vājivegaḥ sthirāṅgaḥ
keśair bhṛṅgāṅganīlair madhusurabhimukho naikayoṣinniṣevī
vāṅmedhādhīsamṛddhaḥ supaṭuhutavaho māsamātropayogāt
dhatte 'sau nārasiṃhaṃ vapur analaśikhātaptacāmīkarābham
attāraṃ nārasiṃhasya vyādhayo na spṛśantyapi
cakrojjvalabhujaṃ bhītā nārasiṃham ivāsurāḥ
bhṛṅgapravālān amunaiva bhṛṣṭān ghṛtena yaḥ khādati yantritātmā
viśuddhakoṣṭho 'sanasārasiddhadugdhānupas tatkṛtabhojanārthaḥ
māsopayogāt sa sukhī jīvatyabdaśatatrayam
gṛhṇāti sakṛd apyuktam aviluptasmṛtīndriyaḥ
anenaiva ca kalpena yas tailam upayojayet
tān evāpnoti sa guṇān kṛṣṇakeśaś ca jāyate
uktāni śakyāni phalānvitāni yugānurūpāṇi rasāyanāni
mahānuśaṃsānyapi cāparāṇi prāptyādikaṣṭāni na kīrtitāni
rasāyanavidhibhraṃśājjāyeran vyādhayo yadi
yathāsvam auṣadhaṃ teṣāṃ kāryaṃ muktvā rasāyanam
satyavādinam akrodham adhyātmapravaṇendriyam
śāntaṃ sadvṛttanirataṃ vidyān nityarasāyanam
guṇair ebhiḥ samuditaḥ sevate yo rasāyanam
sa nivṛttātmā dīrghāyuḥ paratreha ca modate
śāstrānusāriṇī caryā cittajñāḥ pārśvavartinaḥ
buddhir askhalitārtheṣu paripūrṇaṃ rasāyanam
athāto vājīkaraṇavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāhur ātreyādayo maharṣayaḥ
vājīkaraṇam anvicchet satataṃ viṣayī pumān
tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭirapatyaṃ ca guṇavat tatra saṃśritam
apatyasaṃtānakaraṃ yat sadyaḥ saṃpraharṣaṇam
vājīvātibalo yena yātyapratihato 'ṅganāḥ
bhavatyatipriyaḥ strīṇāṃ yena yenopacīyate
tad vājīkaraṇaṃ taddhi dehasyorjaskaraṃ param
dharmyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ lokadvayarasāyanam
anumodāmahe brahmacaryam ekāntanirmalam
alpasattvasya tu kleśair bādhyamānasya rāgiṇaḥ
śarīrakṣayarakṣārthaṃ vājīkaraṇam ucyate
kalyasyodagravayaso vājīkaraṇasevinaḥ
sarveṣvṛtuṣvaharahar vyavāyo na nivāryate
atha snigdhaviśuddhānāṃ nirūhān sānuvāsanān
ghṛtatailarasakṣīraśarkarākṣaudrasaṃyutān
yogavid yojayet pūrvaṃ kṣīramāṃsarasāśinām
tato vājīkarān yogān śukrāpatyabalapradān
acchāyaḥ pūtikusumaḥ phalena rahito drumaḥ
yathaikaścaikaśākhaśca nirapatyastathā naraḥ
skhaladgamanam avyaktavacanaṃ dhūlidhūsaram
api lālāvilamukhaṃ hṛdayāhlādakārakam
apatyaṃ tulyatāṃ kena darśanasparśanādiṣu
kiṃ punar yad yaśodharmamānaśrīkulavardhanam
śuddhakāye yathāśakti vṛṣyayogān prayojayet
śarekṣukuśakāśānāṃ vidāryā vīraṇasya ca
mūlāni kaṇṭakāryāśca jīvakarṣabhakau balām
mede dve dve ca kākolyau śūrpaparṇyau śatāvarīm
aśvagandhām atibalāṃ ātmaguptāṃ punarnavām
vīrāṃ payasyāṃ jīvantīm ṛddhiṃ rāsnāṃ trikaṇṭakam
madhukaṃ śāliparṇīṃ ca bhāgāṃstripalikān pṛthak
māṣāṇām āḍhakaṃ caitad dvidroṇe sādhayed apām
rasenāḍhakaśeṣeṇa pacet tena ghṛtāḍhakam
dattvā vidārīdhātrīkṣurasānām āḍhakāḍhakam
ghṛtāccaturguṇaṃ kṣīraṃ peṣyāṇīmāni cāvapet
vīrāṃ svaguptāṃ kākolyau yaṣṭīṃ phalgūni pippalīm
drākṣāṃ vidārīṃ kharjūraṃ madhukāni śatāvarīm
tat siddhapūtaṃ cūrṇasya pṛthak prasthena yojayet
śarkarāyāstugāyāśca pippalyāḥ kuḍavena ca
maricasya prakuñcena pṛthag ardhapalonmitaiḥ
tvagelākesaraiḥ ślakṣṇaiḥ kṣaudradvikuḍavena ca
palamātraṃ tataḥ khādet pratyahaṃ rasadugdhabhuk
tenārohati vājīva kuliṅga iva hṛṣyati
vidārīpippalīśālipriyālekṣurakād rajaḥ
pṛthak svaguptāmūlācca kuḍavāṃśaṃ tathā madhu
tulārdhaṃ śarkarācūrṇāt prasthārdhaṃ navasarpiṣaḥ
so 'kṣamātram ataḥ khādet yasya rāmāśataṃ gṛhe
sātmaguptāphalān kṣīre godhūmān sādhitān himān
māṣān vā saghṛtakṣaudrān khādan gṛṣṭipayo'nupaḥ
jāgarti rātriṃ sakalām akhinnaḥ khedayan striyaḥ
bastāṇḍasiddhe payasi bhāvitān asakṛt tilān
yaḥ khādet sasitān gacchet sa strīśatam apūrvavat
cūrṇaṃ vidāryā bahuśaḥ svarasenaiva bhāvitam
kṣaudrasarpiryutaṃ līḍhvā pramadāśatam ṛcchati
kṛṣṇādhātrīphalarajaḥ svarasena subhāvitam
śarkarāmadhusarpirbhir līḍhvā yo 'nu payaḥ pibet
sa naro 'śītivarṣo 'pi yuveva parihṛṣyati
karṣaṃ madhukacūrṇasya ghṛtakṣaudrasamanvitam
payo'nupānaṃ yo lihyān nityavegaḥ sa nā bhavet
kulīraśṛṅgyā yaḥ kalkam āloḍya payasā pibet
sitāghṛtapayo'nnāśī sa nārīṣu vṛṣāyate
yaḥ payasyāṃ payaḥsiddhāṃ khāden madhughṛtānvitām
pibed bāṣkayaṇaṃ cānu kṣīraṃ na kṣayam eti saḥ
svayaṅguptekṣurakayor bījacūrṇaṃ saśarkaram
dhāroṣṇena naraḥ pītvā payasā rāsabhāyate
uccaṭācūrṇam apyevaṃ śatāvaryāśca yojayet
candraśubhraṃ dadhisaraṃ sasitāṣaṣṭikaudanam
paṭe sumārjitaṃ bhuktvā vṛddho 'pi taruṇāyate
śvadaṃṣṭrekṣuramāṣātmaguptābījaśatāvarīḥ
piban kṣīreṇa jīrṇo 'pi gacchati pramadāśatam
yat kiṃcin madhuraṃ snigdhaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ balavardhanam
manaso harṣaṇaṃ yacca tat sarvaṃ vṛṣyam ucyate
dravyairevaṃvidhaistasmād darpitaḥ pramadāṃ vrajet
ātmavegena codīrṇaḥ strīguṇaiśca praharṣitaḥ
sevyāḥ sarvendriyasukhā dharmakalpadrumāṅkurāḥ
viṣayātiśayāḥ pañca śarāḥ kusumadhanvanaḥ
iṣṭā hyekaikaśo 'pyarthā harṣaprītikarāḥ param
kiṃ punaḥ strīśarīre ye saṃghātena pratiṣṭhitāḥ
nāmāpi yasyā hṛdayotsavāya yāṃ paśyatāṃ tṛptiranāptapūrvā
sarvendriyākarṣaṇapāśabhūtā kāntānuvṛttivratadīkṣitā yā
kalāvilāsāṅgavayovibhūṣā śuciḥ salajjā rahasi pragalbhā
priyaṃvadā tulyamanaḥśayā yā sā strī vṛṣyatvāya paraṃ narasya
ācarecca sakalāṃ raticaryāṃ kāmasūtravihitām anavadyām
deśakālabalaśaktyanurodhād vaidyatantrasamayoktyaviruddhām
abhyañjanodvartanasekagandhasrakcitravastrābharaṇaprakārāḥ
gāndharvakāvyādikathāpravīṇāḥ samasvabhāvā vaśagā vayasyāḥ
dīrghikā svabhavanāntaniviṣṭā padmareṇumadhumattavihaṅgā
nīlasānugirikūṭanitambe kānanāni purakaṇṭhagatāni
dṛṣṭisukhā vividhā tarujātiḥ śrotrasukhaḥ kalakokilanādaḥ
aṅgasukhartuvaśena vibhūṣā cittasukhaḥ sakalaḥ parivāraḥ
tāmbūlam acchamadirā kāntā kāntā niśā śaśāṅkāṅkā
yad yacca kiṃcid iṣṭaṃ manaso vājīkaraṃ tat tat
madhu mukham iva sotpalaṃ priyāyāḥ kalaraṇanā parivādinī priyeva
kusumacayamanoramā ca śayyā kisalayinī latikeva puṣpitāgrā
deśe śarīre ca na kācid artirartheṣu nālpo 'pi manovidhānaḥ
vājīkarāḥ saṃnihitāśca yogāḥ kāmasya kāmaṃ paripūrayanti
mustā parpaṭakaṃ jvare tṛṣi jalaṃ mṛdbhṛṣṭaloṣṭodbhavaṃ lājāśchardiṣu vastijeṣu girijaṃ meheṣu dhātrīniśe
pāṇḍau śreṣṭham ayo 'bhayānilakaphe plīhāmaye pippalī saṃdhāne kṛmijā viṣe śukatarur medo'nile gugguluḥ
vṛṣo 'srapitte kuṭajo 'tisāre bhallātako 'rśaḥsu gareṣu hema
sthūleṣu tārkṣyaṃ kṛmiṣu kṛmighnaṃ śoṣe surā chāgapayo 'tha māṃsam
akṣyāmayeṣu triphalā guḍūcī vātāsraroge mathitaṃ grahaṇyām
kuṣṭheṣu sevyaḥ khadirasya sāraḥ sarveṣu rogeṣu śilāhvayaṃ ca
unmādaṃ ghṛtam anavaṃ śokaṃ madyaṃ vyapasmṛtiṃ brāhmī
nidrānāśaṃ kṣīraṃ jayati rasālā pratiśyāyam
māṃsaṃ kārśyaṃ laśunaḥ prabhañjanaṃ stabdhagātratāṃ svedaḥ
guḍamañjaryāḥ khapuro nasyāt skandhāṃsabāhurujam
navanītakhaṇḍamarditam auṣṭraṃ mūtraṃ payaśca hantyudaram
nasyaṃ mūrdhavikārān vidradhim acirotthitam asravisrāvaḥ
nasyaṃ kavaḍo mukhajān nasyāñjanatarpaṇāni netrarujaḥ
vṛddhasya kṣīraghṛte mūrchāṃ śītāmbumārutacchāyāḥ
samaśuktārdrakamātrā mande vahnau śrame surā snānam
duḥkhasahatve sthairye vyāyāmo gokṣurur hitaḥ kṛcchre
kāse nidigdhikā pārśvaśūle puṣkarajā jaṭā
vayasaḥ sthāpane dhātrī triphalā guggulur vraṇe
vastir vātavikārān paittān rekaḥ kaphodbhavān vamanam
kṣaudraṃ jayati balāsaṃ sarpiḥ pittaṃ samīraṇaṃ tailam
ityagryaṃ yat proktaṃ rogāṇām auṣadhaṃ śamāyālam
tad deśakālabalato vikalpanīyaṃ yathāyogam
ityātreyād āgamayyārthasūtraṃ tatsūktānāṃ peśalānām atṛptaḥ
bheḍādīnāṃ saṃmato bhaktinamraḥ papracchedaṃ saṃśayāno 'gniveśaḥ
dṛśyante bhagavan kecid ātmavanto 'pi rogiṇaḥ
dravyopasthātṛsampannā vṛddhavaidyamatānugāḥ
kṣīyamāṇāmayaprāṇā viparītāstathāpare
hitāhitavibhāgasya phalaṃ tasmād aniścitam
kiṃ śāsti śāstram asmin iti kalpayato 'gniveśamukhyasya
śiṣyagaṇasya punarvasurācakhyau kārtsnyatastattvam
na cikitsācikitsā ca tulyā bhavitum arhati
vināpi kriyayā svāsthyaṃ gacchatāṃ ṣoḍaśāṃśayā
ātaṅkapaṅkamagnānāṃ hastālambo bhiṣagjitam
jīvitaṃ mriyamāṇānāṃ sarveṣām eva nauṣadhāt
na hyupāyam apekṣante sarve rogā na cānyathā
upāyasādhyāḥ sidhyanti nāhetur hetumān yataḥ
yad uktaṃ sarvasaṃpattiyuktayāpi cikitsayā
mṛtyur bhavati tan naivaṃ nopāye 'styanupāyatā
api copāyayuktasya dhīmato jātucit kriyā
na sidhyed daivavaiguṇyān na tviyaṃ ṣoḍaśātmikā
kasyāsiddho 'gnitoyādiḥ svedastambhādikarmaṇi
na prīṇanaṃ karṣaṇaṃ vā kasya kṣīraṃ gavedhukam
kasya māṣātmaguptādau vṛṣyatve nāsti niścayaḥ
viṇmūtrakaraṇākṣepau kasya saṃśayitau yave
viṣaṃ kasya jarāṃ yāti mantratantravivarjitam
kaḥ prāptaḥ kalyatāṃ pathyād ṛte rohiṇikādiṣu
api cākālamaraṇaṃ sarvasiddhāntaniścitam
mahatāpi prayatnena vāryatāṃ katham anyathā
candanādyapi dāhādau rūḍham āgamapūrvakam
śāstrād eva gataṃ siddhiṃ jvare laṅghanabṛṃhaṇam
catuṣpādguṇasampanne samyag ālocya yojite
mā kṛthā vyādhinirghātaṃ vicikitsāṃ cikitsite
etaddhi mṛtyupāśānām akāṇḍe chedanaṃ dṛḍham
rogottrāsitabhītānāṃ rakṣāsūtram asūtrakam
etat tad amṛtaṃ sākṣājjagadāyāsavarjitam
yāti hālāhalatvaṃ tu sadyo durbhājanasthitam
ajñātaśāstrasadbhāvāñchāstramātraparāyaṇān
tyajed dūrād bhiṣakpāśān pāśān vaivasvatān iva
bhiṣajāṃ sādhuvṛttānāṃ bhadram āgamaśālinām
abhyastakarmaṇāṃ bhadraṃ bhadraṃ bhadrābhilāṣiṇām
iti tantraguṇair yuktaṃ tantradoṣair vivarjitam
cikitsāśāstram akhilaṃ vyāpya yat paritaḥ sthitam
vipulāmalavijñānamahāmunimatānugam
mahāsāgaragambhīrasaṃgrahārthopalakṣaṇam
aṣṭāṅgavaidyakamahodadhimanthanena yo 'ṣṭāṅgasaṃgrahamahāmṛtarāśirāptaḥ
tasmād analpaphalam alpasamudyamānāṃ prītyartham etad uditaṃ pṛthag eva tantram
idam āgamasiddhatvāt pratyakṣaphaladarśanāt
mantravat samprayoktavyaṃ na mīmāṃsyaṃ kathañcana
dīrghajīvitam ārogyaṃ dharmam arthaṃ sukhaṃ yaśaḥ
pāṭhāvabodhānuṣṭhānairadhigacchatyato dhruvam
etat paṭhan saṃgrahabodhaśaktaḥ svabhyastakarmā bhiṣag aprakampyaḥ
ākampayatyanyaviśālatantrakṛtābhiyogān yadi tan na citram
yadi carakam adhīte taddhruvaṃ suśrutādipraṇigaditagadānāṃ nāmamātre 'pi bāhyaḥ
atha carakavihīnaḥ prakriyāyām aklinnaḥ kim iva khalu karotu vyādhitānāṃ varākaḥ
abhiniveśavaśād abhiyujyate subhaṇite 'pi na yo dṛḍhamūḍhakaḥ
paṭhatu yatnaparaḥ puruṣāyuṣaṃ sa khalu vaidyakam ādyam anirvidaḥ
vāte pitte śleṣmaśāntau ca pathyaṃ tailaṃ sarpir mākṣikaṃ ca krameṇa
etad brahmā bhāṣatāṃ brahmajo vā kā nirmantre vaktṛbhedoktiśaktiḥ
abhidhātṛvaśāt kiṃ vā dravyaśaktir viśiṣyate
ato matsaram utsṛjya mādhyasthyam avalambyatām
ṛṣipraṇīte prītiścen muktvā carakasuśrutau
bheḍādyāḥ kiṃ na paṭhyante tasmād grāhyaṃ subhāṣitam
hṛdayam iva hṛdayam etat sarvāyurvedavāṅmayapayodheḥ
kṛtvā yacchubham āptaṃ śubham astu paraṃ tato jagataḥ
